### [1] [Comment on "Quantum phase transitions of Dirac particles in a magnetized rotating curved background: Interplay of geometry, magnetization, and thermodynamics"](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03319)
*R. R. S. Oliveira*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We derive the complete energy spectra for Dirac particles in polar coordinates as studied by Sahan et al., correcting errors in their analysis by properly accounting for both radial ($n$) and angular ($m$) quantum numbers. Our results show that the energy spectra must depend on both $n$ and $m$, consistent with established treatments of the Dirac equation in (2+1)-dimensional curved spacetimes.

我们推导了Sahan等人研究的极坐标下狄拉克粒子的完整能谱，通过正确引入径向($n$)和角向($m$)量子数修正了其分析中的错误。结果表明，能谱必须同时依赖于$n$和$m$，这与(2+1)维弯曲时空下狄拉克方程的标准处理一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the observation that quantized energy spectra of Dirac particles in curved or flat spacetime in polar coordinates generally depend on two quantum numbers: the radial quantum number $n \geq 0$ and the angular quantum number $m \neq 0$. However, Sahan et al. reported spectra depending on only one quantum number despite using polar coordinates and the Dirac equation. This inconsistency prompted a re-examination of their derivation.

动机源于一个观察：在极坐标下，弯曲或平坦时空中狄拉克粒子的量子化能谱通常依赖两个量子数——径向量子数 $n \geq 0$ 和角向量子数 $m \neq 0$。然而，Sahan等人尽管使用了极坐标和狄拉克方程，却只报告了一个量子数的能谱。这种不一致性促使我们重新审视他们的推导过程。

Method: We revisited the Dirac equation in (2+1)-dimensional spacetime in polar coordinates, employing standard definitions of Dirac gamma matrices $\gamma^\mu$ and spin connections. By carefully separating variables and constructing the correct second-order differential equation, we identified and corrected minor errors in the original work. The resulting equation was solved to obtain energy eigenvalues explicitly dependent on both $n$ and $m$.

我们重新考察了(2+1)维极坐标下的狄拉克方程，采用标准的狄拉克伽马矩阵$\gamma^\mu$和自旋联络定义。通过仔细分离变量并构造正确的二阶微分方程，识别并修正了原始工作中的小错误。求解所得方程得到了明确依赖于$n$和$m$的能级。

Result: We obtained the correct second-order differential equation and derived the complete energy spectra $E_{n,m}$ that explicitly depend on both the radial quantum number $n$ and the angular quantum number $m$. For the special case $m < 0$ and $s = -1$, our result recovers the spectrum of Sahan et al. [1] up to a sign error in one term, confirming that their result was a partial case arising from an incomplete treatment.

我们获得了正确的二阶微分方程，并推导出完整能谱$E_{n,m}$，其显式依赖于径向量子数$n$和角向量子数$m$。在特例$m < 0$且$s = -1$下，我们的结果除了一项符号错误外重现了Sahan等人的能谱，证实其结果是由于处理不完整而得到的部分情况。

Conclusion: The energy spectra of Dirac particles in polar coordinates must depend on both $n$ and $m$. The single-quantum-number dependence in Sahan et al. [1] arose from an incomplete separation procedure and incorrect reduction to a second-order equation. Our corrected analysis establishes the full spectral structure consistent with fundamental principles of relativistic quantum mechanics in curved spacetime.

极坐标下狄拉克粒子的能谱必须同时依赖于$n$和$m$。Sahan等人[1]中单量子数依赖性源于不完整的分离过程和错误的二阶方程约化。我们修正后的分析确立了符合弯曲时空中相对论量子力学基本原理的完整谱结构。

Abstract: In this comment, we obtain the complete energy spectra for the paper by Sahan et al. [1], that is, the energy spectra dependent on two quantum numbers, namely, the radial quantum number (given by $n\geq 0$) and the angular quantum number (given by $m\neq 0$). In particular, what motivated us to carry out such a study was the fact that the quantized energy spectra for Dirac particles in a curved or flat spacetime in polar coordinates explicitly depend on two quantum numbers. From this, the following question arose: Why do the energy spectra in the paper by Sahan et al. [1] depends on only one quantum number and not two, given that they worked with the Dirac equation in polar coordinates? So, using several important papers in the literature on the Dirac equation in curved spacetimes, as well as the most commonly used definition for Dirac gamma matrices in (2+1)-dimensions, we corrected some minor errors in the paper by Sahan et al. [1]. Consequently, we obtain the true second-order differential equation for their problem, as well as the complete energy spectra, which explicitly depend on both $n$ and $m$. Finally, we note that for $m<0$ (negative angular momentum) with $s=-1$ (lower component of the Dirac spinor), we obtain (except for one term with the incorrect sign) the particular energy spectra of Sahan et al. [1].

</details>


### [2] [Analysis of Charged Compact Stars with Bardeen Black Hole in $f(\mathfrak{Q}, \mathcal{T})$ Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03332)
*M. Sharif,Iqra Ibrar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper studies charged compact stars in the $f(\mathfrak{Q}, \mathcal{T})$ gravity framework using Bardeen's model for exterior spacetime and Finch-Skea metric for interior structure, demonstrating physically viable and stable configurations through comprehensive analysis of energy conditions, TOV equilibrium, and stability criteria.

本文在$f(\mathfrak{Q}, \mathcal{T})$引力框架下研究带电致密星，采用Bardeen模型描述外部时空，Finch-Skea度规描述内部结构，通过能量条件、TOV平衡和稳定性准则的全面分析，证明了该模型下的解具有物理合理性和稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore alternative gravitational theories beyond general relativity, particularly $f(\mathfrak{Q}, \mathcal{T})$ gravity, which incorporates non-metricity ($\mathfrak{Q}$) and the trace of the energy-momentum tensor ($\mathcal{T}$), to better understand compact stellar objects and their behavior under extreme conditions, especially in the context of cosmic acceleration and modified gravity.

研究动机是探索超越广义相对论的替代引力理论，特别是包含非度量性（$\mathfrak{Q}$）和能量-动量张量迹（$\mathcal{T}$）的$f(\mathfrak{Q}, \mathcal{T})$引力，以更好地理解在极端条件下致密星体的行为，尤其是在宇宙加速膨胀和修改引力背景下的表现。

Method: The method involves constructing a spherically symmetric model of charged compact stars in $f(\mathfrak{Q}, \mathcal{T})$ gravity. The exterior spacetime is described by Bardeen's solution (interpreted here as a regular black hole or mimicker of compact object geometry), while the interior is modeled using the Finch-Skea metric potential. Field equations are solved under these assumptions, and physical observables—such as energy density $\rho$, radial and tangential pressures $p_r$, $p_t$, anisotropy $\Delta$, equation of state parameters, and electromagnetic field contributions—are derived. Graphical analysis is employed to examine energy conditions, TOV equation for hydrostatic equilibrium, mass-radius relation, compactness $u = M/R$, surface redshift $z_s$, causality condition ($0 < dv/d\rho \leq 1$), and adiabatic index $\Gamma > 4/3$.

方法上，在$f(\mathfrak{Q}, \mathcal{T})$引力中构建球对称带电致密星模型，外部时空采用Bardeen解（作为正则黑洞或致密天体几何的模拟），内部使用Finch-Skea度规势。求解相应的场方程，并导出能量密度$\rho$、径向与横向压力$p_r$、$p_t$、各向异性$\Delta$、状态方程参数及电磁场贡献等可观测量。通过图像分析检验能量条件、TOV平衡方程、质量-半径关系、致密性$u = M/R$、表面红移$z_s$、因果律条件（$0 < dv/d\rho \leq 1$）以及绝热指数$\Gamma > 4/3$。

Result: The results show that the derived solutions satisfy all essential physical requirements: energy conditions (NEC, WEC, DEC) are fulfilled, the TOV equation confirms hydrostatic equilibrium, the compactness approaches values typical of neutron stars or quark stars, surface redshift remains within physically acceptable bounds, and both causality and adiabatic stability criteria are met. The inclusion of charge and $f(\mathfrak{Q}, \mathcal{T})$ corrections leads to enhanced stability and more realistic modeling of ultra-dense matter.

结果表明，所得到的解满足所有基本物理要求：能量条件（NEC, WEC, DEC）成立，TOV方程确认处于流体静力平衡，致密性接近中子星或夸克星典型值，表面红移保持在物理可接受范围内，且因果律与绝热稳定性准则均被满足。电荷与$f(\mathfrak{Q}, \mathcal{T})$修正项的引入提升了稳定性，使超密物质建模更加真实。

Conclusion: The study concludes that charged compact star solutions in the $f(\mathfrak{Q}, \mathcal{T})$ gravity framework with Bardeen exterior and Finch-Skea interior metrics are physically plausible, stable, and consistent with observational constraints, offering a viable alternative to general relativity in describing dense astrophysical systems.

研究结论认为，在$f(\mathfrak{Q}, \mathcal{T})$引力框架下结合Bardeen外部解与Finch-Skea内部度规的带电致密星解是物理上合理的、稳定的，并符合观测约束，为描述致密天体系统提供了广义相对论之外的一个可行替代方案。

Abstract: This study investigates the behavior of charged compact stars within the $f(\mathfrak{Q}, \mathcal{T})$ gravitational framework, where $\mathfrak{Q}$ denotes the non-metricity scalar and $\mathcal{T}$ represents the trace of the energy-momentum tensor. Recognized as a promising model for explaining the accelerated expansion of the universe, this approach offers a strong theoretical foundation. A central focus of this research is the application of Bardeen's model to describe the exterior spacetime. Additionally, the study examines the internal structure of compact stars using a solution based on the Finch-Skea metric potential. Various physical properties, including energy density, pressure components, anisotropy, energy conditions and equation of state parameters are analyzed through graphical representations. Equilibrium conditions are explored via the Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff equation while key characteristics such as the mass-radius relationship, compactness, surface redshift and stability criteria based on the causality condition and adiabatic index are thoroughly evaluated. The analysis concludes that the proposed solutions for charged compact stars in this framework are both theoretically consistent and physically valid.

</details>


### [3] [Friedmann cosmology with fluids and hyperfluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03343)
*Ilaria Andrei,Damianos Iosifidis,Laur Järv,Margus Saal*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We explore metric-affine FLRW cosmology where both the metric and connection are independent, and matter possesses hypermomentum including spin. A dark dust fluid with spin hypermomentum exhibits a dynamical equation of state, potentially explaining recent DESI DR2 observations.

我们研究了度量-仿射FLRW宇宙学，其中度量和联络是独立的，且物质具有包含自旋的超动量。携带自旋超动量的暗尘埃流体表现出动力学状态方程，可能解释最新的DESI DR2观测数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent cosmological data, such as from DESI DR2, challenge the standard $\Lambda$CDM model, suggesting possible deviations in the expansion history or growth of structure. This motivates exploring beyond-Riemannian geometries in which spacetime curvature and matter couplings are more general, particularly within the framework of metric-affine gravity (MAG), where the connection is independent of the metric and matter can carry hypermomentum.

近期的宇宙学数据（如DESI DR2）对标准$\Lambda$CDM模型提出了挑战，表明在膨胀历史或结构增长方面可能存在偏差。这促使我们探索超越黎曼几何的理论框架，特别是在度量-仿射引力（MAG）中，联络独立于度量，且物质可携带超动量。

Method: We impose spatial homogeneity and isotropy on both the metric and affine connection in a flat FLRW universe within the metric-affine framework. The matter content includes a 'dark dust' fluid whose energy-momentum tensor is canonical, but which carries spin hypermomentum. The latter acts as a source for the torsion and non-metricity fields. We derive the modified Friedmann equations by varying the action with respect to the metric and connection, incorporating the coupling between hypermomentum and spacetime geometry.

我们在度量-仿射框架下的平直FLRW宇宙中，对度量和仿射联络施加空间均匀性和各向同性条件。物质内容包含一种‘暗尘埃’流体，其能量-动量张量为标准形式，但携带自旋超动量。后者作为挠率和非度量性场的源。通过作用量对度量和联络的变分，推导出修正的Friedmann方程，并纳入超动量与时空几何之间的耦合。

Result: The presence of spin hypermomentum leads to an effective dynamical equation of state for the dark dust fluid, deviating from $w=0$. The evolution of torsion and/or non-metricity sourced by hypermomentum introduces new dynamical terms in the Friedmann equations, mimicking dark energy-like effects or modifying the matter-dominated era. This scenario offers a geometric origin for late-time cosmic acceleration without introducing a cosmological constant.

自旋超动量的存在导致暗尘埃流体的有效状态方程偏离$w=0$。由超动量激发的挠率或非度量性的演化引入了Friedmann方程中的新动力学项，模拟暗能量效应或修改物质主导时期。该情景为晚期宇宙加速提供了几何起源，而无需引入宇宙学常数。

Conclusion: Metric-affine FLRW cosmology with hypermomentum provides a viable alternative to $\Lambda$CDM, where the interplay between spin and spacetime geometry generates an effective dark energy component. This framework naturally accommodates dynamical dark energy behavior consistent with DESI DR2 anomalies and opens new avenues for testing quantum gravitational imprints in cosmology via spin-induced geometric effects.

带有超动量的度量-仿射FLRW宇宙学为$\Lambda$CDM提供了一个可行的替代方案，其中自旋与时空几何的相互作用产生了有效的暗能量成分。该框架自然容纳了与DESI DR2异常一致的动力学暗能量行为，并通过自旋诱导的几何效应为检验宇宙学中的量子引力印记开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We discuss flat Friedmann-Lemaitre-Robertson-Walker (FLRW) metric-affine cosmology where the metric and connection as well as the matter energy-momentum and hypermomentum all obey the symmetry of spatial homogeneity and isotropy. In particular, we outline a scenario where a dark dust fluid carries spin hypermomentum which makes its effective equation of state dynamical and might relate to the DESI DR2 data.

</details>


### [4] [On the Stability of Topologically Non-Trivial Vacuum Bubbles in a Three Form Gauge Sector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03363)
*Muhammad Ghulam Khuwajah Khan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates a three-form gauge theory coupled to spherical membranes (bubble walls) with a Dirac-Born-Infeld action and a worldvolume $U(1)$ gauge field carrying quantized monopole flux $n \in \mathbb{Z}$. The four-form field strength contributes a branch-dependent vacuum energy, and under the Hartle-Hawking-Wu selection criterion, only a specific flux window is semiclassically allowed. It is shown that the energetically favored configuration collapses to a microscopic size, but due to nonzero monopole flux, the energy remains finite, forming stable, particle-like remnant states called 'topolons'. These topolons are interpreted as dark matter candidates, with mass determined by the wall scale and conserved flux, offering a microphysical mechanism for cosmological relic formation.

本文研究了一个三形式规范场理论，该理论与具有Dirac-Born-Infeld作用量的球形膜（泡壁）耦合，并在膜上引入携带量化磁单极通量$n \in \mathbb{Z}$的世界体积$U(1)$规范场。四形式场强贡献了分支依赖的真空能量，在Hartle-Hawking-Wu选择准则下，仅特定通量窗口是半经典可允许的。研究表明，能量最优构型会坍缩至微观尺度，但由于非零磁单极通量，其能量在坍缩极限下保持有限，形成称为“拓扑子”（topolons）的稳定类粒子残余态。这些拓扑子被解释为暗物质候选者，其质量由壁尺度和守恒通量决定，为宇宙学遗存形成提供了具体的微观机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from understanding how stable, massive, particle-like states can emerge in theories with higher-form gauge fields and extended objects like membranes. The authors aim to explore whether such setups can naturally yield stable remnants through semiclassical dynamics, particularly within the framework of quantum cosmology via the Hartle-Hawking wave function. They are interested in identifying viable dark matter candidates arising from non-perturbative gravitational and gauge effects, beyond traditional WIMP paradigms.

研究动机源于理解在具有高阶形式规范场和膜等延展物体的理论中，如何产生稳定的、大质量的类粒子态。作者旨在探索此类模型是否能通过半经典动力学自然地生成稳定残余态，特别是在Hartle-Hawking波函数所描述的量子宇宙学框架内。他们希望识别出源于非微扰引力与规范效应的暗物质候选者，超越传统的WIMP范式。

Method: The method involves analyzing a three-form gauge field in four dimensions coupled to electrically charged spherical membranes governed by a Dirac--Born--Infeld (DBI) action. The four-form field strength yields no local degrees of freedom but induces a vacuum energy that depends on the branch of the solution. Using the Hartle--Hawking--Wu criterion, the authors restrict to semiclassically admissible flux values where the wave function has support. A worldvolume $U(1)$ gauge field with quantized monopole flux $n$ is introduced on the bubble wall, and the full DBI energy of spherical configurations is computed. Energy minimization is performed across branches to determine the preferred vacuum and configuration.

该方法涉及分析四维时空中一个与电荷球形膜耦合的三形式规范场，膜的动力学由Dirac-Born-Infeld (DBI) 作用量支配。四形式场强无局域自由度，但导致依赖于解分支的真空能量。利用Hartle-Hawking-Wu准则，作者将分析限制在波函数有支撑的半经典可允许通量范围内。在泡壁上引入携带量化磁单极通量$n$的世界体积$U(1)$规范场，并计算球对称构型的完整DBI能量。通过对不同分支进行能量最小化，确定最稳定的真空与构型。

Result: The analysis shows that the energetically preferred configuration corresponds to a collapse of the bubble wall to a microscopic core rather than stabilization at finite radius. However, due to the presence of nonzero quantized monopole flux $n$, the DBI energy does not vanish in this limit but approaches a finite value. This results in stable, finite-energy remnants—termed topolons—whose mass scales with the wall tension and the conserved flux. These states are distinguished from runaway vacuum decay channels within the semiclassically allowed sector. Topolons behave as heavy, localized particles at large distances and are thus viable dark matter candidates.

分析表明，能量最优构型对应泡壁坍缩至微观核心，而非在有限半径处稳定。然而，由于存在非零量化磁单极通量$n$，DBI能量在此极限下不消失，而是趋于一个有限值。这导致形成稳定的有限能量残余态——称为拓扑子（topolons），其质量与壁张力和守恒通量相关。这些态在半经典可允许区域内与逃逸型真空衰变通道区分开来。拓扑子在远距离表现为重的局域化粒子，因此是可行的暗物质候选者。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that in a three-form gauge theory with DBI-coupled spherical membranes and worldvolume monopole flux, stable particle-like remnants (topolons) arise from the interplay between vacuum energy branches and topological flux conservation. These topolons are protected from complete dissolution by the conserved $n$-flux and represent a new class of dark relics with masses set by microscopic physics. The framework provides a microphysical realization of dark matter formation within quantum cosmology, with the Hartle--Hawking--Wu criterion selecting the relevant sector. Future work will address cosmological abundance and observational signatures.

论文得出结论：在具有DBI耦合球形膜及世界体积磁单极通量的三形式规范理论中，稳定类粒子残余态（拓扑子）源于真空能量分支与拓扑通量守恒之间的相互作用。这些拓扑子因守恒的$n$通量而免于完全消散，代表一类新的暗遗存，其质量由微观物理设定。该框架在量子宇宙学背景下为暗物质形成提供了微观实现，其中Hartle-Hawking-Wu准则选择了相关物理区域。未来工作将探讨其宇宙学丰度与可观测信号。

Abstract: We study a three-form gauge sector in four spacetime dimensions coupled to electrically charged spherical membranes whose worldvolume dynamics are governed by a Dirac--Born--Infeld action. The associated four-form field strength has no local propagating degrees of freedom and contributes a branch-dependent vacuum energy. Motivated by the Hartle--Hawking--Wu selection argument, we restrict attention to the semiclassically admissible four form flux window for which the Hartle-Hawking wave function has support. We then endow the bubble wall with a worldvolume $U(1)$ gauge field carrying quantized monopole flux $n \in \mathbb{Z}$ and evaluate the full DBI energy of the resulting spherical configurations. We show that the energetically preferred branch collapses toward a microscopic core rather than stabilizing at finite radius, but for nonzero monopole flux the energy does not vanish in the collapsed limit. Instead, the bubble relaxes to a finite-energy remnant whose mass is set by the wall scale and the conserved flux. We interpret these objects as stable flux-supported particle-like states, which we call topolons. Within the admissible sector, the effective energy analysis distinguishes stable collapsed remnants from the contrasting runaway vacuum-decay channel, thereby isolating the sector relevant for cosmological relic formation. At macroscopic distances, topolons behave as heavy localized states and provide a concrete microphysical realization of a dark relic candidate. The detailed cosmological abundance and phenomenology are left for future work.

</details>


### [5] [Multimessenger Signatures of Tilted, Self-Gravitating, Black Hole Disks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03368)
*Milton Ruiz,Antonios Tsokaros,Stuart L. Shapiro*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We present fully relativistic GRMHD simulations of tilted, self-gravitating black hole-disk systems, showing that massive disks around rapidly spinning black holes develop a nonaxisymmetric instability across all tilt angles, which is modulated by magnetic stresses and MRI-driven turbulence, leading to persistent $m=1$ mode-dominated gravitational wave emission and Blandford-Znajek jet launching—supporting their role as multimessenger sources.

我们提出了对倾斜、自引力黑洞-盘系统的完全相对论性GRMHD模拟，表明在快速旋转黑洞周围的巨大盘在所有倾角下都会发展出非轴对称不稳定性，该不稳定性受磁应力和MRI驱动的湍流调制，产生由持久$m=1$模式主导的引力波辐射以及Blandford-Znajek喷流，支持其作为多信使源的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand the dynamics and multimessenger signatures (gravitational waves and jets) of misaligned black hole-disk systems with strong gravity, magnetic fields, and self-gravity—regimes where post-Newtonian or idealized MHD treatments fail.

为了理解强引力、磁场和自引力条件下倾斜黑洞-盘系统的动力学及多信使信号（引力波和喷流），这些区域中超新星后牛顿或理想化MHD处理方法失效。

Method: Fully relativistic general relativistic magnetohydrodynamic (GRMHD) simulations of self-gravitating black hole-disk systems with varying spin-disk tilt angles ($0^\circ$--$180^\circ$), high disk-to-BH mass ratios ($16\%$--$28\%$), and rapidly rotating black holes ($\chi \lesssim 0.97$), incorporating MRI-driven turbulence and gravitational backreaction.

采用完全相对论性的广义相对论磁流体动力学（GRMHD）模拟，研究具有不同自旋-盘倾角（$0^\circ$--$180^\circ$）、高盘-黑洞质量比（$16\%$--$28\%$）和快速旋转黑洞（$\chi \lesssim 0.97$）的自引力黑洞-盘系统，包含MRI驱动的湍流和引力反作用。

Result: Massive, magnetized disks exhibit a global nonaxisymmetric instability across all tilt angles; magnetic stresses damp it in aligned systems but enhance it in antialigned ones via MRI-accelerated angular momentum transport. A persistent $m=1$ mode dominates gravitational wave emission. All models launch Blandford-Znajek (BZ) jets, with collimation dependent on spin orientation. The interplay between fast MRI and slow global instability determines system evolution.

巨大的磁化盘在所有倾角下均表现出全局非轴对称不稳定性；磁应力在对齐系统中抑制该不稳定性，但在反向对齐系统中通过MRI加速的角动量输运增强它。持久的$m=1$模式主导引力波辐射。所有模型均发射Blandford-Znajek（BZ）喷流，其准直程度取决于自旋方向。快速MRI与慢速全局不稳定性之间的耦合决定了系统的演化。

Conclusion: Tilted, self-gravitating black hole-disk systems are unstable and emit detectable gravitational waves via a dominant $m=1$ mode, while launching relativistic jets through the BZ mechanism—making them compelling multimessenger sources. These results are only accessible via self-consistent GRMHD simulations including full gravity and magnetic effects.

倾斜的自引力黑洞-盘系统不稳定，并通过主导的$m=1$模式发射可探测的引力波，同时通过BZ机制发射相对论性喷流，使其成为有吸引力的多信使源。这些结果只能通过包含完整引力和磁效应的自洽GRMHD模拟获得。

Abstract: We perform fully relativistic GRMHD simulations of magnetized, self-gravitating black hole-disk (BHD) systems in which the black hole spin is misaligned with the disk angular momentum. Massive disks (disk to BH mass ratios of $16-28\%$) around rapidly rotating black holes ($χ\lesssim 0.97$) develop a nonaxisymmetric instability for tilt angles from $0^\circ$ to $180^\circ$. Magnetic stresses damp, but do not completely suppress, the nonaxisymmetric instability, and corresponding gravitational wave (GW) emission, in aligned systems, while they enhance it in antialigned BHDs: MRI-driven turbulence enhances angular momentum transport and accelerates nonlinear instability evolution in misaligned configurations. All models launch magnetically driven jets consistent with the Blandford-Znajek (BZ) mechanism, with collimation depending on spin orientation. The GWs reflect strong nonaxisymmetric structure from a persistent $m=1$ mode. The coupling between fast MRI and the slower nonaxisymmetric instability growth governs the outcome, with tilt controlling how MRI modifies the global mode. These simulations provide the first self-consistent GRMHD treatment of tilted, self-gravitating BHD systems and support their role as multimessenger sources.

</details>


### [6] [Dynamical Black Hole Thermodynamics in Modified Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03518)
*Nikko John Leo S. Lobos,Emmanuel T. Rodulfo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates the dynamical and thermodynamic behavior of a Schwarzschild black hole in Modified Gravity (MOG) under scalar gravitational wave perturbations, showing that the interplay between scalar strain velocity and vector charge modifies surface gravity and temperature, leading to non-thermal particle production. By separating reversible horizon dynamics from irreversible entropy growth via the Raychaudhuri equation, the Generalized Second Law is preserved. The model resolves aspects of the information paradox through short-term information-carrying emissions and long-term stabilization into zero-temperature remnants as $M_G \to Q_G$, offering testable signatures for modified gravity with future gravitational-wave detectors.

本文研究了在标量引力波扰动下，修正引力（MOG）中施瓦西黑洞的动力学与热力学演化。结果表明，标量应变速度与矢量荷之间的相互作用会改变有效表面引力和瞬时动力学温度，导致非热粒子产生。通过Raychaudhuri方程分离一阶可逆视界涨落与二阶不可逆熵增，保证了广义第二定律的成立。该模型通过短期携带几何信息的辐射通道和长期趋于零温稳定残余（当$M_G \to Q_G$时）来应对黑洞信息悖论，为下一代引力波观测器检验标量-张量-矢量引力修正提供了可观测信号框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from unresolved issues in black hole thermodynamics and the information paradox within semiclassical gravity. The authors aim to explore how modifications to general relativity—specifically Scalar-Tensor-Vector Gravity (MOG)—alter black hole dynamics and thermodynamics under time-dependent perturbations, particularly whether such frameworks can resolve inconsistencies like violation of adiabaticity, entropy evolution, and information loss.

研究动机源于半经典引力中尚未解决的黑洞热力学与信息悖论问题。作者旨在探索对广义相对论的修正——特别是标量-张量-矢量引力（MOG）——如何在时变扰动下改变黑洞的动力学与热力学行为，尤其是此类理论能否解决绝热近似破坏、熵演化不一致性以及信息丢失等问题。

Method: The analysis employs the dynamical apparent horizon formalism in MOG, incorporating time-dependent scalar and vector fields under a breathing-mode gravitational wave. The effective surface gravity and dynamical temperature are derived from the evolving horizon geometry. Non-thermal particle creation is identified via breakdown of the adiabatic approximation. The Raychaudhuri equation is used to decouple first-order kinematic fluctuations (reversible) from second-order dissipative effects (irreversible entropy production), ensuring consistency with the Generalized Second Law. Long-term evaporation dynamics are studied near the extremal limit $M_G = Q_G$.

研究采用MOG中的动态视界形式体系，结合呼吸模式引力波下的时变标量场与矢量场。从演化视界几何推导有效表面引力与动力学温度，并通过绝热近似破缺识别非热粒子产生。利用Raychaudhuri方程分离一阶运动学涨落（可逆）与二阶耗散效应（不可逆熵产生），确保广义第二定律成立。在极值极限$M_G = Q_G$附近研究长期蒸发动力学。

Result: The scalar strain velocity and repulsive vector charge in MOG jointly modulate the effective surface gravity and instantaneous temperature, breaking the semiclassical adiabatic condition and inducing explicit non-thermal radiation. The Raychaudhuri equation allows a clean separation between reversible and irreversible processes, preserving the Generalized Second Law. Short-timescale emissions carry geometric correlations, providing a pathway for information escape. In the late stage, evaporation ceases as $M_G \to Q_G$, resulting in a stable, zero-temperature remnant.

MOG中的标量应变速度与排斥性矢量荷共同调制有效表面引力与瞬时温度，破坏半经典绝热条件并引发明显的非热辐射。通过Raychaudhuri方程可清晰分离可逆与不可逆过程，保持广义第二定律成立。短时间尺度辐射携带几何关联信息，为信息逃逸提供通道；晚期蒸发在$M_G \to Q_G$时停止，形成稳定的零温残余。

Conclusion: Modified Gravity (MOG) provides a self-consistent framework for black hole thermodynamics beyond general relativity, where dynamical horizons and non-adiabatic effects lead to non-thermal particle creation without violating the Generalized Second Law. The model offers a two-stage resolution to the information paradox: early-time emission of correlated information and late-time stabilization into inert, zero-temperature remnants. These features produce distinctive imprints on gravitational waveforms, making them testable with next-generation detectors like LISA or Einstein Telescope.

修正引力（MOG）为超越广义相对论的黑洞热力学提供了自洽框架，其中动态视界与非绝热效应导致非热粒子产生，同时不违反广义第二定律。该模型以两阶段方式解决信息悖论：早期相关信息辐射与晚期趋于惰性零温残余的稳定化。这些特征在引力波形上留下独特印记，可在LISA或爱因斯坦望远镜等下一代探测器中进行检验。

Abstract: We study the dynamical and thermodynamic evolution of a Schwarzschild black hole in Modified Gravity (MOG) under a scalar gravitational wave breathing mode. The time-dependent apparent horizon reveals that both the scalar strain velocity and the repulsive vector charge modulate the effective surface gravity and the instantaneous dynamical temperature in a quasi-adiabatic way. As a result, this regime breaks the semiclassical adiabatic approximation and triggers explicit non-thermal particle creation. We resolve a thermodynamic paradox by decoupling first-order reversible kinematic-horizon fluctuations from second-order irreversible entropy growth, using the Raychaudhuri equation. Consequently, the Generalized Second Law remains preserved. We apply these results to address the black hole information paradox across two timescales. Short-term non-thermal emission opens a dynamical channel for the escape of correlated geometric information. On long timescales, the massive vector field halts evaporation as mass approaches the extremal bound, $M_G \to Q_G$. This yields a stable, zero-temperature remnant. These signals provide a framework for probing scalar-tensor-vector modifications to general relativity with next-generation gravitational-wave observatories

### [7] [Entanglement generation from gravitationally produced massless vector particles during inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03822)
*Alessio Belfiglio,Mattia Dubbini,Orlando Luongo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We investigate the gravitational production of massless vector particles during single-field inflation in a quasi-de Sitter spacetime, accounting for inflaton-induced metric perturbations. The production amplitude is gauge-invariant and dominated by transverse polarizations, with preferential creation of highly energetic, nearly collinear particle pairs due to conformal symmetry and plane-wave perturbations. Sub-Hubble modes dominate production, while super-Hubble contributions are subdominant but set a lower bound on reheating temperature. We compute von Neumann entropy to study entanglement between sub- and super-Hubble modes across the horizon, analyzing primordial entanglement generation.

我们研究了在单场暴胀模型中，准德西特时空下由引力作用产生的无质量矢量粒子及其跨视界霍金半径的纠缠生成。考虑由暴胀子量子涨落引起的度规非均匀性，计算得到的产生振幅仅依赖于横向极化模式，表现出有效的规范不变性，符合将矢量场解释为电磁场的物理图像。粒子波长远小于哈勃半径，表明亚哈勃尺度的粒子产生占主导地位，且高能粒子更易被产生，极化效应对此有显著贡献。由于理论的共形不变性和度规扰动的平面波特性，近共线粒子对的产生概率最高。我们将分析扩展到超哈勃尺度，确认其对粒子数密度的贡献较小，但仍为再加热温度设定了下限。在此框架下，我们探讨了亚哈勃与超哈勃场模式之间的超视界纠缠，通过计算冯·诺依曼熵讨论了原初纠缠的生成机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Massless vector fields, such as the electromagnetic field, may be gravitationally produced during inflation, potentially leaving imprints on early universe cosmology. However, their production mechanism and associated quantum effects—particularly entanglement across the Hubble horizon—are not fully understood. We aim to clarify the role of gauge invariance, polarization, and background symmetries in particle production, and to explore how quantum correlations (entanglement) between sub- and super-Hubble modes can arise and evolve during inflation.

无质量矢量场（如电磁场）可能在暴胀期间通过引力作用产生，并在早期宇宙中留下可观测印记。然而，其产生机制及相关的量子效应——特别是跨哈勃视界的纠缠——尚未完全理解。我们的目标是阐明规范不变性、极化效应和背景对称性在粒子产生中的作用，并探索亚哈勃与超哈勃模式之间量子关联（纠缠）如何在暴胀过程中产生和演化。

Method: We consider a single-field inflationary model in a quasi-de Sitter background with metric inhomogeneities sourced by inflaton quantum fluctuations. The vector field is coupled minimally to gravity, and its equation of motion is solved in the presence of these perturbations. The particle production amplitude is computed using quantum field theory in curved spacetime, focusing on transverse polarization modes to ensure gauge invariance. The number density of produced particles is evaluated by integrating over momentum space, distinguishing sub-Hubble from super-Hubble contributions. Entanglement entropy is quantified via the von Neumann entropy of the reduced density matrix obtained by tracing out super-Hubble (or sub-Hubble) modes.

我们在准德西特背景下考虑一个单场暴胀模型，其中度规非均匀性由暴胀子量子涨落驱动。矢量场以最小方式耦合到引力，并在这些扰动存在下求解其运动方程。利用弯曲时空中的量子场论计算粒子产生振幅，重点关注横向极化模式以确保规范不变性。通过对动量空间积分计算产生粒子的数密度，区分亚哈勃与超哈勃贡献。纠缠熵通过约化密度矩阵的冯·诺依曼熵来量化，该矩阵通过对超哈勃（或亚哈勃）模式求迹得到。

Result: The particle production amplitude is found to be gauge-invariant and dominated by transverse polarizations, consistent with an electromagnetic interpretation. Production is enhanced for high-energy (ultraviolet) modes, with wavelengths much smaller than the Hubble radius ($\lambda \ll H^{-1}$), indicating that sub-Hubble physics dominates. Polarization effects significantly influence the production rate, favoring configurations with nearly collinear particle pairs due to the conformal invariance of the action and the plane-wave nature of metric perturbations. Super-Hubble contributions to the total number density are subdominant but non-zero, leading to a lower bound on the reheating temperature $T_{\text{reh}}$. Entanglement entropy, measured by the von Neumann entropy, grows with time and reflects quantum correlations between sub- and super-Hubble modes; horizon crossing modifies the entanglement structure, suggesting a dynamical origin for primordial entanglement.

发现粒子产生振幅具有规范不变性，且主要由横向极化主导，符合电磁场的物理解释。高能（紫外）模式的产生被增强，其波长远小于哈勃半径（$\lambda \ll H^{-1}$），表明亚哈勃物理占主导地位。极化效应显著影响产生率，由于作用量的共形不变性和度规扰动的平面波性质，近共线粒子对的构型更受青睐。超哈勃对总数密度的贡献虽次要但非零，从而导出了再加热温度 $T_{\text{reh}}$ 的下限。通过冯·诺依曼熵测量的纠缠熵随时间增长，反映了亚哈勃与超哈勃模式之间的量子关联；视界穿越改变了纠缠结构，暗示原初纠缠具有动力学起源。

Conclusion: Gravitational production of massless vector particles during inflation is dominated by sub-Hubble, high-energy, transversely polarized modes, with significant polarization and collinearity effects due to conformal symmetry. Although super-Hubble production is suppressed, it contributes to long-wavelength correlations and sets a lower bound on $T_{\text{reh}}$. Crucially, quantum entanglement between sub- and super-Hubble modes is generated during inflation, quantified by the von Neumann entropy, and modified by horizon crossing. This suggests that primordial entanglement could serve as a probe of early universe quantum gravity effects within the EFTofLSS and Cosmological Bootstrap frameworks.

暴胀期间无质量矢量粒子的引力产生主要由亚哈勃、高能、横向极化模式主导，共形对称性导致显著的极化和共线性效应。尽管超哈勃产生被抑制，但仍贡献于长波关联并设定了 $T_{\text{reh}}$ 的下限。关键的是，亚哈勃与超哈勃模式之间的量子纠缠在暴胀期间产生，可通过冯·诺依曼熵量化，并受视界穿越影响。这表明原初纠缠可作为早期宇宙量子引力效应的探针，适用于EFTofLSS和Cosmological Bootstrap框架。

Abstract: We study the gravitational production of spectator massless vector particles in a single-field inflationary scenario, and the related entanglement generation across the Hubble horizon. Accordingly, we consider a quasi-de Sitter background evolution, with additional metric inhomogeneities induced by the inflaton quantum fluctuations. Afterwards, we compute the corresponding production amplitude and show that it depends only on the transverse polarizations, appearing \emph{de facto} gauge-invariant, consistently with our interpretation of the vector field as the electromagnetic one. We notice that particle wavelengths turn out to be small compared to the Hubble radius, thus favoring sub-Hubble production relative to super-Hubble one. In particular, highly energetic vector particles are preferentially produced and we show that polarization effects provide a significant contribution to this behavior. Moreover, the production of nearly collinear particle pairs appears as the most probable configuration, due to the background conformal invariance of the theory and the plane-wave (massless particle-like) nature of the metric perturbation. We thus specialize our treatment to super-Hubble scales, confirming their subdominant contribution to the number density of produced particles, albeit setting a corresponding lower bound on the reheating temperature. In this scheme, we explore superhorizon entanglement between sub- and super-Hubble field modes, computing the corresponding von Neumann entropy and discussing the effects of horizon crossing on the generation of primordial entanglement.

</details>


### [8] [Dymnikova-Schwinger quantum-corrected slowly rotating wormholes: Photon and spinning particle dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03864)
*A. Errehymy,Y. Khedif,M. Daoud,B. Turimov,M. A. Khan,S. Usanov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper constructs rotating traversable wormhole solutions supported by a quantum-corrected Dymnikova-Schwinger matter profile using the generalized uncertainty principle (GUP), analyzes their geometric properties, and studies photon propagation and shadow formation via null geodesics, revealing rotational and quantum-induced asymmetries in strong-field optics.

本文基于广义不确定性原理（GUP）修正的Dymnikova-Schwinger物质分布构建了可穿越旋转虫洞解，分析了几何特性，并通过类光测地线研究光子传播与阴影形成，揭示了强场光学中由旋转和量子效应引起的不对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To develop a physically viable and singularity-free model of rotating wormholes by incorporating quantum gravity effects through the generalized uncertainty principle (GUP) while maintaining regularity and asymptotic flatness, and to explore potential observational signatures in photon dynamics and black hole shadow imagery.

为了通过广义不确定性原理（GUP）引入量子引力效应，构建物理上合理且无奇点的旋转虫洞模型，同时保持正则性和渐近平直性，并探索光子动力学和黑洞阴影图像中的潜在可观测特征。

Method: Constructed stationary, axisymmetric rotating wormhole solutions using a GUP-modified Dymnikova energy density profile, interpreted as a gravitational analogue of the Schwinger mechanism. Ensured satisfaction of asymptotic flatness and flare-out conditions at the throat. Analyzed null geodesics in this geometry to study photon motion, photon sphere structure, and shadow formation, including frame-dragging effects due to rotation and quantum corrections from the minimal length scale.

采用GUP修正的Dymnikova能量密度分布构建稳态轴对称旋转虫洞解，将其视为Schwinger机制的引力类比；确保满足渐近平直性和喉部flare-out条件；在此几何背景下分析类光测地线以研究光子运动、光子球结构及阴影形成，包含由旋转导致的拖曳效应以及来自最小长度尺度的量子修正。

Result: Obtained smooth, non-singular rotating wormhole geometries that satisfy energy condition-supporting flare-out criteria. Found that both rotation and GUP-induced quantum corrections modify the photon sphere: rotation causes splitting between co-rotating and counter-rotating orbits, while quantum effects shift the critical impact parameters. These lead to small but measurable asymmetries in the photon trajectories and shadow shape, offering potential observational signatures of quantum-gravity effects in strong-field regimes.

得到了光滑无奇点的旋转虫洞几何，满足支持flare-out条件的能量要求。发现旋转和GUP诱导的量子修正均会改变光子球结构：旋转导致顺向与逆向轨道分裂，量子效应则移动临界撞击参数。这些因素引起光子轨迹和阴影形状上的微小但可测量的不对称性，为强场区域中量子引力效应提供了潜在观测信号。

Conclusion: The GUP-corrected Dymnikova-Schwinger wormhole model provides a consistent framework for studying quantum-gravity effects in strong gravitational fields. The interplay between rotation and quantum corrections leads to observable imprints in photon dynamics and shadow morphology, making such models promising targets for future very-long-baseline interferometry (VLBI) observations and tests of quantum-informed gravity.

GUP修正的Dymnikova-Schwinger虫洞模型为研究强引力场中的量子引力效应提供了一致框架。旋转与量子修正之间的相互作用在光子动力学和阴影形态上留下可观测印记，使此类模型成为未来甚长基线干涉测量（VLBI）观测和量子启发引力理论检验的有力候选对象。

Abstract: This work studies light propagation near slowly rotating traversable wormholes supported by a quantum-inspired matter source. The model is based on the Dymnikova density profile, viewed as a gravitational analogue of the Schwinger mechanism, which yields a smooth, non-singular core. Quantum effects are included through the generalized uncertainty principle (GUP), introducing a minimal length scale while preserving regularity. Within a stationary and axisymmetric framework, we construct rotating wormhole solutions sustained by the GUP-corrected Dymnikova-Schwinger profile. The geometry satisfies key conditions such as asymptotic flatness and the flare-out requirement, and incorporates rotational features like frame dragging. We then examine photon motion via null geodesics. Both rotation and quantum corrections modify the photon sphere structure, with rotation producing a splitting between co-rotating and counter-rotating trajectories. This results in small asymmetries in photon paths and the shadow. These results provide a novel and consistent framework to probe quantum-gravity imprints in strong-field optics.

### [9] [Testing the chaos bound in the spinor field of Einstein-Euler-Heisenberg-Anti-de Sitter spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03914)
*Xiaowei Li,Bingbing Chen,Guoping Li*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We study Lyapunov exponents of chaotic particles in the spinor field within an Einstein-Euler-Heisenberg-Anti-de Sitter spacetime and examine violations of the chaos bound. Unlike in Reissner-Nordström spacetimes, violations occur only in specific parameter ranges and are strongly influenced by particle spin orientation and the cosmological constant.

我们研究了爱因斯坦-欧拉-海森堡-反德西特时空自旋场中粒子的李雅普诺夫指数，并检验了混沌界限在此场中的有效性。与RN时空不同，违背仅出现在特定参数范围内，且显著受粒子自旋取向和宇宙学常数影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The chaos bound, which limits the Lyapunov exponent $\lambda \leq 2\pi T/\hbar$, is a key feature of quantum chaos in holographic systems. While violations have been noted in scalar fields, it remains unclear whether this bound holds for fermionic (spinor) fields in nonlinear electrodynamics with curvature corrections and a cosmological constant. We aim to test the bound's validity in such extended gravitational settings and identify the role of spin and background parameters.

混沌界限$\lambda \leq 2\pi T/\hbar$是全息系统中量子混沌的关键特征。尽管在标量场中已观察到违背现象，但在包含曲率修正和宇宙学常数的非线性电动力学中，费米子（自旋）场是否满足该界限仍不清楚。我们旨在测试该界限在这些扩展引力背景下的有效性，并揭示自旋及背景参数的作用。

Method: We derive the equations of motion for spinning particles in the Einstein-Euler-Heisenberg-Anti-de Sitter black hole background using the Mathisson-Papapetrou-Dixon (MPD) framework with the Tulczyjew spin supplementary condition. The Lyapunov exponents are computed via the out-of-time-order correlator (OTOC) method adapted to classical orbits near the horizon. Parameter space scans are performed numerically for varying black hole charge, Euler-Heisenberg constant $\alpha_{\rm EH}$, cosmological constant $\Lambda$, particle charge $q$, and total angular momentum $j$, with particular attention to spin alignment along the $z$-axis.

我们在爱因斯坦-欧拉-海森堡-反德西特黑洞背景下，使用Mathisson-Papapetrou-Dixon框架结合Tulczyjew自旋补充条件推导自旋粒子的运动方程。通过适应于近 horizon 轨道的OTOC方法计算李雅普诺夫指数。对黑洞电荷、欧拉-海森堡常数$\alpha_{\rm EH}$、宇宙学常数$\Lambda$、粒子电荷$q$和总角动量$j$进行数值参数扫描，特别关注自旋沿$z$轴的取向。

Result: Lyapunov exponents exceed the chaos bound $\lambda > 2\pi T$ only within finite windows of black hole charge, particle spin, or total angular momentum, contrasting with unbounded violations in Reissner-Nordström cases. For anti-aligned spin ($s_z < 0$), even small $|\Lambda|$ can induce violations, while no violations occur for aligned spin ($s_z > 0$) regardless of $\Lambda$. The Euler-Heisenberg constant $\alpha_{\rm EH}$ suppresses chaos at large values. The cosmological constant fundamentally alters the structure of chaos bound violation regions in parameter space.

李雅普诺夫指数仅在黑洞电荷、粒子自旋或总角动量的有限区间内超过混沌界限$\lambda > 2\pi T$，不同于RN时空中随参数增大而增强的违背。对于反平行自旋($s_z < 0$)，即使很小的$|\Lambda|$也能引发违背；而平行自旋($s_z > 0$)无论$\Lambda$多大均无违背。欧拉-海森堡常数$\alpha_{\rm EH}$在较大值时抑制混沌。宇宙学常数从根本上改变了参数空间中混沌界限违背区域的结构。

Conclusion: The chaos bound can be violated in spinor fields within nonlinear electrodynamics and Anti-de Sitter geometry, but only under constrained conditions involving spin alignment and moderate parameter values. The spin degree of freedom plays a critical role in triggering or suppressing chaos, and the cosmological constant reshapes the conditions for chaos onset. This highlights the importance of spin and $\Lambda$ in holographic quantum chaos beyond scalar field models.

在非线性电动力学与反德西特几何中，自旋场内的混沌界限可在特定条件下被违背，但仅限于自旋取向与适中参数范围。自旋自由度在触发或抑制混沌中起关键作用，宇宙学常数重塑了混沌出现的条件。这凸显了自旋与$\Lambda$在超越标量场模型的全息量子混沌中的重要性。

Abstract: Violations of the chaos bound have been observed in scalar fields. In this work, we investigate the Lyapunov exponents of chaotic particles in the spinor field of an Einstein-Euler-Heisenberg-Anti-de Sitter spacetime, and test the validity of the chaos bound in this field. The influences of the black hole charge, the Euler-Heisenberg constant, cosmological constant, particle charge and total angular momentum on the exponents are analyzed. With other parameters fixed, chaos bound violations occur only within specific ranges of black hole charge, particle spin, or total angular momentum-unlike in Reissner-Nordström spacetimes, where violations intensify with larger parameter values. Notably, anti-alignment of particle spin with the $z$-axis can trigger violations even for small cosmological constants, while no violations arise for the spin aligned with the $z$-axis regardless of the cosmological constant. Our results show that the cosmological constant drastically reshapes chaos bound violation conditions compared to Reissner-Nordström spacetimes, highlighting the spin's pivotal role in chaos onset.

</details>


### [10] [Raychaudhuri Equation and Weyl-Driven Shear: A Weak-Field Approach to Lensing and Gravitational Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03996)

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates gravitational wave propagation and gravitational lensing in the weak field limit using the Raychaudhuri equation (RE), highlighting the crucial role of shear and its connection to the Weyl curvature tensor through a damped harmonic oscillator model.

本文在弱场极限下利用Raychaudhuri方程（RE）研究引力波传播和引力透镜现象，强调了剪切（shear）的关键作用，并通过阻尼谐振子模型揭示其与Weyl曲率张量的联系。

Motivation: To understand the role of spacetime curvature, particularly shear and the Weyl tensor, in gravitational phenomena such as lensing and gravitational wave propagation within the framework of the Raychaudhuri equation in the weak field regime.

Method: Applied the Raychaudhuri equation in the weak gravitational field limit; derived a Newtonian analogue of the relativistic RE; analyzed the RE for shear and linked it to the Weyl curvature tensor using a damped harmonic oscillator formalism.

在弱引力场极限下应用Raychaudhuri方程；推导了相对论性RE的牛顿类比；通过阻尼谐振子形式分析剪切的RE，并将其与Weyl曲率张量关联。

Result: Revealed the significant contribution of shear in gravitational lensing and wave propagation; established a clear connection between the shear evolution described by the RE and the Weyl tensor via a damped harmonic oscillator model; demonstrated that tidal forces encoded in the Weyl tensor play a central role in these phenomena.

揭示了剪切在引力透镜和波传播中的显著贡献；通过阻尼谐振子模型建立了RE描述的剪切演化与Weyl张量之间的明确联系；表明Weyl张量中编码的潮汐力在这些现象中起核心作用。

Conclusion: Shear is essential in describing gravitational lensing and gravitational wave propagation in weak fields; the Weyl curvature tensor, representing tidal effects, governs the behavior of geodesic congruences through the Raychaudhuri equation, with implications for both classical and quantum aspects of gravity.

剪切在描述弱场中的引力透镜和引力波传播中至关重要；代表潮汐效应的Weyl曲率张量通过Raychaudhuri方程主导测地线汇的行为，对引力的经典与量子层面均有意义。

Abstract: The letter studies phenomena like gravitational wave propagation and gravitational lensing using the celebrated Raychaudhuri equation (RE) in the weak field limit. Newtonian analogue of Relativistic RE has been explored. In doing so, role of shear has been found to be extremely important in explaining these phenomena. Consequently, the RE for shear has been used in course of the study and importance of Weyl curvature tensor in lensing and gravity wave propagation has been explicitly shown using a damped harmonic oscillator approach.

### [11] [Black Hole Persistence in New General Relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04185)
*Balkar Yildirim,Alan Albert Coley,Diego Fernando López*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates the survival of black holes through a cosmological bounce in a non-singular, closed FLRW universe within teleparallel new general relativity, using a generalized McVittie spacetime and a perturbative approach near the bounce. At leading order, the background evolution resembles a renormalized $\Lambda$-driven bounce, while higher-order effects modify the black hole horizon's evolution, breaking time symmetry due to linear perturbations.

本文研究了在基于新广义相对论的非奇异闭合FLRW宇宙中，黑洞是否能在宇宙反弹过程中存活，采用推广的McVittie时空和近反弹点的微扰方法。最低阶时背景演化类似于一个重整化的含宇宙常数的反弹模型，而高阶效应会修改黑洞视界的演化，并因线性微扰破坏时间对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To determine whether astrophysical black holes could carry information from a previous cosmological phase into the current one in bouncing cosmologies, particularly within modified gravity frameworks like new general relativity (NGR), which offer singularity resolution and alternative gravitational dynamics.

为了确定在能够消除奇点的新广义相对论（NGR）等修正引力框架下，天体物理黑洞是否可能将前一宇宙相的信息带入当前宇宙相，特别是在反弹宇宙学背景下。

Method: The authors employ a generalized McVittie metric to model a black hole embedded in a positively curved FLRW spacetime within teleparallel new general relativity. They solve the field equations perturbatively near the cosmological bounce ($t \approx 0$), treating inhomogeneities as perturbations on the background. The solution is expanded in orders: zeroth order gives the homogeneous background, while higher orders describe the black hole's local dynamics and horizon evolution.

作者采用推广的McVittie度规，在基于正空间曲率的FLRW时空中嵌入黑洞，并置于teleparallel新广义相对论（teleparallel new general relativity）框架下。通过在宇宙反弹附近（$t \approx 0$）使用微扰法求解场方程，将非均匀性视为对背景的扰动。解按阶展开：零阶给出均匀背景，高阶描述黑洞的局域动力学与视界演化。

Result: At zeroth order, the background exhibits a symmetric bounce similar to a closed $\Lambda$-dominated FLRW universe in GR, but with a renormalized spatial curvature term in the Friedmann equation due to NGR. At higher orders, the black hole horizon evolves asymmetrically across the bounce due to the emergence of a linear-in-time term in the perturbation, which breaks $t \rightarrow -t$ symmetry. The qualitative behavior of the horizon depends on the sign of integration constants in the perturbative solution.

在零阶时，背景表现出类似于广义相对论中闭合$\Lambda$主导FLRW宇宙的对称反弹，但由于NGR的影响，Friedmann方程中的空间曲率项被重整化。在高阶时，由于微扰中出现关于时间的线性项，黑洞视界在反弹前后演化不对称，破坏了$t \rightarrow -t$对称性。视界的定性行为依赖于微扰解中积分常数的符号。

Conclusion: Black holes can persist through the cosmological bounce in this model, but their local horizons evolve qualitatively differently compared to the symmetric background, with time-asymmetric dynamics induced by higher-order perturbations. This suggests that black holes may retain memory of the pre-bounce phase, depending on the initial conditions encoded in the perturbation constants, offering a potential mechanism for information transfer across cosmic bounces in NGR.

在此模型中，黑洞可以穿越宇宙反弹，但其局域视界的演化与对称背景有本质不同，高阶微扰导致时间不对称的动力学。这表明黑洞可能保留前反弹相的记忆，具体取决于微扰常数中编码的初始条件，为NGR中宇宙反弹间的信息传递提供了潜在机制。

Abstract: We investigate whether black holes can persist through the bounce with a minimal scale factor in a non-singular cosmology, whereby black holes from a previous contracting phase survive into the current expanding one. We do so by studying a generalized McVittie spacetime which embeds a spherically symmetric black hole in a positive spatial curvature bouncing FLRW cosmological background within the modified theory of teleparallel new general relativity. There are no further assumptions on the spacetime (e.g., on the form of the scale factor) initially, and the local evolution is derived from the field equations of the theory, utilizing a perturbative scheme which is valid ``near the bounce". To leading order we obtain a simple bounce solution similar to that in general relativity for a closed FLRW model with a positive cosmological constant, but in which the curvature term in the Friedmann equation is re-normalized within new general relativity. Qualitatively the minimum of the bounce at $t=0$ changes, but near the bounce the evolution remains symmetric. The central inhomogeneity evolves at higher perturbative orders, where the details depend on the arbitrary constants of the perturbative solution. Hence the evolution of the local horizon during the bounce changes qualitatively, where the effects depend on the signs of the perturbation, and the symmetry across the bounce is disrupted due to a linear term.

### [12] [A Conformal Boundary Ansatz for Warm Inflation Initialization: A Toy Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04219)
*Somnath Das,Rizwan ul Haq Ansari*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We propose a deterministic initialization mechanism for Warm Inflation using classical conformal boundary conditions, solving the 'cold start' paradox by deriving a finite initial radiation density via a Weyl mapping in an asymptotically scale-invariant pre-inflationary phase. The resulting thermal bath enables smooth transition to warm slow-roll inflation in the weak dissipative regime.

我们提出了一种基于经典共形边界条件的温暴胀确定性初始化机制，通过在渐近尺度不变的前暴胀相中利用Weyl映射导出有限初始辐射密度，解决了“冷启动”悖论。由此产生的热浴使得系统平滑过渡到弱耗散区间的温慢滚暴胀。



<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Warm Inflation suffers from the 'cold start' paradox: it requires a pre-existing thermal bath to generate dissipative friction, but there is no established mechanism to initialize this bath without fine-tuning or ad hoc assumptions. This lack of a first-principles origin for the initial conditions undermines the predictive power of the model.

温暴胀存在‘冷启动’悖论：它需要一个预先存在的热浴来产生耗散摩擦，但目前尚无基于第一性原理的机制来初始化该热浴，通常依赖精细调节或人为假设，削弱了模型的预测能力。


Method: We assume an asymptotically scale-invariant (conformally flat) pre-inflationary spacetime and apply a Weyl rescaling to the metric, which maps the vacuum state to one with finite radiation density. Using classical conformal boundary conditions, we derive the initial radiation energy density analytically. We introduce spontaneous conformal symmetry breaking to generate an emergent inflaton field coupled to this radiation bath. The dynamics are analyzed through the evolution equations of warm inflation, including dissipation term $\Gamma$, and we evaluate the initial value of the dissipative ratio $Q = \Gamma / 3H\dot{\phi}$.

我们假设一个渐近尺度不变（共形平坦）的前暴胀时空，并对度规进行Weyl重标度，将真空态映射到具有有限辐射密度的状态。利用经典共形边界条件，我们解析地推导出初始辐射能密度。引入自发共形对称性破缺以生成与该辐射浴耦合的涌现暴胀子场。通过包含耗散项$\Gamma$的温暴胀演化方程分析动力学，并计算耗散比$Q = \Gamma / 3H\dot{\phi}$的初始值。


Result: We obtain an analytically exact expression for the initial radiation density $\rho_r^{(0)} \propto H^4$ due to the conformal mapping. The induced inflaton kinematics yield $Q \ll 1$ initially, placing the universe in the weak dissipative regime. Despite small $Q$, the boundary-derived radiation provides sufficient Hubble friction to enable a deterministic transition into the warm slow-roll attractor solution without requiring quantum fluctuations or stochastic seeding.

我们得到了由共形映射导致的初始辐射密度的解析精确表达式$\rho_r^{(0)} \propto H^4$。诱导的暴胀子运动学给出初始$Q \ll 1$，使宇宙处于弱耗散区间。尽管$Q$较小，边界导出的辐射仍提供足够的哈勃摩擦，从而实现向温慢滚吸引子解的确定性过渡，无需量子涨落或随机种子。


Conclusion: The conformal boundary initialization mechanism resolves the bootstrap problem of Warm Inflation by providing a first-principles derivation of the initial thermal state. It establishes a deterministic pathway from a scale-invariant pre-inflationary phase to the warm slow-roll regime, ensuring self-consistent emergence of both inflaton and radiation. This framework enhances the theoretical consistency of dissipative inflationary models within early universe cosmology.

共形边界初始化机制通过从第一性原理导出初始热态，解决了温暴胀的自举问题。它建立了一条从尺度不变的前暴胀相到温慢滚区间的确定性路径，确保暴胀子与辐射的一致性共同产生。该框架增强了耗散暴胀模型在早期宇宙宇宙学中的理论自洽性。


Abstract: We present a theoretical framework demonstrating a deterministic initialization mechanism for Warm Inflation via classical conformal boundary conditions. A persistent challenge in dissipative inflationary models is the "cold start" paradox: initializing the requisite thermal bath to generate the dissipative friction that subsequently sustains radiation production. Postulating an idealized, asymptotically scale invariant pre-inflationary phase, we mathematically prove that a conformal Weyl mapping to the emergent metric furnishes a finite, analytically derived initial radiation density. Implementing a spontaneous conformal symmetry-breaking ansatz, an emergent inflaton field is subjected to this inherited thermal bath. We analytically derive the initial kinematics of this framework, demonstrating that for strict sub-Planckian temperatures, the universe naturally initializes in the weak dissipative regime (Q << 1). The initial Hubble friction provided by the boundary radiation enables a smooth, deterministic kinematic handoff to the warm slow-roll steady-state attractor. As a mathematical proof-of-concept, this mechanism provides a fully realized framework to bypass the bootstrap problem of warm inflation.

### [13] [Matching Tidal Deformability (Wilson) Coefficients to Black Hole Love Numbers in Higher-Curvature Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04259)
*Luohan Wang,Luis Lehner,Maitá Micol,Riccardo Sturani*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We establish a consistent mapping between tidal Love numbers and Wilson coefficients in effective field theories of higher-curvature gravity, identifying limitations in standard matching procedures and explicitly computing the coefficients for cubic gravity.

我们建立了潮汐Love数与高曲率引力有效场论中Wilson系数之间的一致映射，指出了标准匹配方法在高曲率引力理论中的局限性，并显式计算了立方引力理论的相关系数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Tidal deformability of compact objects, encoded in tidal Love numbers, plays a crucial role in gravitational-wave astronomy. In effective field theory (EFT) extensions of General Relativity, such as those involving higher-curvature terms, physical observables are governed by Wilson coefficients. However, a consistent mapping between these Love numbers and Wilson coefficients has been lacking, especially when applied to black holes in modified gravity. This gap hinders the proper interpretation of tidal effects in gravitational-wave signals within EFT frameworks.

紧凑天体的潮汐形变性（由潮汐Love数表征）在引力波天文学中起着关键作用。在广义相对论的有效场论（EFT）扩展中（例如包含高曲率项的理论），物理可观测量由Wilson系数决定。然而，在这些Love数与Wilson系数之间缺乏一致的映射，尤其是在应用于修改引力中的黑洞时。这一差距阻碍了在EFT框架内对引力波信号中潮汐效应的正确解释。

Method: We perform a systematic computation of the static linear response of a non-spinning black hole in higher-curvature gravity theories using a well-defined matching procedure between the bulk action and boundary dynamics. We go beyond the standard matching approach used in General Relativity by consistently incorporating higher-derivative operators and their contributions to the boundary action. By analyzing control cases—including Einsteinian cubic gravity—we identify conditions under which the Wilson coefficients can be unambiguously related to tidal Love numbers through a renormalized response function.

我们在高曲率引力理论中，通过体作用量与边界动力学之间的明确定义的匹配程序，系统地计算了非自旋黑洞的静态线性响应。我们通过一致地引入高阶导数算子及其对边界作用量的贡献，超越了广义相对论中使用的标准匹配方法。通过对控制案例（包括爱因斯坦立方引力）的分析，我们确定了通过重整化响应函数将Wilson系数明确关联到潮汐Love数的条件。

Result: We derive an explicit relation between the tidal Love number $k_2$ and the Wilson coefficient associated with the cubic curvature operator in cubic gravity. We show that the standard matching procedure fails to capture the correct physical content due to improper treatment of boundary terms and gauge redundancies. Our improved matching yields a physically meaningful and UV-insensitive result. The resulting mapping is robust and applicable to a broader class of higher-curvature theories.

我们推导出了立方引力中潮汐Love数$k_2$与立方曲率算子相关的Wilson系数之间的显式关系。我们表明，由于对边界项和规范冗余的处理不当，标准匹配程序无法捕捉正确的物理内容。我们改进后的匹配得到了物理上有意义且对紫外不敏感的结果。所得到的映射是稳健的，可适用于更广泛的高曲率理论。

Conclusion: A consistent mapping between tidal Love numbers and Wilson coefficients in EFTs of gravity requires careful treatment of boundary dynamics and higher-derivative terms. The standard matching procedure from General Relativity is insufficient for higher-curvature theories. Our framework provides a reliable method for connecting observable tidal responses in gravitational waves to fundamental parameters in UV-complete theories, enabling more accurate tests of gravity beyond General Relativity.

在引力有效场论中，潮汐Love数与Wilson系数之间的一致映射需要仔细处理边界动力学和高阶导数项。来自广义相对论的标准匹配程序对于高曲率理论是不够的。我们的框架提供了一种可靠的方法，将引力波中可观测的潮汐响应与紫外完备理论中的基本参数联系起来，从而实现对超越广义相对论的引力理论进行更精确的检验。

Abstract: We present a consistent mapping between tidal deformability coefficients (tidal Love numbers) and Wilson coefficients in effective field theory (EFT) descriptions of higher-curvature theories of gravity. In this work, we focus on the connection between the static response of a non-spinning black hole and the corresponding Wilson coefficient governing tidal imprints in gravitational-wave signals. We analyze a set of control cases to identify the key ingredients required for a systematic computation and matching procedure. In doing so, we highlight shortcomings in existing results that rely on the standard matching approach used in General Relativity when applied to higher-curvature gravity theories. As an explicit demonstration, we compute the relevant coefficients for cubic gravity theories. Our findings bridge an important gap in the correspondence between tidal Love numbers and Wilson coefficients in EFT extensions of General Relativity, which had not been thoroughly explored previously.

### [14] [Gravity/thermodynamics correspondence via black hole shadows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04441)
*Shao-Wen Wei,Yu-Xiao Liu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper studies the cuspy features of black hole shadows beyond the Kerr paradigm, providing a topological classification into 'rectangular' and '8-shape' types, and establishes a gravity/thermodynamics correspondence by linking shadow cusps to swallowtail singularities in thermodynamic free energy. The geometric phase transition at the cusp is shown to follow mean-field critical exponents.

本文研究了超出克尔范式的黑洞阴影中的尖锐特征，从拓扑角度将其分为“矩形”和“8字形”两类，并通过将阴影尖点与热力学自由能中的燕尾奇异性相对应，建立了引力与热力学之间的对应关系。研究表明，阴影边界自交所标志的几何相变遵循平均场普适类的临界指数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Cuspy features in black hole shadows are potential observational signatures of deviations from the Kerr metric in strong-gravity regimes. Understanding their origin and classifying their structure can provide insights into new physics and test general relativity. This work aims to rigorously classify such shadow morphologies and uncover deeper theoretical principles—particularly a possible link between spacetime geometry and gravitational thermodynamics.

黑洞阴影中的尖锐特征可能是强引力场中偏离克尔度规的可观测信号。理解其起源并分类其结构有助于揭示新物理并检验广义相对论。本工作的目标是对这类阴影形态进行严格分类，并探索更深层的理论原理——特别是时空几何与引力热力学之间可能存在的联系。

Method: The authors use parametric expressions for the shadow boundary to analyze its geometric properties. They apply topological methods to classify shadow shapes into distinct categories (e.g., rectangular vs. 8-shape). By drawing an analogy with catastrophe theory, they map the cusp formation to the swallowtail singularity in thermodynamic free energy. Three independent thermodynamic-like approaches — including bifurcation analysis, scaling laws, and free energy minimization — are used to identify the phase transition point. Analytical techniques are employed to derive critical exponents associated with the emergence of cusps.

作者利用阴影边界的参数表达式分析其几何特性，运用拓扑方法对阴影形状进行分类（如矩形与8字形）。通过类比突变理论，将尖点形成映射到热力学自由能中的燕尾奇异性。采用三种独立但等效的类热力学方法——包括分岔分析、标度律和自由能最小化——来确定相变点，并用解析方法推导出与尖点出现相关的临界指数。

Result: Two distinct topological classes of cuspy shadows are identified: 'rectangular' and '8-shape'. The self-intersection of the shadow boundary corresponds to a geometric phase transition, which maps precisely onto the swallowtail catastrophe in thermodynamic systems. All three methods consistently locate the transition point. The analytically derived critical exponents (e.g., $\beta = 1/2$) match those of the mean-field universality class, indicating universal behavior near the phase transition.

识别出两种不同的尖锐阴影拓扑类型：“矩形”和“8字形”。阴影边界的自交对应于一个几何相变，精确映射到热力学系统中的燕尾突变。三种方法一致地定位了相变点。解析得出的临界指数（例如 $\beta = 1/2$）与平均场普适类匹配，表明在相变附近存在普适行为。

Conclusion: The presence of cuspy features in black hole shadows is not merely a geometric curiosity but reflects an underlying thermodynamic structure in gravity. The established gravity/thermodynamics correspondence via the swallowtail-cusp duality provides a powerful framework for interpreting observational signatures in terms of phase transitions, suggesting that black hole shadows encode information about the fundamental thermodynamic nature of spacetime.

黑洞阴影中尖锐特征的存在不仅是几何上的奇特现象，更反映了引力背后潜在的热力学结构。通过燕尾-尖点对偶建立的引力/热力学对应关系为解释观测信号提供了有力框架，表明黑洞阴影编码了关于时空基本热力学性质的信息。

Abstract: The shadow of a black hole serves as a pristine window into the strong-gravity regime, with cuspy feature emerging as a smoking-gun signature of physics beyond the Kerr paradigm. In this paper, we extend the work of [arXiv:2601.15612 [gr-qc]] and study the detailed properties of the cuspy shadow by using the parametric expressions of the shadow boundary. From a topological perspective, we provide a rigorous topological classification of these shadows, categorizing them into distinct ``rectangular" and ``8-shape" topologies. Crucially, we establish a formal gravity/thermodynamics correspondence by mapping the cuspy shadow to the swallowtail behavior observed in thermodynamic free energy. We demonstrate that the self-intersection of the shadow boundary, marking a geometric phase transition, can be precisely determined through three independent but equivalently thermodynamic-like approaches. Furthermore, we analytically derive the critical exponents governing the emergence of these cusps, revealing that they are consistent with the mean-field universality class. Our results suggest that the observational features of black hole shadows are deeply rooted in the underlying gravitational thermodynamics, offering a novel framework to probe the fundamental nature of spacetime.

</details>


### [15] [Stationary Einstein-vector-Gauss-Bonnet black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04568)
*Burkhard Kleihaus,Jutta Kunz*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We investigate spontaneously vectorized black holes in Einstein-vector-Gauss-Bonnet theory with a quadratic coupling, finding both charged spherically symmetric and uncharged axially symmetric magnetic dipole black holes, the latter being prolate, hotter than Schwarzschild, and possessing lower free energy; rotating solutions are bounded by Kerr, static limits, and critical solutions.

我们研究了具有二次耦合的爱因斯坦-矢量-高斯-博内特理论中的自发矢量化黑洞，发现了带电球对称和不带电轴对称磁偶极黑洞，后者为长球形，温度高于史瓦西黑洞且自由能更低；旋转解的存在域由克尔黑洞、静态极限和临界解所限定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To explore spontaneous vectorization in Einstein-vector-Gauss-Bonnet gravity beyond spherical symmetry and electric charge, extending to magnetic dipole moments and rotation within modified gravity frameworks.

旨在探索爱因斯坦-矢量-高斯-博内特引力中超越球对称与电荷情形的自发矢量化现象，将研究扩展至磁偶极矩和旋转情况，以深化对修正引力框架的理解。

Method: Analytical and numerical study of static and rotating black hole solutions in Einstein-vector-Gauss-Bonnet theory with quadratic vector-Gauss-Bonnet coupling, analyzing domain of existence, thermodynamics, and geometric properties (e.g., prolateness) via field equations and boundary conditions.

Result: Discovery of uncharged, axially symmetric black holes with magnetic dipole moment, exhibiting prolate horizon geometry, higher temperature than Schwarzschild black holes ($T > T_{\rm Schw}$), and lower free energy; identification of radial excitations; domain of rotating vectorized black holes bounded by Kerr, static spherical/axial, and critical solutions.

发现了不带电、轴对称并具有磁偶极矩的黑洞，其视界呈长球形，温度高于史瓦西黑洞（$T > T_{\rm Schw}$），自由能更低；识别出径向激发态；旋转矢量化黑洞的存在域由克尔黑洞、静态球对称/轴对称解及临界解所界定。

Conclusion: Spontaneous vectorization in Einstein-vector-Gauss-Bonnet theory supports new classes of black holes beyond GR, including magnetic dipole and axially symmetric configurations, with distinct thermodynamic and geometric properties; these solutions enrich the black hole landscape in modified gravity and suggest novel phase structures.

Abstract: We study spontaneously vectorized black holes in Einstein-vector-Gauss-Bonnet theory with a quadratic coupling function. Besides the static, spherically symmetric black holes carrying an electric charge, there are uncharged static, axially symmetric black holes that possess a magnetic dipole moment. Both types possess radial excitations. The magnetic black holes are prolate. They are hotter than the Schwarzschild black holes and possess lower free energy. The domain of existence of the rotating vectorized black holes is bounded by the Kerr black holes, the spherically and axially symmetric static black holes, and the critical solutions.

### [16] [Galileon versus Quintessence: A comparative phase space analysis and late-time cosmic relevance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04582)
*Mohd Shahalam*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper compares the light mass Galileon model with Quintessence in explaining late-time cosmic acceleration using phase space analysis. While both models exhibit de-Sitter-like solutions, only Quintessence admits stable accelerating attractors for cosh-type potentials; the Galileon case yields only saddle points, indicating instability without higher-order interactions.

本文通过相空间分析比较了轻质量Galileon模型与Quintessence在解释晚期宇宙加速膨胀方面的表现。尽管两个模型都存在类似de-Sitter的解，但只有Quintessence在cosh型势下具有稳定的加速吸引子；而Galileon情形下的临界点均为鞍点，表明若无高阶相互作用则不稳定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand whether the light mass Galileon model can self-consistently describe late-time cosmic acceleration as effectively as standard Quintessence, particularly by examining the existence and stability of late-time attractor solutions in both frameworks.

旨在理解轻质量Galileon模型是否能像标准Quintessence一样有效地自洽描述晚期宇宙加速，特别是通过比较两种框架中晚期吸引子解的存在性与稳定性。

Method: The authors reformulate the cosmological equations as an autonomous dynamical system using dimensionless variables in a flat FLRW universe. They analyze stationary points and their stability for three scalar potentials (generalized cosh, simple cosh, linear) in both the Galileon and Quintessence cases, identifying critical points and evaluating eigenvalues of the Jacobian matrix to determine stability.

作者在平坦FLRW宇宙中引入无量纲变量，将宇宙学方程重写为自治动力系统。针对三种标量势（广义cosh、简单cosh、线性势），分析Galileon和Quintessence情形下的定态点及其稳定性，通过计算雅可比矩阵本征值判断临界点的稳定性。

Result: In the light mass Galileon model, all critical points are of saddle type—no stable late-time accelerating attractors exist, even when de-Sitter solutions are present. In contrast, Quintessence with cosh potentials admits stable de-Sitter attractors, making it viable for cosmic acceleration. This indicates that higher-order Galileon interactions may be necessary to achieve stability.

在轻质量Galileon模型中，所有临界点均为鞍点——即使存在de-Sitter解，也不存在稳定的晚期加速吸引子。相比之下，具有cosh势的Quintessence存在稳定的de-Sitter吸引子，因而可行为宇宙加速提供合理描述。这表明可能需要高阶Galileon相互作用才能实现稳定加速。

Conclusion: The light mass Galileon model, as studied, fails to produce stable late-time accelerating solutions due to the absence of attracting fixed points, unlike standard Quintessence which supports them for certain potentials. This reveals a qualitative difference between the two models and suggests that extensions beyond cubic Galileon interactions may be required for cosmological viability.

研究表明，轻质量Galileon模型因缺乏吸引型不动点而无法产生稳定的晚期加速解，不同于标准Quintessence可在特定势下支持此类解。这揭示了两类模型间的本质差异，并暗示需引入高于三阶的Galileon相互作用以确保宇宙学上的可行性。

Abstract: We perform a comparative phase space analysis of the light mass Galileon model and standard Quintessence in the context of late--time cosmic acceleration. Focusing on a spatially flat FLRW background, we consider a cubic Galileon interaction supplemented by a scalar potential and examine three representative choices of the potential: a generalized cosh potential, a simple cosh potential, and a linear potential. By introducing suitable dimensionless variables, the cosmological field equations are reformulated as an autonomous dynamical system, allowing a systematic investigation of the stationary points and their stability properties. For the light mass Galileon scenario, we find that although the phase space admits scalar field dominated solutions, all critical points are of saddle type for the potentials considered. In particular, no stable late-time accelerating attractor emerges, even in the presence of de-Sitter like configurations. In contrast, the Quintessence limit admits stable de-Sitter attractors for cosh potentials, providing a viable description of the observed late--time acceleration. Our results highlight a key qualitative distinction between Galileon and Quintessence cosmologies and indicate that, within the light mass Galileon framework, the higher-order Galileon interactions may be required to realize a stable accelerating Universe.

</details>


### [17] [Cosmic Inflation From Regular Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04601)
*Kensuke Sueto,Riku Yoshimoto,Pablo A. Cano*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We study braneworld cosmology in quasi-topological gravity (QTG) with higher-curvature corrections, showing that a FLRW brane in a static bulk with regular black holes undergoes a universal early-time de Sitter inflation phase determined by the length scale $\sqrt{\alpha}$, independent of matter content. The number of e-folds is estimated universally as $N_e \sim \log(r_g/\sqrt{\alpha})$, and standard low-energy cosmology is recovered at late times. Numerical results confirm analytic predictions using Dymnikova-like and Hayward black hole geometries.

我们研究了带有高阶曲率修正的拟拓扑引力（quasi-topological gravity, QTG）中的膜宇宙学，表明在具有正则黑洞解的静态体空间中运动的FLRW膜会在早期经历一个由长度尺度$\sqrt{\alpha}$决定的普适德西特暴胀相，且该过程与膜上物质内容无关。暴胀e-fold数可普适估计为$N_e \sim \log(r_g/\sqrt{\alpha})$，而低能下可恢复标准宇宙学。数值计算基于Dymnikova型和Hayward黑洞几何验证了解析结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: In conventional braneworld models like Randall-Sundrum, early-universe singularities and trans-Planckian energy densities pose serious challenges. Higher-curvature corrections in the bulk may resolve these issues by modifying gravity at high energies. Quasi-topological gravity (QTG), which includes an infinite tower of higher-derivative terms in $D \geq 5$, provides a controlled framework to explore such modifications while admitting regular black hole solutions. We aim to understand how these quantum-gravity-motivated corrections affect cosmological evolution on the brane, particularly in the early universe.

在诸如Randall-Sundrum之类的传统膜宇宙模型中，早期宇宙奇点和超普朗克能量密度带来了严重挑战。体空间中的高阶曲率修正可能通过在高能下修改引力来解决这些问题。拟拓扑引力（QTG）在$D \geq 5$中包含无限阶高阶导数项，为探索此类修正提供了可控框架，并允许存在正则黑洞解。我们的目标是理解这些受量子引力启发的修正如何影响膜上的宇宙演化，特别是在早期宇宙中。

Method: We derive $\mathbb{Z}_2$-symmetric junction conditions for a FLRW brane embedded in a static, spherically symmetric bulk spacetime governed by QTG. Using the generalized Einstein equations with higher-curvature terms, we obtain modified Friedmann equations on the brane. By analyzing the asymptotic behavior of the bulk metric near the origin and at large distances, we identify distinct cosmological regimes. A universal scaling argument gives an estimate for the duration of inflation (number of e-folds) based on the ratio $r_g / \sqrt{\alpha}$. Numerical integration of the full dynamical equations is performed for two explicit regular black hole geometries: Dymnikova-like and Hayward metrics.

我们在由QTG支配的静态、球对称体时空中推导了FLRW膜的$\mathbb{Z}_2$对称连接条件。利用含高阶曲率项的广义爱因斯坦方程，得到膜上的修正弗里德曼方程。通过对体度规在原点附近及大距离下的渐近行为分析，我们识别出不同的宇宙学区域。基于$r_g / \sqrt{\alpha}$比值的普适标度论证给出了暴胀持续时间（e-fold数）的估计。并对两种明确的正则黑洞几何——Dymnikova型和Hayward度规——进行全动力学方程的数值积分。

Result: The modified Friedmann equation takes the form $H^2 \sim \frac{1}{\alpha} f\left(\frac{a}{\sqrt{\alpha}}\right)$, leading to $H \to 1/\sqrt{\alpha}$ as $a \to 0$, i.e., a de Sitter phase with Hubble parameter set solely by the higher-curvature scale. At late times ($a \gg \sqrt{\alpha}$), standard General Relativity (GR) dynamics are recovered. The number of e-folds during inflation is universally estimated as $N_e \approx \log_{e}(r_g / \sqrt{\alpha})$, where $r_g$ is the gravitational radius of the bulk black hole. Numerical simulations confirm this scaling and show that inflation begins when the brane approaches the deep interior of the regular black hole and ends as it exits into the Schwarzschild-like region. Crucially, the inflationary dynamics are insensitive to the brane's matter content.

修正后的弗里德曼方程形式为$H^2 \sim \frac{1}{\alpha} f\left(\frac{a}{\sqrt{\alpha}}\right)$，导致当$a \to 0$时$H \to 1/\sqrt{\alpha}$，即哈勃参数仅由高曲率尺度设定的德西特相。在晚期（$a \gg \sqrt{\alpha}$），恢复标准广义相对论（GR）动力学。暴胀期间的e-fold数可普适估计为$N_e \approx \log_{e}(r_g / \sqrt{\alpha})$，其中$r_g$是体黑洞的引力半径。数值模拟证实了这一标度关系，并显示当膜接近正则黑洞深内部时暴胀开始，当其退出至类施瓦西区域时结束。关键的是，暴胀动力学对膜上的物质内容不敏感。

Conclusion: Quasi-topological gravity in the bulk leads to a robust early-universe inflationary scenario on the brane, driven purely by higher-curvature effects and controlled by the scale $\sqrt{\alpha}$. This inflationary phase is generic, model-independent within the class of regular black hole solutions, and naturally avoids trans-Planckian matter densities. The number of e-folds is determined geometrically by the bulk black hole structure, offering a novel mechanism for graceful exit without fine-tuning. This work demonstrates the potential of QTGs as UV-complete gravitational theories in $D \geq 5$ to yield testable, singularity-free cosmologies in four dimensions.

体空间中的拟拓扑引力在膜上导致了一个稳健的早期宇宙暴胀情景，完全由高曲率效应驱动并由尺度$\sqrt{\alpha}$控制。该暴胀相在正则黑洞解类别中是普适且模型无关的，并自然避免了超普朗克物质密度。e-fold数由体黑洞结构几何决定，提供了一种无需精细调节的优雅退出新机制。本工作展示了QTG作为$D \geq 5$中紫外完备引力理论的潜力，可在四维中产生可检验且无奇点的宇宙学。

Abstract: We study braneworld cosmology in quasi-topological gravity (QTG) with an infinite tower of higher-curvature terms, focusing on the case in which the bulk admits regular black hole solutions. We derive the $\mathbb{Z}_2$-symmetric junction conditions for a FLRW brane moving in a static, spherically symmetric bulk geometry, and obtain the corresponding modified Friedmann equations for the scale factor. We prove that, in the small scale factor regime, the brane generically approaches a de Sitter phase characterized solely by the length scale $\sqrtα$ of the higher-derivative terms, while the standard Einstein-gravity braneworld dynamics is recovered in the low-energy regime. We further provide a universal estimate for the number of e-folds of the de Sitter phase in terms of the ratio between the black hole scale and the scale of new physics $r_g/\sqrtα$. The inflationary regime is fully independent of the brane matter content and hence avoids the problem of trans-Planckian matter densities. Numerical integrations for explicit regular bulk solutions (Dymnikova-like and Hayward black holes) confirm these estimates and illustrate how the bulk black hole sector controls the onset and termination of inflation. This framework leverages the powerful properties of QTGs, defined only in $D\ge 5$, to study consequences for a four-dimensional universe.

</details>


### [18] [Preliminary study on the impact of stress-energy tensor compared to scalar field in Nonminimal Derivative model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04617)
*Ilham Prasetyo,Bobby Eka Gunara,Agus Suroso*

TL;DR: We compare NMDC-T and NMDC-phi models in a nonminimal derivative coupling gravity framework using an incompressible star, finding that the coupling parameter in NMDC-T (trace of stress-energy tensor) is less sensitive than in NMDC-phi (scalar field) regarding compactness and mass-radius relations.

我们比较了非最小导数耦合引力框架下NMDC-T和NMDC-phi模型在不可压缩星体中的表现，发现关于致密性和质量-半径关系，NMDC-T（应力-能量张量的迹）的耦合参数比NMDC-phi（标量场）更不敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

为了研究不同的标量-张量耦合方式——通过应力-能量张量的迹（$T$）与实标量场（$\phi$）——如何影响修改引力下的恒星结构，特别是在非最小导数耦合（NMDC）框架内。

Method: We apply the NMDC-T and NMDC-phi models to an incompressible perfect fluid star with constant energy density.
