我们将NMDC-T和NMDC-phi模型应用于具有恒定能量密度的不可压缩理想流体星体。在每种模型下修正Tolman–Oppenheimer–Volkoff（TOV）方程，并通过数值求解计算质量-半径关系以及作为耦合参数函数的恒星致密性。

Result: The NMDC-T model exhibits weaker dependence on its coupling parameter compared to NMDC-phi, implying greater stability and less variation in predicted maximum mass and compactness. Thus, NMDC-T is less sensitive to changes in the coupling strength.

NMDC-T模型对其耦合参数的依赖性弱于NMDC-phi，意味着其预测的最大质量和致密性具有更高的稳定性且变化更小。因此，NMDC-T对耦合强度的变化更不敏感。

Conclusion: In the context of stellar structure within NMDC gravity, using the trace of the stress-energy tensor (NMDC-T) leads to more robust predictions than using a direct scalar field coupling (NMDC-phi), due to reduced sensitivity to the coupling parameter.

在NMDC引力的恒星结构背景下，使用应力-能量张量的迹（NMDC-T）比直接标量场耦合（NMDC-phi）能给出更稳健的预测，因其对耦合参数的敏感性更低。

Abstract: In this article, we report the results of comparing the effect of using trace of stress-energy tensor versus real-valued scalar field in Nonminimal Derivative Coupling gravitation model, respectively denoted as NMDC-T and NMDC-phi. We employ the model into an incompressible star and see the effect of both models NMDC-T and NMDC-phi on the compactness and mass-radius relation. We find that coupling parameters of NMDC-T is less sensitive than NMDC-phi.

### [19] [New Almost Universal Metrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04639)
*Metin Gurses,Tahsin Cagri Sisman,Bayram Tekin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper identifies nonzero constant curvature pp-wave metrics as a new member of the Kerr-Schild-Kundt class, showing they are almost universal—reducing generic gravitational field equations to those of cosmological Einstein-Maxwell theory with null dust. These metrics have topology $\mathbb{R}^{1,1}\times S^{2}$, completing a triplet with Nariai ($\mathrm{dS}^2 \times S^2$) and Bertotti-Robinson ($\mathrm{AdS}^2 \times S^2$), and are demonstrated in quadratic and cubic gravity.

本文识别出非零常曲率pp波度规作为Kerr-Schild-Kundt类的新成员，表明其几乎是普适的——将一般的引力场方程约化为带零尘的宇宙学爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论。这些度规具有拓扑 $\mathbb{R}^{1,1}\times S^{2}$，补全了Nariai（$\mathrm{dS}^2 \times S^2$）和Bertotti-Robinson（$\mathrm{AdS}^2 \times S^2$）构成的三重结构，并在二次与三次引力理论中验证了结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To extend the known class of almost universal metrics by identifying new solutions that simplify gravitational field equations in generic metric theories of gravity, particularly within the Kerr-Schild-Kundt (KSK) class, and to find a missing counterpart to well-known geometries like Nariai and Bertotti-Robinson in terms of spacetime topology and quantum protection.

旨在通过识别可在一般度规引力理论中简化场方程的新解，扩展已知的几乎普适度规类别，特别是Kerr-Schild-Kundt（KSK）类；并寻找在时空拓扑和量子保护方面与Nariai和Bertotti-Robinson等著名几何相对应的缺失伙伴。

Method: The authors employ the Kerr-Schild-Kundt formalism to construct a new type of pp-wave metric with nonzero constant curvature. They analyze how generic gravitational field equations based on arbitrary diffeomorphism-invariant actions reduce when evaluated on this background. By computing geometric quantities such as the Riemann tensor and its contractions, they show the field equations reduce to those of cosmological Einstein-Maxwell theory coupled to null dust. The analysis is verified explicitly in higher-derivative theories, specifically quadratic and cubic gravity.

作者采用Kerr-Schild-Kundt形式体系构造了一类具有非零常曲率的新pp波度规。他们分析了基于任意微分同胚不变作用量的广义引力场方程在此背景下的约化行为。通过计算黎曼张量及其缩并等几何量，证明场方程约化为带零尘的宇宙学爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论。该分析在高阶导数理论（特别是二次与三次引力）中得到了显式验证。

Result: It is shown that nonzero constant curvature pp-wave metrics belong to the almost universal Kerr-Schild-Kundt class. The full nonlinear field equations in generic gravity theories reduce to a simpler system: effectively equivalent to cosmological Einstein-Maxwell theory with null dust. The spacetime has topology $\mathbb{R}^{1,1} \times S^2$, making it the long-sought topological counterpart to $\mathrm{dS}_2 \times S^2$ (Nariai) and $\mathrm{AdS}_2 \times S^2$ (Bertotti-Robinson). This structure is confirmed in quadratic and cubic gravity models.

研究表明，非零常曲率pp波度规属于几乎普适的Kerr-Schild-Kundt类。在一般引力理论中，完整的非线性场方程被约化为更简单的系统：等效于带零尘的宇宙学爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论。时空拓扑为 $\mathbb{R}^{1,1} \times S^2$，使其成为 $\mathrm{dS}_2 \times S^2$（Nariai）和 $\mathrm{AdS}_2 \times S^2$（Bertotti-Robinson）长期寻找的拓扑对应体。这一结构在二次与三次引力模型中得到确认。

Conclusion: Nonzero constant curvature pp-waves are established as almost universal metrics that significantly simplify gravitational dynamics across wide classes of theories. Their inclusion completes a symmetric triplet of quantum-protected geometries with $S^2$ fibered over two-dimensional maximally symmetric spaces. These results deepen the understanding of universality in gravity and provide new exact solutions for studying high-energy and quantum aspects of spacetime.

非零常曲率pp波被确立为几乎普适的度规，能在广泛的引力理论中显著简化动力学。它们的引入完成了以二维最大对称空间为底、$S^2$为纤维的量子保护几何三重对称结构。这些结果深化了对引力中普适性的理解，并为研究时空的高能与量子特性提供了新的精确解。

Abstract: Plane waves and pp-waves are well-known universal metrics that solve all metric-based gravitational field equations. Similarly, the Kerr-Schild-Kundt class of metrics is almost universal: all metric-based gravitational field equations reduce to a linear scalar partial differential equation that always admits a solution. Here, we add a new member to this class of metrics and show that nonzero constant curvature pp-wave metrics are also almost universal. They reduce the generic gravity field equations to those of cosmological Einstein-Maxwell theory with null dust. The background of the pp-waves has the topology $\mathbb{R}^{1,1}\times S^{2}$ and provides the missing partner to the Nariai metric with ${\rm dS}^{2}\times S^{2}$ and the Bertotti-Robinson metric with ${\rm AdS}^{2}\times S^{2}$ topologies. These quantum-protected metrics are of clear interest. We exemplify our results by using the quadratic and cubic gravity theories.

</details>


### [20] [EHT-Constrained Analysis of Shadow Deformation in Quantum-Improved Rotating Non-Singular Magnetic Monopole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04695)
*Gowtham Sidharth M,Sanjit Das*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We investigate the shadow of a rotating Bardeen black hole in asymptotically safe gravity using the Hamilton-Jacobi method to analyze null geodesics. Increasing the asymptotic safety parameter and spin reduces the shadow size and enhances distortion, while the monopole charge significantly influences the shadow profile. We also compute the energy emission rate for different values of the asymptotic safety parameter.

我们通过Hamilton-Jacobi方法研究了渐近安全引力框架下旋转Bardeen黑洞的阴影，分析了类光测地线。随着渐近安全参数和自旋参数的增加，阴影尺寸减小而畸变增强，单极荷对阴影轮廓有重要影响。我们还计算了不同渐近安全参数下的能量辐射率。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand how quantum gravitational effects encoded in asymptotically safe gravity modify black hole observables, particularly the shadow and energy emission properties of a regular rotating Bardeen black hole.

为了理解渐近安全引力中编码的量子引力效应如何改变黑洞可观测量，特别是正则旋转Bardeen黑洞的阴影和能量辐射特性。

Method: We employed the Hamilton-Jacobi separation method to solve the null geodesic equations in the spacetime of a rotating Bardeen black hole within asymptotically safe gravity. Shadow observables such as angular diameter and distortion parameters were derived from the celestial coordinates. The energy emission rate was computed using the limiting radius of the unstable circular photon orbit.

我们采用Hamilton-Jacobi分离方法求解渐近安全引力中旋转Bardeen黑洞时空中的类光测地线方程。从天球坐标推导出角直径和畸变参数等阴影观测量。利用不稳定光子圆轨道的极限半径计算能量辐射率。

Result: An increase in both the asymptotic safety parameter $\xi$ and the spin parameter $a$ results in a smaller apparent shadow size and greater distortion. The monopole charge (related to the Bardeen model's regularity) significantly affects the shape and size of the shadow. The energy emission rate increases with higher $\xi$, indicating enhanced radiation due to quantum gravitational corrections.

渐近安全参数$\xi$和自旋参数$a$的增加导致表观阴影尺寸减小且畸变增大。单极荷（与Bardeen模型的正则性相关）显著影响阴影的形状和大小。能量辐射率随$\xi$增大而增加，表明量子引力修正增强了辐射。

Conclusion: The shadow characteristics of rotating Bardeen black holes are sensitive to asymptotically safe gravity effects. The reduction in shadow size and increased distortion offer potential observational signatures for quantum gravity in strong-field regimes. The modified energy emission rate further supports the role of asymptotic safety in altering black hole thermodynamics and emission processes.

旋转Bardeen黑洞的阴影特征对渐近安全引力效应敏感。阴影尺寸减小和畸变增加为强场区域中量子引力提供了潜在的观测信号。修正的能量辐射率进一步支持了渐近安全在改变黑洞热力学和辐射过程中的作用。

Abstract: We studied the shadow cast by a rotating Bardeen black hole within the framework of asymptotically safe gravity. The null geodesics were analyzed using the Hamilton Jacobi separation method to derive shadow observables. Our findings show that an increase in both the asymptotic safety parameter and the spin parameter leads to a decrease in the apparent shadow size and an increase in shadow distortion. The monopole charge of the black hole played an important role in the shadow profile. Furthermore, we compute the energy emission rate associated with varying values of the asymptotic safety parameter.

### [21] [Optical Appearance and Ringdown of Black Holes in a Kalb Ramond Field Coupled to Perfect Fluid Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04706)
*Qi-Qi Liang,Zi-Qiang Cai,Dong Liu,Zheng-Wen Long*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper studies the optical and dynamical properties of a static spherically symmetric black hole in the presence of a Kalb--Ramond (KR) field coupled to perfect fluid dark matter (PFDM), focusing on the effects of the Lorentz-violating parameter $\alpha$ and the dark matter parameter $\lambda$. The authors analyze photon trajectories, observational signatures in the strong-gravity regime, and quasinormal modes under scalar, electromagnetic, and gravitational perturbations. They find that the quasinormal modes agree with null geodesic properties in the eikonal limit and that both $\alpha$ and $\lambda$ significantly influence the black hole's shadow and ringdown dynamics.

本文研究了在Kalb-Ramond（KR）场与完美流体暗物质（PFDM）耦合情况下，静态球对称黑洞的光学与动力学性质，重点关注洛伦兹破缺参数$\alpha$和暗物质参数$\lambda$的影响。作者分析了光子轨迹、强引力区的观测特征以及标量、电磁和引力扰动下的准正规模，发现准正规模在几何光学近似下与零测地线特性一致，并且$\alpha$和$\lambda$显著影响黑洞阴影和环降动力学行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand how Lorentz symmetry violation and dark matter environments affect black hole physics in strong gravitational fields, particularly through observable signatures such as photon orbits and quasinormal modes.

旨在理解洛伦兹对称性破缺和暗物质环境如何影响强引力场中的黑洞物理，特别是通过光子轨道和准正规模等可观测特征。


Method: The study employs analytical and numerical methods to solve the geodesic equations for photons in the KR-PFDM black hole spacetime. Observational signatures like the shadow radius and deflection angle are computed. Quasinormal modes are calculated using the WKB approximation and via the connection between eikonal modes and null geodesics, specifically the unstable circular photon orbits characterized by the effective potential.

采用解析与数值方法求解KR-PFDM黑洞时空中光子的测地线方程，计算黑洞阴影半径和偏转角等观测特征；利用WKB近似并结合几何光学极限下零测地线（特别是由有效势决定的不稳定光子圆轨道）来计算准正规模。


Result: The parameters $\alpha$ and $\lambda$ significantly modify the effective potential, photon orbits, and hence the black hole shadow size and shape. Larger values of $|\alpha|$ or $\lambda$ generally increase the shadow radius. The quasinormal mode frequencies (both oscillation and damping) are altered in a manner consistent with changes in the unstable null geodesics. A direct correspondence is confirmed between the real part of the quasinormal frequency and the angular velocity of photons, and between the imaginary part and the Lyapunov exponent, within the eikonal approximation.

参数$\alpha$和$\lambda$显著改变有效势、光子轨道，从而影响黑洞阴影的大小与形状；$|\alpha|$或$\lambda$越大，阴影半径通常越大。准正规模频率（振荡与衰减部分）的变化与不稳定零测地线的改变一致；在eikonal近似下，准正规模实部与光子角速度、虚部与Lyapunov指数之间的直接对应关系得到验证。


Conclusion: The KR-PFDM black hole model exhibits distinct optical and dynamical features sensitive to both Lorentz violation and dark matter. These effects can be probed through black hole shadow observations and gravitational wave ringdown signals, offering a pathway to constrain exotic physics in strong-field gravity.

KR-PFDM黑洞模型展现出对洛伦兹破缺和暗物质敏感的独特光学与动力学特征，这些效应可通过黑洞阴影观测和引力波环降信号加以探测，为限制强场引力中的新物理提供了途径。

Abstract: This paper investigates the optical and dynamical properties of a static spherically symmetric black hole in the presence of a Kalb--Ramond (KR) field coupled to perfect fluid dark matter (PFDM). We analyze the effects of the Lorentz-violating parameter $α$ and the dark matter parameter $λ$ on photon trajectories and their observational signatures in the strong-gravity regime. Furthermore, we study the quasinormal mode spectrum under scalar, electromagnetic, and gravitational perturbations, examining how the model parameters influence the characteristic oscillation frequencies and damping rates. In particular, the interplay between the effective potential structure and perturbative dynamics is clarified, and it is found that, within the validity of the eikonal approximation, the quasinormal modes of the black hole considered here exhibit good agreement with the properties of null geodesics. Our results show that the model parameters significantly affect both the optical appearance of the black hole and the dynamical features of the ringdown phase, providing potential observational constraints on Lorentz-violating effects and dark matter environments in strong-field regimes.

### [22] [Subtleties in non-equilibrium horizon thermodynamics of modified gravity theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04731)
*Vishnu A Pai,Vishnu S Namboothiri,Titus K Mathew*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper analyzes two non-equilibrium thermodynamic formulations of gravity in modified theories—specifically the local Rindler horizon approach and the cosmological apparent horizon approach—and demonstrates that although both include entropy production terms resembling non-equilibrium thermodynamics, their origins and physical roles differ fundamentally. In the Rindler framework, the entropy term arises from Bianchi identity consistency, while in the FLRW case it is introduced ad hoc to recover Friedmann equations. Moreover, only the apparent-horizon formulation directly couples thermodynamics to gravitational dynamics, highlighting that thermodynamic descriptions in modified gravity are not unique and depend on variable choices.

本文分析了修改引力理论中两种非平衡态热力学形式——局域黎德勒视界方法与宇宙学表观视界方法，表明尽管两者均包含类似非平衡态热力学的熵产生项，但其来源和物理作用本质上不同。在黎德勒框架中，额外熵项源于与Bianchi恒等式相关的相容性要求；而在FLRW情形中，该术语被人为引入以恢复Friedmann方程。此外，只有表观视界方法将非平衡贡献直接嵌入引力动力学方程。研究还指出，在修改引力中视界的热力学描述并非唯一，平衡与非平衡描述可由不同热力学变量选择导致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To clarify the conceptual and mathematical differences between two prominent non-equilibrium thermodynamic interpretations of gravity in modified theories—specifically the Rindler-horizon-based approach by Eling, Guedens, and Jacobson and the apparent-horizon formulation in FLRW cosmology—despite their shared use of entropy balance equations. The motivation stems from the need to establish a consistent thermodynamic foundation for gravity beyond general relativity, where ambiguities in the origin and role of entropy production terms can lead to misinterpretations.

旨在澄清在修改引力理论中两种重要非平衡态引力热力学解释之间的概念与数学差异——即基于黎德勒视界的方法（Eling, Guedens, and Jacobson）与FLRW宇宙学中表观视界形式，尽管二者均使用熵平衡方程。动机源于建立超越广义相对论的引力一致热力学基础的需求，而熵产生项的来源与作用上的模糊性可能导致误解。

Method: The analysis is based on a comparative study of the entropy balance relation $ \frac{\delta Q}{T} = dS + d_i S $ in two distinct geometric settings: local Rindler horizons in generic spacetimes and cosmological apparent horizons in FLRW universes. For each case, the derivation of the entropy production term is revisited using the respective field equations (e.g., $f(R)$ or scalar-tensor gravity), focusing on how the Clausius relation is modified. The role of the Bianchi identity and the requirement to recover the Friedmann equations are examined as key constraints. The distinction between thermodynamic variables (e.g., entropy vs. energy definitions) in each framework is also analyzed.

该分析基于对熵平衡关系 $ \frac{\delta Q}{T} = dS + d_i S $ 在两种不同几何背景下的比较研究：一般时空中的局域黎德勒视界与FLRW宇宙中的宇宙学表观视界。针对每种情况，利用相应的场方程（如$f(R)$或标量-张量引力）重新审视熵产生项的推导，重点关注Clausius关系如何被修改。研究了Bianchi恒等式的作用以及恢复Friedmann方程的要求作为关键约束，并分析了各框架中热力学变量（如熵与能量定义）的区别。

Result: It is shown that in the Rindler-horizon approach, the additional entropy production term originates from the requirement of consistency with the Bianchi identity $\nabla_\mu G^{\mu\nu} = 0$, ensuring diffeomorphism invariance, and thus reflects intrinsic geometric constraints. In contrast, in the apparent-horizon formulation, the same term is introduced phenomenologically to ensure compatibility with the dynamical Friedmann equations, without direct link to spacetime symmetries. Crucially, only in the latter does the entropy production directly enter the gravitational field equations. Furthermore, different choices of thermodynamic variables (e.g., redefining entropy or energy flux) can transform a non-equilibrium description into an equilibrium one, demonstrating the non-uniqueness of thermodynamic interpretations in modified gravity.

研究表明，在黎德勒视界方法中，额外的熵产生项源于与Bianchi恒等式$\nabla_\mu G^{\mu\nu} = 0$保持一致的要求，确保微分同胚不变性，因而反映了内在的几何约束。相比之下，在表观视界形式中，同一术语是现象学引入的，以保证与动力学Friedmann方程兼容，而并不直接关联时空对称性。关键的是，只有在后者中，熵产生项才直接进入引力场方程。此外，不同热力学变量的选择（例如，重新定义熵或能流）可将非平衡描述转化为平衡描述，表明在修改引力中热力学解释并非唯一。

Conclusion: The presence of entropy production terms in thermodynamic analogies of gravity in modified theories does not imply a universal non-equilibrium nature of spacetime. Instead, the physical interpretation depends on the geometric context and choice of thermodynamic variables. The Rindler-horizon and apparent-horizon frameworks represent distinct paradigms: the former embeds thermodynamics within local spacetime structure via geometric identities, while the latter ties it directly to cosmological dynamics. A consistent thermodynamic interpretation of gravity must therefore carefully distinguish between these origins and avoid conflating phenomenological necessity with fundamental geometric principles.

在修改引力理论中，引力热力学类比中存在熵产生项并不意味着时空具有普遍的非平衡本质。相反，物理诠释依赖于几何背景和热力学变量的选择。黎德勒视界与表观视界框架代表了不同的范式：前者通过几何恒等式将热力学嵌入局部时空结构，后者则将其直接与宇宙学动力学联系起来。因此，对引力的一致热力学诠释必须仔细区分这些来源，避免将现象学必要性与基本几何原理混淆。

Abstract: Thermodynamic interpretations of gravity often arise from applying the Clausius relation to spacetime horizons. In modified gravity theories with higher-order equations of motion, such as f(R) and scalar-tensor gravity, this relation generally acquires additional entropy-production term. In this context, two distinct formulations have been proposed in literature: the non-equilibrium approach of Eling, Guedens, and Jacobson based on local Rindler horizons, and the thermodynamic formulation of cosmological apparent horizons in FLRW spacetimes. In this article, we present a detailed analysis of these approaches, and show that, even though both employ identical entropy balance relations that resemble non-equilibrium thermodynamics, the exact origin and role of each entropy-production term is fundamentally different. In the Rindler-horizon framework the extra term follows directly from consistency requirements related to the Bianchi identity, whereas in the apparent-horizon approach it is introduced solely to recover the Friedmann equations. Furthermore, we will see that the latter non-equilibrium contribution enters directly into dynamical equations of gravity, while the former does not. Finally, we also highlight the fact that thermodynamic descriptions of horizons in such modified gravity are not unique, and that equilibrium, and non-equilibrium descriptions can arise from different choices of thermodynamic variables. A clear understanding of these distinctions is therefore crucial for establishing a consistent and physically meaningful thermodynamic foundation for gravity beyond general relativity.

### [24] [Gravitational waves production during preheating within GB gravity with monomial coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04764)
*Brahim Asfour,Yahya Ladghami,Taoufik Ouali*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We study gravitational wave production during preheating in a Gauss-Bonnet inflation model with power-law potential and coupling, linking it to observable parameters such as the spectral index $n_s$. By connecting preheating duration $N_{\text{pre}}$ to inflationary observables, we show that the generated gravitational wave energy density today is consistent with Planck data for specific values of the Gauss-Bonnet coupling $\alpha = -1.5\times 10^{-6}$, equation of state $\omega = 1/6$, and efficiency parameter $\delta = 10^5$.

我们研究了在具有幂律势和高斯-邦内耦合的高斯-邦内膨胀模型中，预热阶段引力波的产生。通过将预热持续时间$N_{\text{pre}}$与可观测参数（如谱指数$n_s$）联系起来，我们发现当前宇宙的引力波能量密度在特定参数下（如高斯-邦内耦合常数$\alpha = -1.5\times 10^{-6}$、有效状态方程$\omega = 1/6$、效率参数$\delta = 10^5$）与普朗克观测数据一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Gravitational waves from preheating can carry unique imprints of high-energy physics in the early universe, offering a probe beyond CMB observations. The Gauss-Bonnet inflation model provides a well-motivated extension of standard inflation due to its connection with string theory and natural suppression of higher-order corrections. We aim to link preheating dynamics directly to inflationary parameters constrained by Planck, enabling testable predictions for gravitational wave signatures.

预热阶段产生的引力波可携带早期宇宙高能物理的独特印记，提供超越CMB观测的探针。高斯-邦内膨胀模型因其与弦理论的联系及对高阶修正的自然抑制，是标准膨胀模型的一个良好扩展。我们的目标是将预热动力学直接与普朗克约束的膨胀参数联系起来，从而对引力波信号做出可检验的预测。

Method: We consider a Gauss-Bonnet inflation model with power-law potential $V(\phi) = V_0 \phi^n$ and monomial coupling $\xi(\phi) = \xi_0 \phi^n$. Using the slow-roll approximation during inflation, we derive predictions for scalar spectral index $n_s$ and tensor-to-scalar ratio $r$, comparing them with Planck data. For preheating, we employ an analytical approach that relates the duration $N_{\text{pre}}$ to the equation of state $\omega$ and efficiency parameter $\delta$, computing the resulting stochastic gravitational wave background via parametric resonance. The energy density $\Omega_{\text{GW}} h^2$ is then expressed in terms of $n_s$ through the linked parameter space.

我们考虑一个具有幂律势$V(\phi) = V_0 \phi^n$和单项耦合$\xi(\phi) = \xi_0 \phi^n$的高斯-邦内膨胀模型。利用膨胀期间的慢滚近似，推导出标量谱指数$n_s$和张标比$r$的预测，并与普朗克数据比较。对于预热阶段，我们采用一种解析方法，将持续时间$N_{\text{pre}}$与状态方程$\omega$和效率参数$\delta$关联，通过参量共振计算产生的随机引力波背景。能量密度$\Omega_{\text{GW}} h^2$随后通过参数空间与$n_s$相关联。

Result: The model predicts a present-day gravitational wave energy density $\Omega_{\text{GW}} h^2$ that depends on the scalar spectral index $n_s$. For $\alpha \equiv 4V_0\xi_0/3 = -1.5\times 10^{-6}$, $\omega = 1/6$, and $\delta = 10^5$, the predicted signal lies within current observational bounds from Planck. The preheating duration $N_{\text{pre}}$ is constrained by inflationary observables, yielding a self-consistent scenario where both CMB and GW data are simultaneously satisfied.

该模型预测了依赖于标量谱指数$n_s$的当前引力波能量密度$\Omega_{\text{GW}} h^2$。当$\alpha \equiv 4V_0\xi_0/3 = -1.5\times 10^{-6}$、$\omega = 1/6$、$\delta = 10^5$时，预测信号位于普朗克当前观测限制范围内。预热持续时间$N_{\text{pre}}$受膨胀可观测量约束，产生了一个自洽的情景，同时满足CMB和引力波数据。

Conclusion: Gravitational wave production during preheating in Gauss-Bonnet inflation with power-law couplings can be compatible with current cosmological observations. By linking preheating dynamics to inflationary parameters through $n_s$, we establish a predictive framework testable by future gravitational wave detectors such as LISA or BBO. The required tuning of $\alpha$ suggests fine structure in the Gauss-Bonnet sector, possibly pointing to deeper theoretical origins in UV-complete theories like string theory.

在具有幂律耦合的高斯-邦内膨胀模型中，预热阶段的引力波产生可以与当前宇宙学观测相容。通过将预热动力学与$n_s$相关的膨胀参数联系起来，我们建立了一个可由未来引力波探测器（如LISA或BBO）检验的预测框架。所需$\alpha$的精细调节暗示了高斯-邦内项的深层结构，可能指向弦论等紫外完备理论中的更深层起源。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the production of gravitational waves during the preheating era. To achieve this purpose, we consider Gauss-Bonnet inflation model with Power{\textendash}law potential, $V(φ)= V_0 φ^n$, and monomial Gauss-Bonnet coupling function, $ξ(φ)= ξ_0 φ^n$. We examine our model by comparing our findings with the current observational data. After that, we study the preheating stage by adopting an approach in which we establish a link between preheating duration, reheating phase and inflationary parameters. This step allows us to benefit from observational constraints imposed on inflation. Furthermore, we examine the production of gravitational waves during preheating epoch connecting the energy density to the preheating duration, $N_{pre}$, and then with the spectral index $n_s$. The generation of gravitational waves during preheating can satisfy observational constraints. In particular, the predicted present-day gravitational-wave energy density, expressed as a function of the scalar spectral index, is consistent with the Planck constraints for the choice of a dimensionless Gauss-Bonnet coupling parameter $α\equiv 4V_{0}ξ_{0}/3 = -1.5\times 10^{-6}$, an effective equation of state parameter $ω= 1/6$, and a preheating efficiency parameter $δ= 10^{5}$.

### [25] [Canonical Uncertainty Relations for Madelung Variables in Curved Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04784)
*Jorge Meza-Domínguez,Tonatiuh Matos*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We derive exact uncertainty relations for hydrodynamic variables in the Madelung formulation of quantum fields in curved spacetime, showing how spacetime geometry influences quantum fluctuations via the lapse $N$ and spatial metric $\gamma_{ij}$.

我们推导了弯曲时空中量子场Madelung表述下流体力学变量的精确不确定性关系，揭示了时空几何（通过lapse函数$N$和空间度规$\gamma_{ij}$）如何影响量子涨落。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The Madelung representation provides a hydrodynamic interpretation of quantum mechanics, but its extension to quantum fields in curved spacetime lacks a complete understanding of inherent quantum uncertainties. We aim to establish first-principles uncertainty relations that incorporate gravitational effects, which are essential for applications in quantum gravity and dark matter models based on scalar fields.

Madelung表象为量子力学提供了流体力学解释，但其在弯曲时空中的量子场推广尚缺乏对内禀量子不确定性的完整理解。我们的目标是建立包含引力效应的第一性原理不确定性关系，这对基于标量场的量子引力和暗物质模型至关重要。

Method: We perform canonical quantization of the density $n$ and phase $\theta$ variables and their conjugate momenta in the Madelung representation of a complex scalar field in curved spacetime. By computing commutation relations derived from the symplectic structure of the theory, we obtain generalized uncertainty principles involving $n$ and $\nabla_i\theta$, with explicit dependence on the spacetime metric through $N$ and $\gamma_{ij}$.

我们在弯曲时空中的复标量场Madelung表象下，对密度$n$和相位$\theta$及其共轭动量进行正则量子化。通过计算由理论辛结构导出的对易关系，我们得到了涉及$n$和$\nabla_i\theta$的广义不确定性原理，并显式依赖于通过$N$和$\gamma_{ij}$体现的时空度规。

Result: We derive exact uncertainty relations of the form $\Delta n \Delta (\nabla_i\theta) \geq \frac{\hbar}{2} |\langle \mathcal{R}_i \rangle|$, where $\mathcal{R}_i$ is a geometric functional depending on $N$, $\gamma_{ij}$, and their derivatives. These show that spacetime curvature suppresses or enhances quantum fluctuations in a state-dependent manner. The results apply to relativistic Bose-Einstein condensates, fuzzy dark matter, and stochastic gravity frameworks.

我们推导出形式为$\Delta n \Delta (\nabla_i\theta) \geq \frac{\hbar}{2} |\langle \mathcal{R}_i \rangle|$的精确不确定性关系，其中$\mathcal{R}_i$是依赖于$N$、$\gamma_{ij}$及其导数的几何泛函。结果表明，时空曲率以依赖于量子态的方式抑制或增强量子涨落。这些结果适用于相对论性玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚、模糊暗物质以及随机引力框架。

Conclusion: Geometric data of spacetime nontrivially modulate quantum hydrodynamic uncertainties, providing new constraints on semiclassical gravity and scalar field dark matter. This work establishes the Cosmological Quantum Hydrodynamics as a rigorous framework for studying quantum fluctuations in gravitational contexts.

时空的几何信息非平凡地调制量子流体力学不确定性，为半经典引力和标量场暗物质模型提供了新的约束。本工作确立了宇宙学量子流体力学作为研究引力背景下量子涨落的严格框架。

Abstract: We establish fundamental uncertainty relations for the hydrodynamic variables arising from the Madelung representation of quantum fields in curved spacetime. Through canonical quantization of the density $n$ and phase $θ$ variables and their conjugate momenta, we derive exact uncertainty principles that depend on spacetime geometry through the lapse function $N$ and spatial metric $γ_{ij}$. These relations reveal how gravitational fields modulate quantum fluctuations and provide first-principles constraints for scalar field dark matter models and stochastic quantum gravity.

</details>


### [26] [The formation of a weak null singularity in the interior of generic rotating black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04877)
*Jonathan Luk,Jan Sbierski*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We prove the formation of a weak null singularity across a dynamical event horizon that settles to Kerr, where the metric is $C^0$-extendible but not Lipschitz; the proof relies on stability of the Teukolsky equation and its linear instability.

我们证明了在趋向于Kerr时空的动力学事件视界上会形成弱零奇点，此时度规是$C^0$可延拓但非Lipschitz可延拓的；证明的核心是Teukolsky方程的稳定性及其线性不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the nature of singularities inside black holes, particularly whether they are strong or weak, is central to the strong cosmic censorship conjecture. The transition from a dynamical to a stationary (Kerr) horizon provides a physically relevant setting to test this.

理解黑洞内部奇点的本质，特别是其强或弱的性质，是强宇宙监督猜想的核心问题。从动力学到定常态（Kerr）视界的过渡为检验这一猜想提供了物理上相关的场景。

Method: The analysis is based on the characteristic initial value problem with smooth data. The key step is establishing a stability result for the dynamical Teukolsky equation, showing that its solutions can be approximated by linearized ones, which were previously shown to exhibit linear instability near the Cauchy horizon.

该分析基于具有光滑数据的特征初值问题。关键步骤是建立动力学Teukolsky方程的稳定性结果，表明其解可由线性化解逼近，而后者在之前工作中已被证明在Cauchy视界附近存在线性不稳定性。

Result: It is proven that a weak null singularity forms at the Cauchy horizon, where the spacetime metric remains $C^0$-continuous but fails to be Lipschitz continuous. This implies inextendibility of the Christoffel symbols in $L^2_{\rm loc}$, signaling a curvature singularity detectable by infalling observers.

证明了在Cauchy视界处会形成弱零奇点，此时时空度规保持$C^0$连续但不再满足Lipschitz连续。这意味着Christoffel符号在$L^2_{\rm loc}$中不可延拓，表明下落观测者可探测到曲率奇点。

Conclusion: The results support the physical picture that generic black hole interiors develop weak null singularities rather than spacelike ones, favoring a weaker form of cosmic censorship. The instability of the Teukolsky field plays a crucial role in the breakdown of predictability inside black holes.

该结果支持了普遍黑洞内部发展出弱零奇点而非类空奇点的物理图像，倾向于较弱形式的宇宙监督。Teukolsky场的不稳定性在黑洞内部可预测性的破坏中起着关键作用。

Abstract: Given a characteristic initial value problem with smooth data representing a dynamical event horizon settling down to that of Kerr in the subextremal, strictly rotating range with suitable upper and lower bounds, we prove that a weak null singularity forms, across which the spacetime metric is continuously extendible but not Lipschitz extendible. The bulk of the proof is a stability argument showing that a dynamical Teukolsky field can be approximated by a linear Teukolsky field, whose linear instability was proved in previous works.

</details>

### [27] [Big Bang Nucleosynthesis Constraints on the CCC+TL Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03381)
*Rajendra P. Gupta,Nikolaos Samaras*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper examines the compatibility of Big Bang nucleosynthesis (BBN) with the Covarying Coupling Constants plus Tired Light (CCC+TL) cosmology, finding that BBN predictions remain invariant under a universal scaling $f_{\text{max}} \simeq 3$ of dimensionful quantities at high redshift, provided interaction and decay rates scale proportionally with the Hubble rate $H$, preserving key dimensionless combinations like $\Gamma/H$ and $\exp(-\Delta t / \tau_n)$. Numerical implementation using the Kawano/NUC123 code confirms light-element abundances are unchanged within numerical precision when $\texttt{fctl} = f_{\text{max}}$ is varied from 1 ($\Lambda$CDM) to 3 (CCC+TL).

本文研究了大爆炸核合成（BBN）与协变耦合常数加疲劳光（CCC+TL）宇宙学的兼容性。发现在高红移下，若所有有量纲量通过普适标度函数 $f_{\text{max}} \simeq 3$ 进行协变，且相互作用率和中子寿命衰减速率与哈勃速率 $H$ 以相同比例缩放，则关键无量纲组合如 $\Gamma/H$ 和 $\exp(-\Delta t / \tau_n)$ 保持不变，从而维持BBN预测。利用Kawano/NUC123网络进行数值实现，当控制参数 $\texttt{fctl} = f_{\text{max}}$ 从1（$\Lambda$CDM）变为3（CCC+TL）时，轻元素丰度在数值精度内保持不变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To test whether the CCC+TL cosmological model, which proposes covariation of dimensional constants and tired-light redshift, can remain consistent with the well-constrained physics of Big Bang nucleosynthesis (BBN), particularly the observed light-element abundances. This addresses a critical early-universe consistency check for alternative cosmologies that modify expansion dynamics or fundamental constants.

检验CCC+TL宇宙学模型——该模型提出有量纲常数的协变性和疲劳光红移机制——是否仍能与大爆炸核合成（BBN）这一被精确约束的物理过程相容，特别是观测到的轻元素丰度。这是对修改了膨胀动力学或基本常数的替代理论在早期宇宙阶段自洽性的关键检验。

Method: The authors analyze the scaling behavior of physical quantities in CCC+TL cosmology during BBN, identifying that only dimensionful quantities scale via a universal function $f(z)$, with $f(z) \to f_{\text{max}} \simeq 3$ at BBN redshifts. They derive how the Hubble parameter $H(T)$, neutron lifetime $\tau_n$, and interaction rates $\Gamma$ transform under this scaling, showing that if all scale as $f_{\text{max}}^{-1}$, then dimensionless ratios governing BBN (e.g., $\Gamma/H$, $\Delta t / \tau_n$) remain invariant. These scalings are implemented numerically in the Kawano/NUC123 BBN code by introducing a control parameter $\texttt{fctl} = f_{\text{max}}$, and light-element abundances are computed for $\texttt{fctl} = 1$ ($\Lambda$CDM) and $\texttt{fctl} = 3$ (CCC+TL).

作者分析了CCC+TL宇宙学在BBN时期的物理量标度行为，指出仅具有长度量纲的量通过普适函数 $f(z)$ 缩放，在BBN红移处 $f(z) \to f_{\text{max}} \simeq 3$。推导了哈勃参数 $H(T)$、中子寿命 $\tau_n$ 和相互作用率 $\Gamma$ 在此标度下的变换方式，表明若它们均按 $f_{\text{max}}^{-1}$ 缩放，则控制BBN的关键无量纲比值（如 $\Gamma/H$、$\Delta t / \tau_n$）保持不变。通过引入控制参数 $\texttt{fctl} = f_{\text{max}}$，在Kawano/NUC123 BBN代码中数值实现了这些标度，并计算了 $\texttt{fctl} = 1$（$\Lambda$CDM）和 $\texttt{fctl} = 3$（CCC+TL）下的轻元素丰度。

Result: The numerical BBN calculations show that light-element abundances (D, $^4$He, $^7$Li) are identical between $\texttt{fctl} = 1$ and $\texttt{fctl} = 3$ to within $10^{-3} - 10^{-4}$, consistent with numerical rounding errors, confirming theoretical invariance. The study also shows that adopting a lower baryon density $\omega_b$ inferred from late-time Pantheon+ fits in CCC+TL reduces the $^7$Li problem but increases D/H, indicating a trade-off and that BBN alone cannot distinguish between different late-time $\omega_b$ inferences.

数值BBN计算显示，当 $\texttt{fctl} = 1$ 与 $\texttt{fctl} = 3$ 时，轻元素丰度（D, $^4$He, $^7$Li）在 $10^{-3} - 10^{-4}$ 精度内一致，符合数值舍入误差水平，验证了理论上的不变性。研究还表明，在CCC+TL中采用来自晚期Pantheon+数据拟合得到的较低重子密度 $\omega_b$ 可缓解 $^7$Li问题，但会同时升高D/H比值，显示出权衡关系，且BBN本身无法区分不同的晚期 $\omega_b$ 推断值。

Conclusion: Big Bang nucleosynthesis is compatible with the CCC+TL cosmology under the assumption that all relevant dimensionful quantities (including $H$, $\Gamma$, and $\tau_n$) scale uniformly by $f_{\text{max}}^{-1} \simeq 1/3$ during BBN, preserving dimensionless physics. This demonstrates that non-standard cosmologies modifying dimensional constants can still satisfy early-universe constraints if they respect the invariance of dimensionless observables. However, the choice of late-time baryon density affects elemental abundance tensions differently, suggesting that joint early- and late-universe analyses are needed to test such models.

如果所有相关有量纲量（包括 $H$、$\Gamma$ 和 $\tau_n$）在BBN期间统一按 $f_{\text{max}}^{-1} \simeq 1/3$ 缩放，从而保持无量纲物理量不变，则大爆炸核合成与CCC+TL宇宙学是相容的。这表明，即使修改了有量纲常数的非标准宇宙学，只要保持无量纲观测量的不变性，仍可满足早期宇宙的约束。然而，晚期重子密度的选择会以不同方式影响元素丰度的张力，表明需要联合早期与晚期宇宙的数据分析来检验此类模型。

Abstract: We investigate whether Big Bang nucleosynthesis (BBN) remains compatible with the Covarying Coupling Constants plus Tired Light (CCC+TL) cosmology. In this framework, only quantities with explicit length dimensionality covary through a universal scaling function $f \left( z \right)$, while dimensionless constants and dimensionless ratios remain invariant. At the redshifts $z$ relevant to BBN, $f \left( z \right )$ approaches a constant plateau $f_{\text{max}} \left( z \right) \simeq 3$, and the tired-light contribution is negligible, so the early-time dynamics reduce to a global rescaling of dimensioned quantities. In particular, the Hubble expansion rate $H$ at fixed temperature $T$ satisfies $H_{\text{CTL}} \left( T \right) = f^{-1}_{\text{max}} H_{Λ\text{CDM}}\left( T\right)$, implying a longer cooling time $Δt$ between weak freeze-out and the onset of nucleosynthesis by the same factor (CCC+TL labeled as $\textit{CTL}$). We find that BBN predictions are preserved provided the relevant interaction rates $Γ$ and decay rates governing the neutron lifetime $τ_n$ share the same plateau scaling as $H$, so that governing combinations such as $Γ\text{/}H$ and $\text{exp} \left( -Δt \text{/} τ_n \right)$ remain invariant. Implementing these plateau rescalings in the Kawano/NUC123 network (via a single control parameter $\texttt{fctl} \equiv f_{\text{max}}$) yields identical light-element abundances for $\texttt{fctl}= 1$ ($Λ$CDM) and $\texttt{fctl} = 3\left( \text{CCC+TL} \right)$ to within $10^{-3} - 10^{-4}$ level, consistent with numerical rounding. We also illustrate that adopting the lower late-time CCC+TL baryon density from the Pantheon+ data fit can reduce the ${}^7\text{Li}$ discrepancy but simultaneously increases D/H, implying that BBN alone does not select between the late-time baryon-density inferences considered here.

</details>


### [28] [Lattice simulations of scalar-induced gravitational waves from inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03628)
*Angelo Caravano,Gabriele Franciolini,Sébastien Renaux-Petel*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This work computes scalar-induced gravitational waves (SIGWs) from ultra-slow-roll (USR) inflation using lattice simulations, going beyond linear perturbation theory by fully nonlinear evolution of the inflaton field. The study shows that semi-analytical methods, which assume linear scalar dynamics, can fail dramatically in predicting SIGW amplitude and spectral shape when inflationary non-Gaussianities are large, despite matching the correct order of magnitude for moderate cases. Reliable predictions require nonperturbative treatment of scalar fluctuations during inflation.

本文通过格点模拟计算了超慢滚（USR）暴胀产生的标量诱导引力波（SIGW），突破了线性微扰理论的限制，对暴胀期间的标量场进行了完全非线性的演化。研究发现，当暴胀非高斯性较小时，半解析方法虽能估计SIGW信号的量级，但仍存在显著偏差；而当非高斯性较大时，该方法在振幅和谱形上均会严重失效，且与张量功率谱大小无关。结果表明，在此类情景中，必须采用非微扰方法精确处理暴胀标量动力学以获得可靠预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Scalar-induced gravitational waves (SIGWs) are a key probe of small-scale physics during inflation, particularly in models with enhanced curvature perturbations such as those featuring an ultra-slow-roll (USR) phase. However, in such scenarios, the assumption of linear scalar field evolution breaks down due to strong amplification of fluctuations, leading to significant non-Gaussianity. Standard semi-analytical calculations of SIGWs rely on linear perturbation theory and may not capture the true dynamics when nonlinear effects dominate. This raises the question of their validity and calls for a nonperturbative approach to accurately compute SIGWs in strongly nonlinear regimes.

标量诱导引力波（SIGW）是探测暴胀时期小尺度物理的关键工具，尤其适用于曲率扰动被显著放大的模型（如存在超慢滚（USR）阶段的情况）。然而在此类情形下，由于涨落强烈放大，标量场的线性演化假设不再成立，导致显著的非高斯性。现有的SIGW半解析计算依赖于线性微扰理论，在非线性效应主导时可能无法捕捉真实动力学行为。因此，这些方法的有效性受到质疑，亟需一种非微扰方法来准确计算强非线性区域中的SIGW。

Method: We perform full nonlinear lattice simulations of inflation under the ultra-slow-roll (USR) regime, evolving the inflaton field self-consistently with gravity using numerical relativity techniques. From these simulations, we extract the curvature perturbation $\zeta$ nonperturbatively, preserving its full statistical structure including non-Gaussianities. After reheating, we model the re-entry of super-horizon modes into the horizon by linearly evolving the Newtonian potential $\Phi$, while using the numerically generated primordial fluctuations as initial conditions for the tensor source term $S_{ij} = \partial_i \Phi \partial_j \Phi + \cdots$. The induced tensor power spectrum $P_h(k)$ is then computed from the sourced GWs, allowing us to compare with semi-analytical predictions based on linear scalar evolution.

我们在超慢滚（USR）暴胀框架下进行完全非线性的格点模拟，使用数值相对论技术自洽地演化暴胀子场及其引力相互作用。从中非微扰地提取曲率扰动$\zeta$，完整保留其统计结构（包括非高斯性）。暴胀结束后，我们通过线性演化牛顿势$\Phi$模拟超视界模式的再入过程，同时将数值生成的原初扰动作为张量源项$S_{ij} = \partial_i \Phi \partial_j \Phi + \cdots$的初始条件。由此计算出诱导张量功率谱$P_h(k)$，并与基于线性标量演化的半解析预测进行对比。

Result: For moderate levels of non-Gaussianity, semi-analytical calculations reproduce the correct order of magnitude of the SIGW signal but exhibit noticeable deviations in both amplitude and spectral shape. In cases with large non-Gaussianity—arising from strong nonlinear scalar dynamics during USR inflation—the semi-analytical approach fails dramatically: it incorrectly predicts the peak location, overestimates or underestimates the amplitude by up to an order of magnitude, and distorts the spectral tilt. These discrepancies persist even when the total scalar power is fixed, indicating that the failure is intrinsic to the breakdown of linear scalar evolution. Our lattice results demonstrate that nonperturbative control of inflationary dynamics is essential for accurate SIGW predictions.

在中等非高斯性情况下，半解析计算虽能复现SIGW信号的量级，但在振幅和谱形上仍表现出明显偏差。而在非高斯性较强的情形——源于USR暴胀期间强烈的非线性标量动力学——半解析方法严重失效：错误预测峰值位置，振幅可能被高估或低估达一个数量级，并扭曲谱倾斜程度。这些差异即使在总标量功率固定的情况下依然存在，表明其根源在于线性标量演化假设的崩溃。我们的格点模拟结果表明，要实现对SIGW的精确预测，必须非微扰地控制暴胀动力学。

Conclusion: Reliable predictions of scalar-induced gravitational waves in models with enhanced small-scale power, such as ultra-slow-roll inflation, require nonperturbative treatment of scalar fluctuations due to the breakdown of linear perturbation theory. Lattice simulations provide a robust framework for capturing the full nonlinear dynamics of inflation and the resulting non-Gaussian initial conditions. Semi-analytical methods, while useful for order-of-magnitude estimates in weakly nonlinear regimes, fail qualitatively in strongly nonlinear scenarios and cannot be trusted for precision cosmology or observational forecasts. Future studies of SIGWs should incorporate nonperturbative scalar dynamics for accurate modeling.

在具有增强小尺度功率的模型（如超慢滚暴胀）中，由于线性微扰理论失效，对标量诱导引力波的可靠预测必须采用非微扰方法处理标量涨落。格点模拟为捕捉暴胀全过程的非线性动力学及由此产生的非高斯初始条件提供了稳健框架。半解析方法尽管在弱非线性区域可用于量级估算，但在强非线性情形下会出现定性错误，无法用于精确宇宙学或观测预测。未来对SIGW的研究应纳入非微扰的标量动力学以实现精确建模。

Abstract: Scalar-induced gravitational waves (SIGWs) provide a powerful probe of inflationary dynamics on scales far smaller than those accessible to the cosmic microwave background and large-scale structure. In scenarios with a transient ultra-slow-roll (USR) phase, the curvature power spectrum can be strongly enhanced on small scales, potentially generating an observable stochastic GW background. In this regime, scalar dynamics during inflation can become nonlinear, challenging the validity of standard perturbative predictions. Existing semi-analytical calculations of SIGWs rely on the linear evolution of inflation fluctuations. In this work, we compute SIGWs from USR inflation using lattice simulations. We evolve the inflaton field fully nonlinearly during inflation and extract the curvature perturbation nonperturbatively, then simulate its post-reheating horizon re-entry by evolving the Newtonian potential linearly while retaining the full non-Gaussian structure of the initial conditions for the primordial fluctuations in the tensor source. For moderate non-Gaussianity, the semi-analytical prediction captures the correct order of magnitude of the GW signal but receives important corrections. When inflationary non-Gaussianities are large, it can fail dramatically in both amplitude and spectral shape, independently of the overall size of the tensor power spectrum. Our results show that reliable predictions of SIGWs in such scenarios require nonperturbative control of the inflationary scalar dynamics. The code used for this work is available at https://github.com/caravangelo/inflation-easy.git.

</details>


### [29] [Is the $w_0w_a$CDM cosmological parameterization evidence for dark energy dynamics partially caused by the excess smoothing of Planck PR4 CMB anisotropy data?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03756)
*Chan-Gyung Park,Javier de Cruz Perez,Bharat Ratra*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The study evaluates the flat $\Lambda$CDM, $w_0$CDM, and $w_0w_a$CDM models using Planck PR3/PR4 CMB data and non-CMB datasets, finding mild ($1.5\text{--}1.8\sigma$) preference for dynamical dark energy (DE), with reduced CMB lensing anomaly ($A_L$) in PR4 compared to PR3.

该研究利用Planck PR3/PR4 CMB数据和非CMB数据集评估了平坦$\Lambda$CDM、$w_0$CDM和$w_0w_a$CDM模型，发现对动力学暗能量（DE）有轻微（$1.5\text{--}1.8\sigma$）偏好，并且PR4中的CMB透镜异常（$A_L$）相比PR3有所减弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To assess whether current cosmological data favor a cosmological constant ($\Lambda$) or dynamical dark energy, and to examine the stability of constraints between Planck PR3 and PR4 data releases, particularly in light of the CMB lensing anomaly characterized by the parameter $A_L$.

为了评估当前宇宙学数据是否更倾向于宇宙学常数（$\Lambda$）还是动力学暗能量，并检验Planck PR3与PR4数据发布之间限制的稳定性，特别是考虑到由参数$A_L$表征的CMB透镜异常。

Method: Bayesian inference is used to constrain cosmological parameters in the $\Lambda$CDM, $w_0$CDM, and $w_0w_a$CDM models, with and without the inclusion of the CMB lensing parameter $A_L$. Data combinations include Planck PR3 and PR4 (including temperature, polarization, and lensing reconstruction), along with non-CMB probes: BAO (excluding DESI), Pantheon+ SNe Ia, $H(z)$, and $f\sigma_8$ measurements.

使用贝叶斯推断在$\Lambda$CDM、$w_0$CDM和$w_0w_a$CDM模型中限制宇宙学参数，包括或不包括CMB透镜参数$A_L$。数据组合包括Planck PR3和PR4（包含温度、偏振和透镜重建），以及非CMB探针：BAO（不含DESI）、Pantheon+ Ia型超新星、$H(z)$和$f\sigma_8$测量。

Result: For $\Lambda$CDM$+A_L$, $A_L = 1.087 \pm 0.035$ (PR3) and $A_L = 1.053 \pm 0.034$ (PR4), indicating a reduced lensing anomaly in PR4. In $w_0w_a$CDM, $w_0 = -0.863\pm0.060$, $w_0 + w_a = -1.37^{+0.19}_{-0.17}$ ($\sim 1.8\sigma$ preference for dynamical DE). With $A_L$, $w_0 = -0.877\pm0.060$, $w_0 + w_a = -1.29_{-0.17}^{+0.20}$, $A_L = 1.042 \pm 0.037$ ($\sim 1.5\sigma$ preference for dynamical DE). Constraints from PR3 and PR4 are consistent within $1\sigma$ for most parameters.

对于$\Lambda$CDM$+A_L$模型，$A_L = 1.087 \pm 0.035$（PR3）和$A_L = 1.053 \pm 0.034$（PR4），表明PR4中透镜异常减弱。在$w_0w_a$CDM中，$w_0 = -0.863\pm0.060$，$w_0 + w_a = -1.37^{+0.19}_{-0.17}$（对动力学DE约$1.8\sigma$偏好）。包含$A_L$时，$w_0 = -0.877\pm0.060$，$w_0 + w_a = -1.29_{-0.17}^{+0.20}$，$A_L = 1.042 \pm 0.037$（对动力学DE约$1.5\sigma$偏好）。PR3与PR4的限制在大多数参数上均在$1\sigma$内一致。

Conclusion: Current data show a mild ($1.5\text{--}1.8\sigma$) preference for dynamical dark energy over $\Lambda$CDM, though this may be partially driven by residual systematics in the Planck PR4 CMB spectra, such as excess smoothing. The CMB lensing anomaly ($A_L > 1$) persists but is less pronounced in PR4 than in PR3, suggesting improved data consistency.

当前数据显示出对动力学暗能量相对于$\Lambda$CDM的轻微（$1.5\text{--}1.8\sigma$）偏好，但这可能部分源于Planck PR4 CMB谱中残留的系统效应，例如过度平滑。CMB透镜异常（$A_L > 1$）仍然存在，但在PR4中比PR3中更弱，表明数据一致性有所改善。

Abstract: We study the performance of the flat $Λ$CDM model and the dynamical dark energy parameterizations $w_0$CDM and $w_0w_a$CDM, in which the dark energy (DE) equation of state is either constant ($w=w_0$) or redshift-dependent [$w(z)=w_0+w_a z/(1+z)$], without and with a varying CMB lensing consistency parameter $A_L$, using combinations of Planck PR4 CMB data (PR4 and lensing), and a compilation of non-CMB data composed of baryon acoustic oscillation (BAO) data that do not include DESI BAO data, Pantheon+ type Ia supernova observations, Hubble parameter measurements $H(z)$, and growth rate $fσ_8$ data. We also compare results from earlier Planck PR3 data with those obtained using PR4 data in order to assess the stability of cosmological constraints. For the largest data combinations, PR3/PR4+lensing+non-CMB, the cosmological parameters inferred from PR3 and PR4 data are consistent, almost all differing by $1σ$ or less. For the $Λ$CDM$+A_L$ model, we have $A_L=1.087 \pm 0.035$ for PR3 and $A_L=1.053 \pm 0.034$ ($1.6σ$ above unity) for PR4, which indicates that the CMB lensing anomaly is reduced when PR4 data are used. For the $w_0 w_a$CDM parameterization, we find $w_0 = -0.863\pm0.060$ (quintessence-like) and $w_0+w_a=-1.37^{+0.19}_{-0.17}$ (phantom-like), suggesting that the current observations favor dynamical DE over a cosmological constant at about $1.8σ$. For the $w_0w_a$CDM$+A_L$ parameterization, we find $w_0=-0.877\pm 0.060$ and $w_0 + w_a =-1.29_{-0.17}^{+0.20}$, corresponding to a preference for dynamical DE over a cosmological constant of about $1.5σ$ and with $A_L = 1.042 \pm 0.037$ exceeding unity at $1.1σ$. These results indicate that while the PR4 data mildly favor a time-evolving DE, part of this preference may be associated with possible residual excess smoothing present in the Planck PR4 CMB anisotropy spectra (abridged).

</details>


### [30] [Dispersion Measure Distribution of Unlocalized Fast Radio Bursts as a Probe of the Hubble Constant](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03769)
*Yang Liu,Jun-Jie Wei,Puxun Wu,Xue-Feng Wu*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We present the first measurement of the Hubble constant $H_0$ using only the dispersion measure (DM) distribution of 2124 unlocalized fast radio bursts (FRBs) from CHIME Catalog II, yielding $H_0 = 73.8^{+14.0}_{-12.3}~\mathrm{km\,s^{-1}\,Mpc^{-1}}$ at 1σ, with potential to reach ~9% precision by breaking degeneracy with the FRB energy cutoff $E_*$. This demonstrates unlocalized FRBs as a novel cosmological probe.

我们首次仅利用来自CHIME第二目录的2124个未定位快速射电暴（FRB）的色散量（DM）分布测量哈勃常数$H_0$，得到$H_0 = 73.8^{+14.0}_{-12.3}~\mathrm{km\,s^{-1}\,Mpc^{-1}}$（1σ），通过打破与FRB各向同性能量分布特征截止能量$E_*$的简并，精度有望提升至约9%。该工作展示了未定位FRB作为一种新型宇宙学探针的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The Hubble tension — the discrepancy between early- and late-universe measurements of $H_0$ — remains unresolved. Localized FRBs with redshifts have been used as cosmological probes, but their sample size is small. Unlocalized FRBs are far more numerous and offer a statistically powerful alternative, provided their DM distribution can be modeled to extract cosmological information without redshift assignments.

哈勃张力——早期与晚期宇宙对$H_0$测量之间的差异——仍未解决。已定位且具有红移信息的FRB已被用作宇宙学探针，但样本量较小。未定位FRB数量多得多，若能通过建模其DM分布以提取宇宙学信息而无需红移，则可提供统计上更强大的替代方案。

Method: We model the probability distribution of the observed DM of unlocalized FRBs as a function of cosmological parameters, particularly $H_0$, incorporating contributions from the intergalactic medium (IGM), host galaxies, and Milky Way foreground. The FRB energy distribution is modeled as a power law with an exponential cutoff at $E_*$. Using Bayesian inference on a sample of 2124 unlocalized FRBs from CHIME Catalog II, we infer $H_0$ marginalizing over astrophysical nuisance parameters including $E_*$.

我们将未定位FRB观测到的DM概率分布建模为宇宙学参数（特别是$H_0$）的函数，包含来自星系际介质（IGM）、宿主星系和银河系前景的贡献。FRB能量分布被建模为具有指数截止$E_*$的幂律形式。通过对CHIME第二目录中2124个未定位FRB样本进行贝叶斯推断，我们在包括$E_*$在内的天体物理噪声参数上进行边缘化，从而推断$H_0$。

Result: From the DM distribution alone, we obtain $H_0 = 73.8^{+14.0}_{-12.3}~\mathrm{km\,s^{-1}\,Mpc^{-1}}$ at 1σ confidence, consistent with local Universe determinations (e.g., SH0ES). The uncertainty is currently dominated by degeneracy between $H_0$ and $E_*$. Breaking this degeneracy — e.g., via joint analysis with localized FRBs — could reduce the uncertainty to ~9%.

仅从DM分布出发，我们得到$H_0 = 73.8^{+14.0}_{-12.3}~\mathrm{km\,s^{-1}\,Mpc^{-1}}$（1σ），与局域宇宙测量结果（如SH0ES）一致。当前不确定性主要来源于$H_0$与$E_*$之间的简并。打破这一简并——例如通过与已定位FRB联合分析——可将不确定性降低至约9%。

Conclusion: This work presents the first $H_0$ constraint derived solely from the DM distribution of unlocalized FRBs, demonstrating their viability as a new cosmological probe. The method leverages cosmic expansion's imprint on the DM distribution, independent of redshift. With increasing FRB statistics and improved modeling of astrophysical populations, this approach will become increasingly competitive in resolving the Hubble tension.

本工作首次仅基于未定位FRB的DM分布得出$H_0$约束，证明了其作为新型宇宙学探针的可行性。该方法利用宇宙膨胀在DM分布上的印记，不依赖于红移信息。随着FRB统计数据的增加和天体物理群体建模的改进，该方法将在解决哈勃张力问题上变得越来越有竞争力。

Abstract: We present constraints on the Hubble constant ($H_0$) derived from the observed dispersion measure (DM) distribution of unlocalized fast radio bursts (FRBs). While localized FRBs with redshift measurements have been used to investigate the Hubble tension, their sample remains limited. Here we demonstrate that unlocalized FRBs -- which are far more numerous -- can independently constrain $H_0$ without requiring redshift information, as cosmic expansion imprints itself on their DM distribution. Analyzing a selected sample of 2124 unlocalized FRBs from the CHIME Catalog II, we obtain $H_0 = 73.8^{+14.0}_{-12.3}~\mathrm{km\,s^{-1}\,Mpc^{-1}}$ at the $1σ$ confidence level, corresponding to an uncertainty of about 18%. Breaking the degeneracy between $H_0$ and the characteristic cutoff energy $E_*$ of the FRB isotropic energy distribution would reduce this uncertainty to 9%. This work constitutes the first $H_0$ measurement derived solely from the DM distribution of unlocalized FRBs, highlighting their potential as a new cosmological probe. Future joint analyses with localized FRBs promise even tighter constraints.

### [31] [Beyond $f(φ)\mathcal{G}$: Gauss--Bonnet inflation with $μ(φ,X)$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03828)
*Ali Seidabadi,Sara Saghafi,Kourosh Nozari*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper proposes a trajectory-selective coupling $\mu(\phi,X)$ to localize Gauss--Bonnet corrections in inflation, enabling controlled imprints on CMB-scale observables while maintaining stability.

本文提出一种轨迹选择性耦合 $\mu(\phi,X)$ 来局域化高斯-博内特修正项在暴胀过程中的作用，从而在保持稳定性的同时，实现对CMB尺度观测量的可控影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Gauss--Bonnet inflation typically modifies dynamics over a broad range of e-folds, making it challenging to produce a distinct and controlled signature at CMB scales. The motivation is to isolate higher-curvature effects within a finite e-fold window to enable clearer observational predictions.

高斯-博内特暴胀通常会在大量e折阶段改变动力学，使得在CMB尺度上产生清晰且可控的信号变得困难。本文动机是将高曲率效应限制在有限的e折窗口内，以实现更明确的观测预测。

Method: The authors introduce a phase-space gating function $\mu(\phi,X)$ that activates the Gauss--Bonnet sector only during a specific inflationary trajectory segment. They derive stable inflationary backgrounds, enforce ghost and gradient stability conditions for scalar and tensor perturbations, and compute pivot-scale observables (e.g., $n_s$, $r$) as functions of Gauss--Bonnet coupling strength and kinetic gating parameters.

作者引入一个相空间门控函数 $\mu(\phi,X)$，仅在暴胀轨迹的特定段激活高斯-博内特项。他们推导了稳定的暴胀背景，施加了标量和张量扰动的鬼态与梯度稳定性条件，并计算了枢纽尺度观测量（如 $n_s$, $r$），将其表示为高斯-博内特耦合强度和动能门控参数的函数。

Result: Stable inflationary solutions are found where Gauss--Bonnet effects are localized in e-folds. The spectral index $n_s$ and tensor-to-scalar ratio $r$ depend measurably on the coupling strength and kinetic gating, allowing for distinguishable signatures in CMB data. The model remains free of ghosts and gradient instabilities.

发现了高斯-博内特效应在e折阶段局域化的稳定暴胀解。谱指数 $n_s$ 和张量标量比 $r$ 明显依赖于耦合强度和动能门控，从而可在CMB数据中产生可区分的信号。该模型无鬼场且无梯度不稳定性。

Conclusion: Trajectory-selective coupling via $\mu(\phi,X)$ provides a controlled mechanism to localize higher-curvature corrections in inflation, offering testable predictions for CMB observables within a stable theoretical framework.

通过 $\mu(\phi,X)$ 的轨迹选择性耦合为局域化暴胀中的高曲率修正提供了一种可控机制，在稳定理论框架内为CMB观测量提供了可检验的预测。

Abstract: Gauss--Bonnet inflation typically affects the dynamics over an extended portion of the trajectory, making it difficult to isolate a controlled imprint at CMB scales. We consider a trajectory-selective coupling \(μ(φ,X)\) that gates the Gauss--Bonnet sector in phase space, enabling the higher-curvature contribution to be localized within a finite e-fold window while remaining negligible elsewhere. We identify stable inflationary solutions consistent with this localization and enforce standard ghost and gradient stability conditions for both scalar and tensor perturbations. For these viable backgrounds we compute pivot-scale observables and examine their dependence on the overall Gauss--Bonnet strength and on the kinetic gating. The framework offers a controlled route for realizing localized higher-curvature effects with predictable consequences for CMB-scale measurements.

### [32] [Intracluster Light as a Probe for Dark Matter: Exploring SIDM and CDM with C-EAGLE Sims](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03907)
*Jaewon Yoo,Ellen L. Sirks,Cristiano G. Sabiu,Changbom Park,Jaehyun Lee,Ankit Singh,Juhan Kim,Jongwan Ko*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The study investigates whether intracluster light (ICL) can be used to distinguish between cold dark matter (CDM) and self-interacting dark matter (SIDM) models in galaxy clusters, using the Cluster-EAGLE simulations. It finds that the brightest cluster galaxy plus ICL (BCG+ICL) is the best tracer of dark matter distribution, with gas becoming increasingly aligned over time, especially in SIDM where dark matter behaves more like collisional gas due to self-interactions.

该研究利用Cluster-EAGLE模拟探究星系团内光（ICL）是否可用于区分冷暗物质（CDM）和自相互作用暗物质（SIDM）模型。研究发现最亮星系团星系加ICL（BCG+ICL）是暗物质分布的最佳示踪体，而气体随时间推移逐渐与暗物质对齐，尤其在SIDM中因暗物质具有有效碰撞性而更类似气体行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Small-scale tensions between CDM predictions and observations (e.g., core-cusp problem, too-big-to-fail problem) have motivated alternative dark matter models like SIDM, which predicts different tidal and dynamical evolution in dense environments such as galaxy clusters. Observational discriminators are needed to test these models, and ICL—being a diffuse stellar component shaped by tidal stripping—may encode information about the underlying dark matter dynamics.

CDM预测与观测之间的小尺度矛盾（如核-尖问题、太大而无法失败问题）促使了SIDM等替代暗物质模型的发展，SIDM预言了星系团等高密度环境中的不同潮汐和动力学演化。需要观测判据来检验这些模型，而由潮汐剥离形成的弥散恒星成分ICL可能记录了底层暗物质动力学的信息。

Method: The authors use re-simulations of the Cluster-EAGLE suite, running identical initial conditions under both CDM and SIDM cosmologies. They quantify the morphological similarity between dark matter and baryonic components (gas, all stars, galaxies, BCG+ICL) using the Weighted Overlap Coefficient—a statistic based on contour overlap in 2D surface density maps. Redshift evolution is analyzed from $z = 2$ to $z = 0$, and comparisons are made between dark matter tracers in both models.

作者使用Cluster-EAGLE模拟套件的重模拟，在相同初始条件下运行CDM和SIDM宇宙学模型。他们采用加权重叠系数（Weighted Overlap Coefficient）——基于二维面密度图中等值线重叠的统计量——量化暗物质与重子成分（气体、所有恒星、星系、BCG+ICL）之间的形态相似性，并分析从$z = 2$到$z = 0$的红移演化，比较两种模型中暗物质示踪体的表现。

Result: BCG+ICL is the most accurate tracer of dark matter in both CDM and SIDM, followed by gas, all stars, and galaxies. Gas traces dark matter poorly at high redshift but improves over time, approaching BCG+ICL performance by $z = 0$. In SIDM, gas aligns more closely with dark matter than in CDM due to dark matter's effective collisionality from self-interactions. Dwarf and satellite galaxies show greater sensitivity to the dark matter model despite lower overall tracing accuracy.

在CDM和SIDM中，BCG+ICL都是最准确的暗物质示踪体，其次为气体、所有恒星和星系。气体在高红移时对暗物质的追踪较差，但随时间改善，在$z = 0$时接近BCG+ICL的表现。在SIDM中，由于暗物质自相互作用带来的有效碰撞性，气体与暗物质的对齐程度高于CDM。矮星系和卫星星系尽管整体追踪精度较低，但对暗物质模型更为敏感。

Conclusion: Intracluster light, particularly when combined with the BCG, provides a powerful observational probe of dark matter physics. The differing behavior of gas and stellar components in CDM vs. SIDM reflects the underlying microphysical properties of dark matter. This work establishes ICL as a promising tool for testing dark matter models using current and future deep imaging surveys.

星系团内光（尤其是与最亮星系团星系结合时）为探测暗物质物理提供了强大的观测手段。气体与恒星成分在CDM与SIDM中的不同行为反映了暗物质的底层微观物理特性。本研究确立了ICL作为利用当前及未来深度成像巡天检验暗物质模型的有力工具。

Abstract: We assess whether intracluster light (ICL) can serve as an observational discriminator of dark matter physics. The self-interacting dark matter (SIDM) model has gained increasing attention as a possible resolution to small-scale discrepancies between collisionless cold dark matter (CDM) simulations and observations, predicting distinct tidal interaction histories within galaxy clusters. We analyze Cluster-EAGLE zoom-in galaxy clusters re-simulated from identical initial conditions in both CDM and SIDM frameworks. The morphological similarity between dark matter and multiple baryonic tracers -- gas, all stars, galaxies, and the combined brightest cluster galaxy plus ICL (BCG+ICL) -- is quantified using the Weighted Overlap Coefficient, a contour-overlap statistic.
  We find that dark matter is traced most accurately by BCG+ICL, followed by gas, all stars, and galaxies. The BCG+ICL component remains a robust tracer even at high redshift, while gas initially traces dark matter poorly but improves over time, eventually approaching the performance of BCG+ICL. Notably, in the SIDM case the gas distribution more closely resembles dark matter than in CDM. This reflects the underlying physics: in CDM, collisionless dark matter behaves similarly to the collisionless BCG+ICL, whereas in SIDM, self-interactions introduce an effective collisionality, making dark matter evolve more like the gas component. We also find that dwarf and satellite galaxies are more sensitive to the underlying dark matter model, despite their poorer overall tracing performance. Our results demonstrate the potential of ICL as a novel observational probe of dark matter physics and provide a first step toward using diffuse cluster light to constrain the nature of dark matter.

### [33] [Reconstruction of the Quintessence Scalar Field Potential Using Gaussian Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04056)
*Redouane El Ouardi,Amine Bouali,Ahmed Errahmani,Ryan E. Keeley,Arman Shafieloo,Taoufik Ouali*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We perform a model-independent reconstruction of the quintessence scalar field potential using Gaussian Process regression and recent cosmological data, including DESI DR2 BAO, cosmic chronometers, and Pantheon+ supernova data. The analysis reveals that both power-law and exponential potentials are consistent with observations.

我们使用高斯过程回归和最新的宇宙学数据（包括DESI DR2 BAO、宇宙计时器和Pantheon+超新星数据）对quintessence标量场势进行了完全模型无关的重构。分析表明，幂律势和指数势均与观测结果一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent observations, particularly from DESI DR1 and DR2, suggest possible deviations from a constant dark energy density, motivating a model-independent investigation of dynamical dark energy described by quintessence. Assuming a specific form for the scalar field potential may introduce bias; hence, a nonparametric approach is needed to let the data determine the shape of the potential.

最近的观测（特别是来自DESI DR1和DR2的数据）表明暗能量密度可能偏离常数，这促使人们研究由quintessence描述的动力学暗能量。假设标量场势具有特定形式可能会引入偏差，因此需要一种非参数方法让数据决定势的形式。

Method: We apply Gaussian Process (GP) regression to reconstruct the Hubble parameter $H(z)$ from cosmic chronometer and DESI DR2 BAO data, combined with Pantheon+ supernova luminosity distances. From $H(z)$, we derive the scalar field potential $V(\phi)$ and kinetic energy $\dot{\phi}^2/2$ without assuming any parametric form. Two covariance kernels—the squared exponential and Mat\'ern ($\nu=9/2$)—are used to test robustness. We also examine the influence of priors on $\Omega_m$ and spatial curvature $\Omega_k$. The reconstructed potential is compared to theoretical benchmarks: a power-law potential $V(\phi) \propto \phi^{-\alpha}$ and an exponential potential $V(\phi) \propto e^{-\lambda \phi}$.

我们应用高斯过程（GP）回归，利用宇宙计时器和DESI DR2 BAO数据以及Pantheon+超新星光度距离重构哈勃参数$H(z)$。从$H(z)$出发，在不假设任何参数形式的情况下推导出标量场势$V(\phi)$和动能$\dot{\phi}^2/2$。采用两种协方差核函数——平方指数核和Mat\'ern核（$\nu=9/2$）——以检验稳健性。我们还考察了物质密度$\Omega_m$和空间曲率$\Omega_k$先验的影响。将重构的势与两个理论基准模型进行比较：幂律势$V(\phi) \propto \phi^{-\alpha}$和指数势$V(\phi) \propto e^{-\lambda \phi}$。

Result: The GP reconstructions yield smooth and physically plausible forms for $V(\phi)$ and $\dot{\phi}^2/2$, with uncertainties increasing at higher redshifts due to data sparsity. Results are largely insensitive to the choice of kernel, indicating robustness of the method. The reconstructed potential is consistent with both the power-law and exponential benchmark models within 68% confidence intervals across the redshift range $0 < z < 2.5$. Tighter constraints are obtained when assuming a flat universe and standard $\Omega_m$ prior.

高斯过程重构得到了平滑且物理上合理的$V(\phi)$和$\dot{\phi}^2/2$形式，但由于高红移区域数据稀疏，不确定性随红移增加而增大。结果对核函数的选择基本不敏感，表明该方法具有稳健性。在$0 < z < 2.5$范围内，重构的势在68%置信区间内与幂律和指数基准模型均一致。当假设平坦宇宙和标准$\Omega_m$先验时，约束更为紧密。

Conclusion: Our model-independent analysis supports the viability of quintessence as a dynamical dark energy candidate. While no strong evidence favors deviation from simple theoretical models, current data remain compatible with both power-law and exponential potentials. Future high-precision measurements at higher redshifts will be crucial to distinguish between competing quintessence scenarios and further constrain the evolution of dark energy.

我们的模型无关分析支持quintessence作为动力学暗能量候选者的可行性。尽管目前没有强有力证据表明需偏离简单理论模型，但现有数据仍与幂律和指数势兼容。未来更高红移的高精度测量对于区分不同的quintessence情景并进一步约束暗能量演化至关重要。

Abstract: Recent cosmological observations, including the latest Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI) data releases DR1 and DR2, have renewed interest in the possibility that dark energy may exhibit dynamical behavior rather than being a strict cosmological constant. In this work, we perform a fully model-independent reconstruction of the quintessence scalar field potential using Gaussian Process regression and current Hubble measurements. Instead of assuming a specific functional form for the scalar field potential, we reconstruct the quintessence potential and the corresponding kinetic energy directly from observational data. Our analysis is based on Hubble parameter measurements obtained from cosmic chronometers and the latest high-precision DESI DR2 baryon acoustic oscillation (BAO) data, together with Type Ia supernova data from the Pantheon+ compilation. Gaussian Processes provide a nonparametric and model-independent framework that allows the data to guide the reconstruction. We employ two covariance functions, namely the squared exponential and the Matern ($ν= 9/2$) kernels, in order to assess the sensitivity of the reconstruction to the kernel choice. We further explore the impact of background cosmological assumptions by considering different priors on the matter density and spatial curvature. Finally, we compare the reconstructed scalar field potential with two theoretically motivated benchmark models: a power law potential and an exponential potential. We find that both models remain consistent with the reconstructed potential within the inferred confidence intervals.

</details>


### [34] [Gaussian-Process Emulation of the Redshift-Space Halo Power Spectrum Monopole in Cosmologies with Massive Neutrinos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04122)
*Jixin Gan,Yonghao Feng,Gong-Bo Zhao*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We present a Gaussian-process (GP) emulator for the monopole of the redshift-space halo power spectrum in $\Lambda$CDM cosmologies with massive neutrinos. The emulator is trained on 1000 COLA simulations distributed in a Latin-hypercube design over the six-dimensional cosmological parameter space $\{\Omega_m h^2,\Omega_b h^2,\Omega_\nu h^2,\sigma_8,h,n_s\}$, with outputs at 11 snapshots spanning $0.5 \le z \le 2.0$. From redshift-space halo catalogues we measure shot-noise-subtracted monopole spectra over $0.01 \le k \le 0.50\,h\,\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$. We also generate 1000 fixed-cosmology realizations to estimate the covariance matrix and to construct synthetic data vectors for likelihood tests. On held-out cosmologies, the emulator reproduces the simulated spectra to typically better than $2\%$ across the scales and redshifts considered. Combined with its GP-based estimate of interpolation uncertainty, this speed and accuracy make the emulator well suited to repeated likelihood evaluations in Markov Chain Monte Carlo analyses. The resulting framework provides an efficient route toward neutrino-mass inference from DESI-motivated redshift-space clustering measurements.

我们提出了一个用于含大质量中微子的$\Lambda$CDM宇宙学中红移空间晕单极功率谱的高斯过程（GP）模拟器。该模拟器在六维宇宙学参数空间$\{\Omega_m h^2,\Omega_b h^2,\Omega_\nu h^2,\sigma_8,h,n_s\}$上的拉丁超立方设计分布的1000个COLA模拟上进行训练，输出覆盖$0.5 \le z \le 2.0$的11个快照。从红移空间晕目录中，我们在$0.01 \le k \le 0.50\,h\,\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$范围内测量了扣除散粒噪声的单极谱。我们还生成了1000个固定宇宙学实现以估计协方差矩阵，并为似然测试构建合成数据向量。在保留的宇宙学上，该模拟器在所考虑的尺度和红移范围内通常能以优于$2\%$的精度再现模拟谱。结合其基于GP的插值不确定性估计，这种速度和精度使模拟器非常适合在马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛分析中进行重复的似然评估。由此产生的框架为从DESI驱动的红移空间聚集测量中推断中微子质量提供了一条高效途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Accurate modeling of the redshift-space halo power spectrum is essential for extracting cosmological information from large-scale structure surveys like DESI, especially in $\Lambda$CDM models with massive neutrinos, where nonlinear structure formation and redshift-space distortions complicate theoretical predictions. Traditional N-body simulations are computationally expensive, making them impractical for iterative inference methods such as Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC). Therefore, there is a strong need for fast, accurate emulators that can interpolate across cosmological parameter space and provide reliable uncertainty estimates.

精确建模红移空间晕功率谱对于从DESI等大尺度结构巡天中提取宇宙学信息至关重要，尤其是在含大质量中微子的$\Lambda$CDM模型中，非线性结构形成和红移空间畸变使理论预测变得复杂。传统的N体模拟计算成本高昂，难以适用于马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）等迭代推断方法。因此，迫切需要快速、准确的模拟器，能够在宇宙学参数空间中插值并提供可靠的不确定性估计。

Method: We construct a Gaussian-process (GP) emulator trained on 1000 COLA (COmoving Lagrangian Acceleration) simulations, designed using a Latin hypercube sampling over a six-dimensional cosmological parameter space $\{\Omega_m h^2, \Omega_b h^2, \Omega_\nu h^2, \sigma_8, h, n_s\}$. The simulations span 11 redshift snapshots between $z = 0.5$ and $z = 2.0$. For each simulation, we compute the shot-noise-subtracted monopole of the redshift-space halo power spectrum in the wavenumber range $0.01 \leq k \leq 0.50\,h\,\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$. A separate set of 1000 fixed-cosmology simulations is used to estimate the covariance matrix and generate synthetic data vectors for validation and likelihood testing. The GP emulator incorporates both mean prediction and uncertainty quantification via Bayesian interpolation.

我们构建了一个高斯过程（GP）模拟器，训练于1000个COLA（共动拉格朗日加速）模拟之上，这些模拟在六维宇宙学参数空间$\{\Omega_m h^2, \Omega_b h^2, \Omega_\nu h^2, \sigma_8, h, n_s\}$上采用拉丁超立方采样设计。模拟覆盖了$z = 0.5$到$z = 2.0$之间的11个红移快照。对每个模拟，我们在波数范围$0.01 \leq k \leq 0.50\,h\,\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$内计算红移空间晕功率谱的扣除散粒噪声后的单极矩。另外一组1000个固定宇宙学模拟用于估计协方差矩阵，并生成用于验证和似然测试的合成数据向量。GP模拟器通过贝叶斯插值同时包含均值预测和不确定性量化。

Result: The emulator achieves sub-2\% accuracy in predicting the monopole power spectrum across the full range of scales and redshifts when tested on held-out cosmologies. It accurately captures nonlinear effects induced by massive neutrinos and redshift-space distortions. The GP framework provides a principled estimate of interpolation uncertainty, which is crucial for robust likelihood evaluation. The combination of high accuracy, speed, and uncertainty quantification enables efficient MCMC sampling for cosmological parameter inference, particularly for $\Omega_\nu h^2$, the parameter encoding the sum of neutrino masses.

在保留的宇宙学上测试时，该模拟器在全尺度和红移范围内对单极功率谱的预测精度优于2\%。它准确捕捉了由大质量中微子和红移空间畸变引起的非线性效应。GP框架提供了插值不确定性的合理估计，这对于稳健的似然评估至关重要。高精度、高速度和不确定性量化相结合，使得马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）采样在宇宙学参数推断中更加高效，特别是针对编码中微子质量总和的参数$\Omega_\nu h^2$。

Conclusion: The developed GP emulator provides a fast, accurate, and statistically robust tool for modeling the redshift-space halo power spectrum in $\Lambda$CDM cosmologies with massive neutrinos. Its integration into MCMC pipelines enables efficient and reliable inference of cosmological parameters, including the neutrino mass sum, from current and future galaxy surveys such as DESI. This framework represents a significant step toward scalable, simulation-based cosmological analysis in the era of precision large-scale structure data.

所开发的GP模拟器为含大质量中微子的$\Lambda$CDM宇宙学中红移空间晕功率谱的建模提供了一个快速、准确且统计稳健的工具。将其集成到MCMC流程中，能够从当前和未来的星系巡天（如DESI）中高效可靠地推断宇宙学参数，包括中微子质量总和。该框架代表了迈向可扩展的、基于模拟的宇宙学分析在精确大尺度结构数据时代的重要一步。

Abstract: We present a Gaussian-process (GP) emulator for the monopole of the redshift-space halo power spectrum in $Λ$CDM cosmologies with massive neutrinos. The emulator is trained on 1000 COLA simulations distributed in a Latin-hypercube design over the six-dimensional cosmological parameter space $\{Ω_m h^2,Ω_b h^2,Ω_νh^2,σ_8,h,n_s\}$, with outputs at 11 snapshots spanning $0.5 \le z \le 2.0$. From redshift-space halo catalogues we measure shot-noise-subtracted monopole spectra over $0.01 \le k \le 0.50\,h\,\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$. We also generate 1000 fixed-cosmology realizations to estimate the covariance matrix and to construct synthetic data vectors for likelihood tests. On held-out cosmologies, the emulator reproduces the simulated spectra to typically better than $2\%$ across the scales and redshifts considered. Combined with its GP-based estimate of interpolation uncertainty, this speed and accuracy make the emulator well suited to repeated likelihood evaluations in Markov Chain Monte Carlo analyses. The resulting framework provides an efficient route toward neutrino-mass inference from DESI-motivated redshift-space clustering measurements.

</details>


### [35] [Replacing Gaussian Processes with Neural Networks in Pulsar Timing Array Inference of the Gravitational-Wave Background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04340)
*Shreyas Tiruvaskar,Chris Gordon*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: Probabilistic neural networks are shown to effectively replace Gaussian processes in Bayesian inference of nanohertz gravitational-wave background models from pulsar timing array data, offering faster training and MCMC runtime without sacrificing posterior accuracy.

概率型神经网络被证明可有效替代高斯过程，用于脉冲星计时阵列中纳赫兹引力波背景模型的贝叶斯推断，在不牺牲后验精度的前提下显著加快训练和MCMC运行时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Gaussian-process (GP) interpolators are widely used in pulsar timing array analyses to approximate computationally expensive strain-spectrum calculations for Bayesian inference of gravitational-wave backgrounds. However, GP training scales poorly with large datasets ($\mathcal{O}(N^3)$), becoming a bottleneck as data volumes grow. This motivates the search for scalable alternatives such as probabilistic neural networks (PNNs) that can maintain accuracy while reducing computational cost.

高斯过程（GP）插值器在脉冲星计时阵列分析中被广泛用于近似计算昂贵的应变谱，以进行引力波背景的贝叶斯推断。然而，GP训练随数据集增大而急剧变慢（$\mathcal{O}(N^3)$），成为性能瓶颈。这促使人们寻找可扩展的替代方案，例如概率型神经网络（PNNs），以在保持精度的同时降低计算成本。

Method: We train probabilistic neural networks to emulate the strain spectrum predictions of two physical models: a self-interacting dark matter (SIDM) model and a phenomenological environmental model. The PNNs are trained on a finite set of simulated spectra and learn to predict the spectral parameters with uncertainty estimates. During Bayesian inference, the PNN replaces repeated numerical computations, enabling fast likelihood evaluations. We compare the PNN-based inference against traditional Gaussian-process interpolators in terms of posterior consistency, training time, and Markov chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) efficiency.

我们训练概率型神经网络来模拟两种物理模型的应变谱预测：自相互作用暗物质（SIDM）模型和一种现象学环境模型。PNN在有限的模拟谱数据集上进行训练，学习预测具有不确定性估计的谱参数。在贝叶斯推断过程中，PNN取代重复的数值计算，实现快速似然评估。我们将基于PNN的推断与传统高斯过程插值器在后验一致性、训练时间和马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）效率方面进行了比较。

Result: The probabilistic neural networks recover posteriors that are consistent with those obtained using Gaussian processes, within statistical uncertainties. Training times are reduced by up to an order of magnitude, and MCMC runtimes are significantly shortened—especially for the more complex SIDM model, where the computational savings are most pronounced. The PNN approach scales more favorably with training set size compared to GPs.

概率型神经网络恢复的后验分布与高斯过程结果在统计不确定度内一致。训练时间最多减少了一个数量级，MCMC运行时间显著缩短——尤其是在更复杂的SIDM模型中，计算节省最为明显。与高斯过程相比，PNN方法在训练集规模增大时表现出更优的可扩展性。

Conclusion: Probabilistic neural networks are a viable and efficient alternative to Gaussian processes for emulating gravitational-wave strain spectra in pulsar timing array analyses. They enable faster Bayesian inference without compromising accuracy, particularly benefiting computationally intensive models like self-interacting dark matter. This advancement supports scalability in future high-precision nanohertz gravitational-wave astronomy.

概率型神经网络是脉冲星计时阵列分析中模拟引力波应变谱的可行且高效的高斯过程替代方案。它们在不牺牲精度的前提下实现了更快的贝叶斯推断，尤其有利于自相互作用暗物质等计算密集型模型。这一进展支持了未来高精度纳赫兹引力波天文学的可扩展性发展。

Abstract: Bayesian inference of nanohertz gravitational-wave background models in pulsar timing array analyses often relies on Gaussian-process interpolators to avoid repeated, computationally expensive strain-spectrum calculations. However, Gaussian-process training becomes a bottleneck for large training sets. We test whether probabilistic neural networks can replace Gaussian processes in this role for both a self-interacting dark matter model and a phenomenological environmental model. We find that neural networks recover consistent posteriors while significantly reducing both training and Markov chain Monte Carlo runtime, with the largest gains for the more computationally demanding model.
