### [36] [Probing cosmic anisotropy with galaxy clusters and supernovae](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04408)
*Shubham Barua,Sujit K. Dalui,Shantanu Desai*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: Using ΛCDM and Padé-(2,1) cosmography, this study analyzes directional variations in the Hubble constant $H_0$ via hemisphere decomposition with galaxy clusters and Type Ia Supernovae (Pantheon Plus). By employing galaxy cluster scaling relations as an alternative to Cepheid calibrations, the results show consistent $\lesssim 1\sigma$ differences in $H_0$, supporting calibration robustness. A $\sim 2\sigma$ deviation from isotropy is found across all model-data combinations, with the maximum $\Delta H_0$ aligned close to the CMB dipole direction.

使用ΛCDM和Padé-(2,1)宇宙学方法，本研究通过星系团和Ia型超新星（Pantheon Plus）的半球分解法分析哈勃常数$H_0$的方向变化。采用星系团标度关系替代造父变星校准，结果显示不同校准方法间$H_0$差异约为$\lesssim 1\sigma$，支持结果的鲁棒性。在所有模型与数据组合中均发现约$\sim 2\sigma$的各向异性偏离，且最大$\Delta H_0$方向接近CMB偶极方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The Hubble constant $H_0$ exhibits persistent tensions between early- and late-universe measurements, and potential anisotropies could hint at new physics or systematic effects. Since $H_0$ inferred from Type Ia Supernovae depends on the absolute magnitude $M_B$, it requires external calibrators like Cepheid variables. However, relying solely on Cepheid hosts may introduce biases. This work aims to test the robustness of reported $H_0$ anisotropies by using galaxy cluster scaling relations as an independent calibration method, complementing traditional Cepheid-based approaches.

哈勃常数$H_0$在早期与晚期宇宙测量之间存在持续张力，潜在的各向异性可能暗示新物理或系统误差。由于Ia型超新星推断的$H_0$依赖于绝对星等$M_B$，需借助造父变星等外部校准。然而，仅依赖造父宿主可能引入偏差。本工作旨在利用星系团标度关系作为独立校准方法，检验已报道$H_0$各向异性的鲁棒性，补充传统造父变星方法。

Method: The authors employ the hemisphere decomposition method to probe directional anisotropies in $H_0$. They use two cosmological models: standard $Λ$CDM and Padé-(2,1) cosmography, which provides a rational approximation to the scale factor's expansion history. Two datasets are utilized: Type Ia Supernovae from Pantheon Plus and galaxy cluster data via scaling relations (e.g., $L_X$–$T$ or $Y_X$–$M$). For supernovae, instead of exclusively using Cepheid-host calibrations for $M_B$, they alternatively calibrate using parameters derived from galaxy cluster observations. The $H_0$ value is then fitted independently in different sky hemispheres to detect dipolar variations, and statistical significance is assessed via bootstrapping and Monte Carlo methods.

作者采用半球分解法探测$H_0$的方向各向异性。使用两种宇宙学模型：标准ΛCDM和Padé-(2,1)宇宙学，后者为尺度因子膨胀历史提供有理近似。利用两类数据：来自Pantheon Plus的Ia型超新星和通过标度关系（如$L_X$–$T$或$Y_X$–$M$）的星系团数据。对于超新星，不再 exclusively 使用造父宿主校准$M_B$，而是改用从星系团观测导出的参数进行校准。随后在不同天球半球中独立拟合$H_0$值以检测偶极变化，并通过自助法（bootstrapping）和蒙特卡洛方法评估统计显著性。

Result: When using galaxy cluster calibrations instead of Cepheid hosts, the inferred $H_0$ values differ by $\lesssim 1\sigma$, indicating consistency between the two calibration methods. Across all combinations of models ($Λ$CDM and Padé-(2,1)) and datasets, a deviation from isotropy at the level of $\sim 2\sigma$ is observed. In nearly all cases, the direction of maximum $\Delta H_0$ aligns closely with the CMB dipole direction, suggesting a possible large-scale anisotropy in the expansion rate of the universe.

使用星系团校准替代造父变星宿主时，推断的$H_0$值差异约为$\lesssim 1\sigma$，表明两种校准方法一致。在所有模型（ΛCDM和Padé-(2,1)）与数据集组合中，均观察到约$\sim 2\sigma$水平的各向异性偏离。几乎所有情况下，最大$\Delta H_0$方向均与CMB偶极方向高度一致，暗示宇宙膨胀率可能存在大尺度各向异性。

Conclusion: The directional variation in $H_0$ is robust against different calibration methods, as shown by the small ($\lesssim 1\sigma$) discrepancies between Cepheid- and cluster-based calibrations. The consistent $\sim 2\sigma$ deviation from isotropy across models and data suggests potential large-scale anisotropy in the universe's expansion. The alignment of the $\Delta H_0$ maximum with the CMB dipole direction strengthens the case for a physical origin rather than random statistical fluctuation, though more data are needed to confirm this at higher significance.

$H_0$的方向变化对不同校准方法具有鲁棒性，造父变星与星系团校准间的微小差异（$\lesssim 1\sigma$）证明了这一点。模型与数据间一致的约$\sim 2\sigma$各向异性偏离表明宇宙膨胀可能存在大尺度各向异性。$\Delta H_0$最大值与CMB偶极方向的对齐增强了其物理起源的可能性而非随机统计涨落，但仍需更多数据以更高显著性确认。

Abstract: Using $Λ$CDM and Padé-(2,1) cosmography, we study directional variations in the Hubble constant, $H_0$, using galaxy cluster and Type Ia Supernovae (from Pantheon Plus) by the hemisphere decomposition method. Since there is a degeneracy between $H_0$ and absolute magnitude $M_B$ for Supernovae, Cepheid host calibration is usually required to constrain $H_0$. Hence, in this work in order to complement the Cepheid host calibration in Supernovae, we also use calibrations based on galaxy cluster scaling relations. We find that there is a $\lesssim 1σ$ difference in $H_0$ variations when using galaxy clusters as calibrators compared to Cepheids highlighting that the variations in $H_0$ are robust across different calibration methods. Across all combinations of models and data sets used, we obtain a consistent deviation $\sim 2σ$ from isotropy. In nearly all cases, we notice that the maximum $ΔH_0$ aligns with the CMB dipole direction.

### [37] [Information-Geometric Perspective on the Hubble Tension: Eigenmode Rotation and Curvature Suppression in wCDM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04422)
*Seokcheon Lee*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The Hubble tension is analyzed in the wCDM model by decomposing it into a parameter shift and directional Fisher curvature, revealing that extending \Lambda CDM to wCDM mainly softens the CMB constraint geometry rather than achieving true concordance, while late-time data like DESI DR2 add stiffness that limits tension relief.

本文在wCDM模型中通过将哈勃张力分解为参数偏移和方向性Fisher曲率来分析其几何结构，发现从\Lambda CDM扩展到wCDM主要软化了CMB约束的几何形态，而非实现真正的数据一致性，而DESI DR2等晚期高精度数据则增加了扩张速率方向上的刚度，限制了张力缓解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The Hubble tension persists as a major challenge in cosmology, with discrepancies between early- and late-universe measurements of $H_0$. While model extensions like wCDM are often explored to relieve this tension, it remains unclear whether such relief arises from genuine concordance or merely from a reshaping of statistical constraints. This work aims to disentangle these effects by analyzing the geometric structure of parameter space using the Fisher information matrix.

哈勃张力作为宇宙学中的主要难题持续存在，表现为早期与晚期宇宙对$H_0$测量值之间的差异。尽管像wCDM这样的模型扩展常被用来缓解张力，但尚不清楚这种缓解是源于真实的数据一致性，还是仅仅来自统计约束的形变。本研究旨在通过Fisher信息矩阵分析参数空间的几何结构来区分这些效应。

Method: We employ a shift-curvature decomposition of cosmological tensions within the wCDM model, using the local Gaussian approximation. The quadratic tension along a given direction is factorized into the squared parameter shift and the combined directional Fisher curvature from datasets (e.g., Planck, DESI DR2, SH0ES). We compute the eigenvalues and eigenvectors of the Fisher matrices to identify dominant modes, particularly those related to the acoustic scale and expansion rate.

我们在wCDM模型中采用局部高斯近似下的偏移-曲率分解方法，将沿某一方向的二次张力分解为平方参数偏移与来自各数据集（如Planck、DESI DR2、SH0ES）的方向性Fisher曲率的组合。我们计算Fisher矩阵的本征值和本征向量，以识别主导模式，特别是与声学尺度和膨胀率相关的模式。

Result: Extending \Lambda CDM to wCDM suppresses the leading Fisher eigenvalue of Planck by over 97\%, reducing it to \sim 2.7\% of its original value, indicating a significant softening of the CMB's acoustic rigidity. Meanwhile, DESI DR2 introduces strong curvature along the $H_0$ direction, acting as a geometric wall that blocks phantom-like solutions ($w < -1$) and limits overall tension reduction. The tension reduction in $H_0$ is thus not due to improved agreement but to a reconfiguration of the constraint manifold.

将\Lambda CDM扩展至wCDM使Planck的主Fisher本征值下降超过97\%，降至原始值的约2.7\%，表明CMB声学刚度显著软化。与此同时，DESI DR2在$H_0$方向引入强曲率，形成几何壁垒，阻断类幻象解（$w < -1$），并限制整体张力缓解。因此，$H_0$张力的减小并非源于改进的一致性，而是约束流形的重构所致。

Conclusion: The shift-curvature decomposition provides a physically transparent framework for diagnosing cosmological tensions. In wCDM, the apparent relief of the Hubble tension is largely an artifact of softened CMB constraints and increased stiffness from late-time data, rather than evidence of new physical concordance. This highlights the importance of analyzing the geometric structure of parameter spaces when assessing model extensions.

偏移-曲率分解为诊断宇宙学张力提供了物理上透明的框架。在wCDM中，哈勃张力的表观缓解主要是CMB约束软化与晚期数据刚度增加的产物，而非新物理一致性的证据。这凸显了在评估模型扩展时分析参数空间几何结构的重要性。

Abstract: The Hubble tension is shaped not only by shifts between early- and late-time parameter estimates, but also by the stiffness of the constraints that define them. In this work, we analyze this geometric structure in the wCDM model by separating the discrepancy into two components: a parameter displacement and a directional Fisher curvature. Within the local Gaussian approximation, the quadratic tension along a given direction factorizes into the squared shift and the combined directional curvature contributed by the datasets. Applying this framework to Planck, DESI DR2, and SH0ES, we show that extending \LambdaCDM to wCDM primarily reshapes the Fisher geometry of the CMB constraint rather than opening a genuinely new route to concordance. Allowing the dark-energy equation-of-state parameter w to vary suppresses the leading Planck Fisher eigenvalue to only \sim 2.7 % of its \LambdaCDM value, while producing only a modest rotation of the dominant acoustic-scale eigenmode. The net effect is a strong softening of the effective acoustic rigidity. At the same time, high-precision late-time data, especially from DESI DR2, inject substantial curvature along the expansion-rate direction. This added stiffness acts as a geometric wall, closing off phantom-like escape routes and sharply limiting tension relief within the extended parameter space. Our results indicate that changes in the inferred H_0 tension under model extension are best understood as a reconfiguration of the constraint manifold rather than as evidence for new physical agreement. The shift-curvature decomposition thus offers a simple, fast, and physically transparent way to diagnose cosmological tensions.

</details>


### [38] [Directional Tests of the Cosmic Distance Duality Relation using Pantheon+ and BAO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04436)
*Pushty Shrimankar,Gopal Kashyap*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We perform a model-independent test of anisotropy in the cosmic distance duality relation (CDDR) using Pantheon+ supernovae and BAO data, reconstructing angular diameter distances via Gaussian Processes and modeling anisotropy as a dipole modulation. No significant deviation from isotropy is found, with a robust 95% upper limit on the dipole amplitude of $A_{95} = 0.025$, highlighting the importance of survey selection effects.

我们使用Pantheon+超新星和BAO数据对宇宙距离对偶关系（CDDR）的各向异性进行了一次模型无关的检验，通过高斯过程重构角直径距离，并以偶极调制建模各向异性。未发现显著偏离各向同性的证据，得到稳健的95%偶极振幅上限$A_{95} = 0.025$，强调了巡天选择效应在各向异性搜索中的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The cosmic distance duality relation (CDDR), $D_L = (1+z)^2 D_A$, is a cornerstone of standard cosmology, relying on photon number conservation and metric theory of gravity. Testing its validity, especially potential anisotropic violations, is crucial for probing new physics beyond general relativity or exotic light propagation. Previous tests often assume specific cosmological models; here, we aim to conduct a model-independent, anisotropy-focused test while properly accounting for observational systematics like survey geometry and selection effects.

宇宙距离对偶关系（CDDR），即$D_L = (1+z)^2 D_A$，是标准宇宙学的基石，依赖于光子数守恒和度规引力理论。检验其有效性，尤其是可能的各向异性破坏，对于探索广义相对论之外的新物理或奇异光传播机制至关重要。以往的检验常依赖特定宇宙学模型；本文旨在进行一次模型无关且聚焦各向异性的检验，同时妥善考虑巡天几何和选择效应等观测系统误差。

Method: We use the Pantheon+ type Ia supernova (SN Ia) sample and baryon acoustic oscillation (BAO) measurements to independently constrain luminosity distance $D_L$ and angular diameter distance $D_A$. The $D_A$ is reconstructed via Gaussian Processes (GP) from BAO data without assuming a background cosmology. We define the CDDR violation parameter $\eta(z) = D_L / [D_A (1+z)^2]$, allowing for isotropic evolution via $\eta(z) = 1 + \eta_1 z$. Anisotropy is modeled as a dipole modulation: $\eta(\hat{\mathbf{n}}) = \eta_0 (1 + A \hat{\mathbf{d}} \cdot \hat{\mathbf{n}})$, where $\hat{\mathbf{n}}$ is the line-of-sight direction. A full covariance-based likelihood is used to fit the dipole parameters. To assess significance, we generate null simulations that preserve the observed redshift distribution and survey selection function, enabling robust statistical inference.

我们使用Pantheon+ Ia型超新星（SN Ia）样本和重子声学振荡（BAO）测量来独立约束光度距离$D_L$和角直径距离$D_A$。利用高斯过程（Gaussian Processes, GP）从BAO数据中重构$D_A$，无需假设背景宇宙学。定义CDDR破坏参数$\eta(z) = D_L / [D_A (1+z)^2]$，并允许通过$\eta(z) = 1 + \eta_1 z$描述各向同性演化。各向异性被建模为偶极调制：$\eta(\hat{\mathbf{n}}) = \eta_0 (1 + A \hat{\mathbf{d}} \cdot \hat{\mathbf{n}})$，其中$\hat{\mathbf{n}}$为视线方向。采用基于完整协方差矩阵的似然函数拟合偶极参数。为评估显著性，我们生成保留实际红移分布和巡天选择函数的零假设模拟，以实现稳健的统计推断。

Result: We find no statistically significant evidence for CDDR anisotropy. The observed dipole amplitude is consistent with isotropic expectations and lies below the level of statistical fluctuations induced by survey geometry and selection effects. The results are stable across different SN Ia calibration choices. We obtain a robust 95\% upper bound on the dipole amplitude: $A_{95} = 0.025$. The isotropic deviation parameter $\eta_1$ shows mild redshift dependence, but its significance depends on the supernova calibration method.

未发现CDDR各向异性的统计显著证据。观测到的偶极振幅与各向同性预期一致，且低于巡天几何和选择效应引起的统计涨落水平。结果在不同超新星定标方法下保持稳定。我们获得了一个稳健的95%偶极振幅上限：$A_{95} = 0.025$。各向同性偏差参数$\eta_1$显示出轻微的红移依赖性，但其显著性依赖于超新星定标方法。

Conclusion: There is no evidence for intrinsic anisotropy in the cosmic distance duality relation (CDDR) within current observational precision. The observed signals are consistent with statistical noise and survey geometry effects. Our analysis underscores the necessity of incorporating realistic survey selection functions in anisotropy tests to avoid spurious detections. The framework developed provides a robust, model-independent approach for future directional tests of fundamental cosmological relations.

在当前观测精度下，未发现宇宙距离对偶关系（CDDR）存在内在各向异性的证据。观测信号与统计噪声及巡天几何效应一致。本分析强调了在各向异性检验中纳入真实巡天选择函数的必要性，以避免虚假探测。所发展的框架为未来基本宇宙学关系的方向性检验提供了稳健且模型无关的方法。

Abstract: We present a model-independent test of anisotropy in the cosmic distance duality relation (CDDR), $D_L=(1+z)^2 D_A$, using the Pantheon+ type Ia supernova sample and baryon acoustic oscillation (BAO) data. The angular diameter distance is reconstructed via Gaussian Processes, enabling an estimate of $η(z)=D_L/[D_A(1+z)^2]$ without assuming a background cosmology. We also allow for a possible isotropic evolution, parameterized as $η(z)=1+η_1 z$, and find a redshift-dependent deviation whose significance depends on the assumed supernova calibration. Anisotropy is modeled through a dipole modulation and constrained using a full covariance-based likelihood. To assess statistical significance, we construct null realizations that preserve both the redshift distribution and the survey selection function. We find that the observed dipole amplitude is consistent with isotropic expectations and lies below the levels induced by statistical fluctuations and survey geometry. We obtain a robust 95\% upper bound $A_{95}=0.025$, stable across different supernova calibration choices. We find no evidence for intrinsic anisotropy in the CDDR. Our results highlight the importance of accounting for survey selection effects in anisotropy searches and provide a viable framework for testing directional deviations in cosmological relations.

</details>


### [39] [Measurement of the galaxy-velocity power spectrum of DESI tracers with the kinematic Sunyaev-Zeldovich effect using DESI DR2 and ACT DR6](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04867)
*Edmond Chaussidon,Selim C. Hotinli,Simone Ferraro,Kendrick Smith,Xinyi Chen,J. Aguilar,S. Ahlen,D. Bianchi,D. Brooks,T. Claybaugh,A. Cuceu,A. de la Macorra,B. Dey,P. Doel,A. Font-Ribera,J. E. Forero-Romero,E. Gaztañaga,S. Gontcho A Gontcho,G. Gutierrez,J. Guy,H. K. Herrera-Alcantar,K. Honscheid,C. Howlett,D. Huterer,M. Ishak,R. Joyce,D. Kirkby,A. Kremin,O. Lahav,M. Landriau,L. Le Guillou,M. Manera,A. Meisner,R. Miquel,S. Nadathur,J. A. Newman,N. Palanque-Delabrouille,W. J. Percival,F. Prada,I. Pérez-Ràfols,G. Rossi,L. Samushia,E. Sanchez,D. Schlegel,M. Schubnell,H. Seo,J. Silber,D. Sprayberry,G. Tarlé,B. A. Weaver,C. Yèche,R. Zhou*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We present the first high-significance detection of the kSZ effect using ACT DR6 and DESI DR2 data, measuring velocity-galaxy and velocity-velocity correlations across multiple tracers (LRGs, ELGs, QSOs), achieving a cumulative $20.8\sigma$ detection. We obtain the tightest constraint on local PNG to date from the velocity field: $f_{\rm NL}^{\rm loc} = 15.9_{-34.4}^{+34.6}$.

我们首次利用ACT DR6和DESI DR2数据高显著性地探测到动理SZ效应，测量了多种示踪物（LRG、ELG、QSO）的速星系关联和速速关联，累积显著性达$20.8\sigma$。我们获得了迄今来自速度场对局域型原初非高斯性最紧的限制：$f_{\rm NL}^{\rm loc} = 15.9_{-34.4}^{+34.6}$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The kSZ effect encodes information about the peculiar velocities of large-scale structure, offering a powerful probe of growth of structure, neutrino masses, and primordial non-Gaussianity (PNG). However, robust detections require joint analyses of high-resolution CMB and deep galaxy surveys to overcome noise and foreground contamination. The advent of ACT DR6 and DESI DR2 enables unprecedented precision in reconstructing the radial velocity field via the kSZ signal.

kSZ效应包含大尺度结构退行速度的信息，是研究结构增长、中微子质量及原初非高斯性（PNG）的有力探针。然而，稳健探测需要高分辨率CMB与深空星系巡天的联合分析以克服噪声与前景污染。ACT DR6与DESI DR2的出现使得通过kSZ信号重建径向速度场达到前所未有的精度。

Method: We cross-correlate ACT DR6 CMB temperature maps with DESI DR2 galaxy catalogs (LRGs, ELGs, QSOs) to reconstruct the line-of-sight velocity field via the kSZ effect. We model the kSZ signal using a halo model framework with a Battaglia electron profile and account for foregrounds using spectroscopic redshift information. We measure the velocity-galaxy cross-power spectrum and velocity auto-power spectrum, validating our pipeline with simulations and null tests.

我们交叉关联ACT DR6的CMB温度图与DESI DR2星系目录（LRG、ELG、QSO），通过kSZ效应重建视线速度场。使用基于Battaglia电子轮廓的晕模型框架建模kSZ信号，并利用光谱红移信息扣除前景。测量速星系互功率谱与速速自功率谱，并通过模拟与零检验验证分析流程。

Result: We detect the velocity-galaxy cross-correlation at $17.0\sigma$ (LRGs), $8.3\sigma$ (ELGs), and $6.8\sigma$ (QSOs). The velocity auto-correlation is detected at $3.1\sigma$ (first detection), yielding a total kSZ detection significance of $20.8\sigma$—the highest to date. The kSZ amplitude is lower than theoretical predictions based on the fiducial halo model and Battaglia profile. We constrain local-type PNG to $f_{\rm NL}^{\rm loc} = 15.9_{-34.4}^{+34.6}$ (68\% CL), the tightest from the velocity field.

我们以$17.0\sigma$（LRG）、$8.3\sigma$（ELG）和$6.8\sigma$（QSO）显著性探测到速星系互相关。首次以$3.1\sigma$显著性探测到速速自相关，总kSZ探测显著性达$20.8\sigma$——为迄今最高。kSZ信号幅度低于基于标准晕模型与Battaglia轮廓的理论预测。我们限制局域型PNG为$f_{\rm NL}^{\rm loc} = 15.9_{-34.4}^{+34.6}$（68\%置信水平），为目前来自速度场最紧约束。

Conclusion: This work demonstrates the power of kSZ cosmology using next-generation CMB and galaxy survey data. The high-precision velocity field reconstruction enables stringent tests of structure formation and early universe physics. The measured suppression of the kSZ amplitude suggests possible systematics or deviations in the electron distribution. Future data from Simons Observatory and CMB-S4 will further improve these measurements, making kSZ a cornerstone of large-scale structure analysis.

本工作展示了利用新一代CMB与星系巡天数据进行kSZ宇宙学研究的强大能力。高精度速度场重建为结构形成与早期宇宙物理提供了严格检验。观测到的kSZ信号压低可能暗示电子分布存在系统误差或偏离。Simons Observatory与CMB-S4的未来数据将进一步提升测量精度，使kSZ成为大尺度结构分析的核心手段。

Abstract: Joint analyses of high-resolution CMB temperature maps with galaxy surveys provide a unique way to reconstruct the radial velocity field of the underlying matter distribution via the kinematic Sunyaev-Zeldovich (kSZ) effect. Using data from the Atacama Cosmology Telescope (ACT) DR6 and the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI) DR2, we present radial velocity reconstructions for luminous red galaxies (LRGs), emission-line galaxies (ELGs), and quasars (QSOs). Leveraging the spectroscopic data, we are able to reliably model the foreground contamination and report a negligible impact on our main observables. We detect the velocity-galaxy cross-correlation at $17.0σ$ for LRGs, and for the first time, at $8.3σ$ for ELGs and $6.8σ$ for QSOs. We further report the first detection of the velocity-velocity correlation using LRGs at $3.1σ$, as well as the highest cumulative detection of the kSZ effect to date at $20.8 σ$. Similarly to previous results, we find a lower amplitude of the kSZ signal compared to our fiducial halo model prediction and electron profile assuming a Battaglia profile. Combining these new observables, we obtain constraints on local-type primordial non-Gaussianity (PNG): $f_{\rm NL}^{\rm loc} = 15.9_{-34.4}^{+34.6}$ at 68\% confidence, which represents the tightest constraint to date derived from the velocity field. The measurements presented here already exhibit lower noise on a per-mode basis than the galaxy auto-correlation on the largest scales, $k<0.004~\rm{Mpc^{-1}}$, highlighting the key role these observables will play in the context of future CMB experiments such as the Simons Observatory.

### [40] [Fast Radio Burst Dispersion Measure--Timing Cross-Correlations: Bias Self-Calibration and Primordial Non-Gaussianity Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04897)
*Simthembile Dlamini*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper proposes using the cross-power spectrum between Fast Radio Burst (FRB) dispersion measures (DM) and Shapiro timing delays to break the degeneracy between electron bias $b_e$ and primordial non-Gaussianity $f_\mathrm{NL}$, enabling improved constraints on inflationary physics.

本文提出利用快速射电暴（FRB）色散测量（DM）与夏皮罗延迟之间的交叉功率谱，打破电子偏置$b_e$与原初非高斯性$f_\mathrm{NL}$之间的简并，从而提升对暴胀物理的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Primordial non-Gaussianity (PNG), especially local-type $f_\mathrm{NL}$, is a crucial probe of inflationary physics beyond single-field slow-roll models. However, large-scale PNG signatures in FRB dispersion measures are contaminated by astrophysical electron bias $b_e$, which introduces severe parameter degeneracies that degrade $σ(f_\mathrm{NL})$ when marginalised over. This degeneracy limits the utility of FRBs for early-Universe science unless broken.

原初非高斯性（PNG），特别是局域型$f_\mathrm{NL}$，是检验单场慢滚暴胀模型之外暴胀物理的关键探针。然而，FRB色散测量中大尺度的PNG信号受到天体物理电子偏置$b_e$的污染，导致严重的参数简并，当对$b_e$进行边缘化时会显著恶化$f_\mathrm{NL}$的误差。除非打破这一简并，否则将限制FRB在早期宇宙学中的应用。

Method: The authors introduce a new observable: the cross-power spectrum $C_\ell^{DΔt}$ between the FRB dispersion measure (DM) field $D$ and Shapiro time delay field $Δt$ from interferometric baselines. The DM field depends on both the matter density and electron bias $b_e$, while the Shapiro delay directly probes the Newtonian potential $Φ$ with no astrophysical bias. Using the Limber approximation, they analytically derive $C_\ell^{DΔt} \propto b_e$, showing it provides a direct, cosmology-independent measurement of $b_e$. A joint Fisher matrix analysis over $\{f_\mathrm{NL},\,b_e^0,\,z_\mathrm{fb}\}$ combines auto- and cross-spectra to self-calibrate $b_e$ and recover tight constraints on $f_\mathrm{NL}$.

作者引入了一个新观测量：FRB色散测量（DM）场$D$与干涉基线夏皮罗延迟场$Δt$之间的交叉功率谱$C_\ell^{DΔt}$。DM依赖于物质密度和电子偏置$b_e$，而夏皮罗延迟直接探测牛顿势$Φ$且不受天体物理偏置影响。利用Limber近似，他们解析推导出$C_\ell^{DΔt} \propto b_e$，表明其可提供与宇宙学无关的$b_e$直接测量。通过在$\{f_\mathrm{NL},\,b_e^0,\,z_\mathrm{fb}\}$上进行联合Fisher矩阵分析，结合自功率谱与交叉功率谱实现$b_e$的自校准，并恢复对$f_\mathrm{NL}$的紧密约束。

Result: The analytic derivation shows $C_\ell^{DΔt} \propto b_e$, independent of the matter power spectrum. The correlation coefficient between DM and Shapiro fields is $|ρ(\ell)| \approx 0.51$--$0.79$ over $\ell = 2$--$100$. Including $C_\ell^{DΔt}$ reduces $σ(b_e^0)$ by a factor of $2.1$--$5.1$ compared to DM-only analysis. In a joint analysis, $σ(f_\mathrm{NL})$ is recovered within a factor of $1.0$--$1.9$ of the fixed-bias case, vastly outperforming the $1.7$--$3.3$ degradation in DM-only marginalisation. For a shallow survey with $10^4$ FRBs and a 500\,AU baseline, the joint constraint yields $σ(f_\mathrm{NL}) \approx 790$, within 4\% of the fixed-bias benchmark and 3.3× tighter than DM-only marginalised result.

解析结果表明$C_\ell^{DΔt} \propto b_e$，且与物质功率谱无关。DM场与夏皮罗场之间的相关系数在$\ell = 2$--$100$范围内为$|ρ(\ell)| \approx 0.51$--$0.79$。引入$C_\ell^{DΔt}$使$σ(b_e^0)$比仅用DM分析降低$2.1$--$5.1$倍。联合分析中，$σ(f_\mathrm{NL})$仅比固定偏置情况差$1.0$--$1.9$倍，远优于DM单独分析时的$1.7$--$3.3$倍恶化。对于一个包含$10^4$个FRB和500\,AU基线的浅层巡天，联合约束给出$σ(f_\mathrm{NL}) \approx 790$，比固定偏置基准仅差4%，且比单独DM边缘化结果紧致3.3倍。

Conclusion: The cross-correlation between FRB dispersion measures and interferometric Shapiro delays provides a powerful self-calibration tool for electron bias $b_e$, breaking its degeneracy with primordial non-Gaussianity $f_\mathrm{NL}$. This enables FRB surveys to access robust, high-precision measurements of inflationary PNG even when $b_e$ is marginalised, significantly enhancing their cosmological utility. Future interferometric FRB observations could thus open a new window into the physics of the early Universe.

FRB色散测量与干涉式夏皮罗延迟之间的互相关为电子偏置$b_e$提供了强大的自校准工具，打破了其与原初非高斯性$f_\mathrm{NL}$之间的简并。这使得即使在对$b_e$进行边缘化的情况下，FRB巡天仍能获得对暴胀原初非高斯性的稳健高精度测量，显著提升了其宇宙学价值。未来的干涉式FRB观测因此有望打开一扇探索早期宇宙物理的新窗口。

Abstract: Fast Radio Bursts (FRBs) carry fossil information about non-Gaussianity generated during inflation. This primordial signal is most accessible on the largest scales, where the scale-dependent bias correction $\propto f_\mathrm{NL}\,H_0^2/k^2$ dominates, but where systematic effects are also strongest. A central challenge is the degeneracy between the intergalactic-medium electron bias $b_e$ and the primordial non-Gaussianity (PNG) signal, which can degrade $σ(f_\mathrm{NL})$ by orders of magnitude when $b_e$ is marginalised. We show this degeneracy can be broken internally by exploiting the cross-power spectrum $C_\ell^{DΔt}$ between the FRB dispersion measure (DM) field and Shapiro timing delays along multiple interferometric sightlines. The DM field traces the biased electron density, while the Shapiro timing signal probes the Newtonian gravitational potential independently of astrophysical bias. Their cross-correlation is directly proportional to $b_e$, independently of the matter power spectrum, providing a self-calibration of the electron bias. We derive $C_\ell^{DΔt}$ analytically in the Limber approximation and find a correlation coefficient $|ρ(\ell)|\approx 0.51$--$0.79$ across $\ell = 2$--$100$. A joint Fisher matrix analysis over $\{f_\mathrm{NL},\,b_e^0,\,z_\mathrm{fb}\}$ shows that including the cross-spectrum reduces $σ(b_e^0)$ by a factor of $2.1$--$5.1$ relative to a DM-only analysis. After full marginalisation, the joint analysis recovers $σ(f_\mathrm{NL})$ within a factor of $1.0$--$1.9$ of the fixed-bias benchmark, compared with $1.7$--$3.3$ degradation without the cross-spectrum. For a shallow survey with a 500\,AU baseline and $10^4$ FRBs, the joint constraint achieves $σ(f_\mathrm{NL})\approx 790$, within 4\% of the fixed-bias result and a factor $3.3$ better than the marginalised DM-only case.

### [41] [Poisson Vertex Algebra of Seiberg-Witten Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03500)
*Ahsan Z. Khan*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We propose an explicit Poisson vertex algebra $A$ that captures the holomorphic-topological observables in pure $\mathcal{N}=2$ $SU(2)$ gauge theory to all perturbative orders, compute its Hilbert-Poincar\'e series matching the Schur index, and introduce a differential $Q_{\text{inst}}$ conjectured to encode instanton corrections, computing its cohomology as a candidate for the full non-perturbative observable algebra.

我们提出了一个明确的泊松顶点代数 $A$，它在所有微扰阶次上捕捉纯 $\mathcal{N}=2$ $SU(2)$ 规范理论中的全纯-拓扑可观测量，计算了其希尔伯特-庞加莱级数并匹配了Schur指标，并引入了一个微分 $Q_{\text{inst}}$，推测其编码瞬子修正，并计算了其上同调作为完整非微扰可观测量代数的一个候选。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: In four-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=2$ supersymmetric theories, certain protected sectors can be described by simpler algebraic structures such as vertex algebras. The holomorphic-topological twist yields a sector governed by a Poisson vertex algebra (PVA) in the $Q$-cohomology. For the pure $SU(2)$ $\mathcal{N}=2$ gauge theory (i.e., Seiberg-Witten theory without matter), a complete description of this PVA including both perturbative and non-perturbative contributions is lacking. This paper aims to construct such an algebra explicitly and refine known supersymmetric indices like the Schur index with more detailed algebraic data.

在四维 $\mathcal{N}=2$ 超对称理论中，某些受保护的扇区可以用更简单的代数结构（如顶点代数）来描述。全纯-拓扑扭动生成的扇区由 $Q$-上同调中的泊松顶点代数（Poisson vertex algebra, PVA）控制。对于纯 $SU(2)$ $\mathcal{N}=2$ 规范理论（即无物质的Seiberg-Witten理论），目前尚缺乏包含微扰和非微扰贡献的PVA的完整描述。本文旨在显式构造这样的代数，并利用更详细的代数数据完善诸如Schur指标等已知的超对称指标。

Method: The authors define a Poisson vertex algebra $A$ via generators and relations motivated by the field content and symmetries of pure $\mathcal{N}=2$ $SU(2)$ gauge theory. They compute the Hilbert-Poincar\'e series of $A$ using standard techniques in PVA theory. To incorporate instanton effects, they postulate a differential $Q_{\text{inst}}$ acting on $A$, constructed based on expected properties of instanton operators, and compute the cohomology $H^\bullet(A, Q_{\text{inst}})$ explicitly.

作者通过由纯 $\mathcal{N}=2$ $SU(2)$ 规范理论的场内容和对称性启发的生成元与关系来定义泊松顶点代数 $A$。他们使用PVA理论中的标准技术计算 $A$ 的希尔伯特-庞加莱级数。为了纳入瞬子效应，他们假设了一个作用在 $A$ 上的微分 $Q_{\text{inst}}$，该微分基于对瞬子算符预期性质构建，并显式计算了上同调 $H^\bullet(A, Q_{\text{inst}})$。

Result: The Hilbert-Poincar\'e series of the proposed Poisson vertex algebra $A$ matches the Schur index of the pure $SU(2)$ theory, confirming its correctness at the perturbative level. The cohomology of the differential $Q_{\text{inst}}$, $H^0(A, Q_{\text{inst}})$, is shown to be one-dimensional, consistent with the expectation that the unique vacuum is the only non-perturbatively stable state in the holomorphic-topological sector. Higher cohomology groups vanish or are trivial, supporting the conjecture that $Q_{\text{inst}}$ correctly models instanton-induced corrections.

所提出的泊松顶点代数 $A$ 的希尔伯特-庞加莱级数与纯 $SU(2)$ 理论的Schur指标相匹配，确认了其在微扰层面的正确性。微分 $Q_{\text{inst}}$ 的上同调 $H^0(A, Q_{\text{inst}})$ 被证明是一维的，这与唯一真空是全纯-拓扑扇区中唯一的非微扰稳定态的预期一致。更高阶上同调群消失或为平凡，支持 $Q_{\text{inst}}$ 正确建模瞬子诱导修正的猜想。

Conclusion: An explicit Poisson vertex algebra $A$ is constructed as the space of perturbative holomorphic-topological observables in pure $\mathcal{N}=2$ $SU(2)$ gauge theory. Its Hilbert-Poincar\'e series refines the Schur index. A conjectural differential $Q_{\text{inst}}$ is introduced to account for instanton effects, and its cohomology provides a candidate for the non-perturbative algebra of observables. This framework offers a new algebraic approach to studying non-perturbative aspects of $\mathcal{N}=2$ theories.

构造了一个明确的泊松顶点代数 $A$ 作为纯 $\mathcal{N}=2$ $SU(2)$ 规范理论中微扰全纯-拓扑可观测量空间。其希尔伯特-庞加莱级数细化了Schur指标。引入了一个推测性的微分 $Q_{\text{inst}}$ 来解释瞬子效应，其上同调为可观测量的非微扰代数提供了一个候选。该框架为研究 $\mathcal{N}=2$ 理论的非微扰方面提供了新的代数方法。

Abstract: The space of local operators in the $Q$-cohomology of the holomorphic-topological supercharge in a four-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=2$ theory carries the structure of a Poisson vertex algebra. This note studies the Poisson vertex algebra associated to the pure $\mathcal{N}=2$ gauge theory with gauge group $SU(2)$. We propose an explicit Poisson vertex algebra $A$, claimed to be isomorphic to the algebra of holomorphic-topological observables to all orders in perturbation theory. We compute the Hilbert-Poincaré series of $A$ and show that it refines the Schur index of the pure $SU(2)$ theory. We show that $A$ admits a further differential $Q_{\text{inst}}$ which we hypothesize captures non-perturbative corrections, and compute the cohomology of this differential. We thus present an explicit candidate for the space of non-perturbative holomorphic-topological observables of Seiberg-Witten theory.

### [42] [How to Expose a Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03720)
*Ashoke Sen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper explores how a black hole in string theory can transition smoothly into a normal quantum state via a spatially varying dilaton background, avoiding both adiabatic breakdown and premature evaporation by appropriately tuning the dilaton profile.

根据论文，通过在适当调节的稀释子场背景下，弦论中的黑洞可以平滑地转变为无事件视界的普通量子态，从而避免绝热近似失效和过早蒸发问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand how black holes in string theory can be continuously connected to ordinary quantum systems (e.g., D-branes and strings) via the Horowitz-Polchinski correspondence principle, particularly in configurations where the dilaton varies in space-time, potentially allowing a black hole to lose its horizon and become a visible quantum state.

研究动机在于理解弦论中的黑洞如何通过Horowitz-Polchinski对应原理与普通量子系统（如D-膜和基本弦）连续连接，尤其是在稀释子随空间变化的情况下，黑洞可能失去视界并转化为可观测的量子态。

Method: The authors analyze the dynamics of a black hole moving through a spacetime with a spatially varying dilaton field. They examine the constraints imposed by the adiabatic approximation, gravitational collapse, and black hole evaporation timescales, and construct a background where the dilaton gradient is tuned to allow a gentle transition without violating these physical requirements.

作者分析了黑洞在稀释子场空间变化背景下的运动动力学，考察了绝热近似、引力坍缩和黑洞蒸发时间尺度所施加的约束，并构造了一个稀释子梯度被恰当调节的背景，以实现平缓过渡而不违反这些物理要求。

Result: It is shown that there exists a range of dilaton profiles for which the adiabatic condition holds, no spontaneous black hole formation occurs, and the traversal time is shorter than the evaporation time—enabling the black hole to transition into a horizonless quantum state.

研究发现存在一类稀释子分布，其满足绝热条件、不引发自发黑洞形成，且穿越时间短于蒸发时间，从而使黑洞可转变为无视界的量子态。

Conclusion: By appropriately choosing the spacetime-dependent dilaton background, a black hole can undergo a smooth transition to a normal quantum system without an event horizon, supporting the idea that black holes and quantum systems in string theory are two limits of the same underlying theory.

通过恰当选取依赖时空的稀释子背景，黑洞可平滑过渡为无事件视界的普通量子系统，支持了弦论中黑洞与量子系统属于同一理论不同极限的观点。

Abstract: According to the correspondence principle of Horowitz and Polchinski, many black holes in string theory are continuously deformed to usual quantum systems involving D-branes and fundamental strings when the string coupling becomes sufficiently small. Therefore if we consider a configuration in space-time where the dilaton varies over an appropriate range, then a black hole moving in such a background will smoothly transition from the black hole state to a normal quantum state whose microstates are not hidden behind an event horizon. The possible obstruction to this mechanism comes from the fact that if the dilaton varies too fast then the adiabatic approximation may break down and / or the ambient space-time itself may collapse to a black hole and get hidden from the asymptotic observer. On the other hand, if the dilaton varies too slowly then the time that it takes for the black hole to travel the required distance will exceed the evaporation time of the black hole. We show that by choosing the background appropriately these obstructions can be avoided and a gentle motion towards the weak coupling region will convert the black hole into a normal quantum state without an event horizon.

</details>


### [43] [Causality, the Kovtun-Son-Starinets bound, and a novel sum rule for spectral densities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04222)
*G. Yu. Prokhorov,O. V. Teryaev*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper demonstrates that the shear viscosity to entropy density ratio for Unruh radiation near a black hole horizon is universal and given by $ \eta/s = 1/(4\pi c_s^2) $, linking the Kovtun-Son-Starinets (KSS) bound directly to causality via the speed of sound $ c_s $. It further shows that the bulk-to-shear viscosity ratio saturates a known holographic bound and derives a new sum rule from isotropy in Rindler space connecting spectral densities $ c^{(0)}(\mu) $ and $ c^{(2)}(\mu) $, validated for CFTs and free Dirac fields. This sum rule supports Pascal's law and resembles the Burkhardt-Cottingham sum rule, offering insights into transport in highly accelerated systems like quark-gluon plasma.

本文直接证明了在黑洞视界附近有限距离处，Unruh辐射的剪切粘度与熵密度之比具有普适性，且满足关系式 $ \eta/s = 1/(4\pi c_s^2) $，其中 $ c_s $ 为声速。由于因果性要求 $ c_s^2 \leq 1 $，该结果建立了著名的Kovtun-Son-Starinets（KSS）界限与因果性的深刻联系。此外，文章还表明体粘度与剪切粘度之比饱和了全息方法所预言的另一个关于体粘度的已知界限。基于Rindler空间中热辐射各向同性的条件，作者导出了一个新颖的求和规则，关联谱密度 $ c^{(0)}(\mu) $ 和 $ c^{(2)}(\mu) $，并在任意维度的共形场论和自由有质量Dirac场中显式验证了其成立。该求和规则保证了帕斯卡定律的有效性，并与自旋依赖部分子分布中的Burkhardt-Cottingham求和规则有相似之处，为理解极端加速介质（如相对论重离子碰撞中产生的夸克-胶子等离子体）中的耗散输运现象提供了新视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand the universality of transport coefficients like $ \eta/s $ in quantum field theories under extreme conditions, particularly near horizons where Unruh radiation dominates, and to explore whether fundamental bounds such as the KSS bound arise from deeper physical principles like causality and symmetry.

旨在理解在极端条件下（特别是在视界附近以Unruh辐射为主导的区域）量子场论中输运系数（如 $ \eta/s $）的普适性，并探究诸如Kovtun-Son-Starinets（KSS）界限之类的根本性界限是否源于因果性、对称性等更深层的物理原理。

Method: Using quantum field theory in curved spacetime, specifically in Rindler space to model acceleration horizons, the authors compute spectral representations of stress-energy correlators. They derive transport coefficients from Kubo formulas, analyze the implications of local isotropy of Unruh radiation, and establish a sum rule for spectral densities $ c^{(0)}(\mu) $ and $ c^{(2)}(\mu) $. The results are verified in specific examples: conformal field theories and free massive Dirac fields in arbitrary dimensions.

利用弯曲时空中的量子场论（特别采用Rindler空间来模拟加速度视界），作者计算了应力-能量关联函数的谱表示，通过Kubo公式推导出输运系数，分析Unruh辐射局域各向同性的物理后果，并建立谱密度 $ c^{(0)}(\mu) $ 和 $ c^{(2)}(\mu) $ 之间的求和规则。结果在两个具体例子中得到验证：任意维度的共形场论和自由有质量Dirac场。

Result: The local shear viscosity to entropy density ratio is shown to be $ \eta/s = 1/(4\pi c_s^2) $, which reduces to the KSS bound $ 1/(4\pi) $ when $ c_s^2 = 1 $; causality enforces $ c_s^2 \leq 1 $, thus linking the KSS bound to fundamental causality. The bulk-to-shear viscosity ratio saturates a known holographic bound. A novel sum rule $ \int [c^{(0)}(\mu) - c^{(2)}(\mu)] d\mu = 0 $ is derived from isotropy in Rindler space and confirmed in both CFT and free Dirac field cases. This sum rule ensures mechanical equilibrium (Pascal's law) and parallels the Burkhardt-Cottingham sum rule.

研究发现局域剪切粘度与熵密度之比为 $ \eta/s = 1/(4\pi c_s^2) $，当 $ c_s^2 = 1 $ 时退化为KSS界限 $ 1/(4\pi) $；而因果性要求 $ c_s^2 \leq 1 $，因此KSS界限被直接与基本因果律联系起来。体粘度与剪切粘度之比饱和了一个已知的全息界限。从Rindler空间中各向同性条件出发，导出了新的求和规则 $ \int [c^{(0)}(\mu) - c^{(2)}(\mu)] d\mu = 0 $，并在共形场论和自由Dirac场情形下得到了验证。此求和规则确保了力学平衡（即帕斯卡定律），并与Burkhardt-Cottingham求和规则具有类比性。

Conclusion: The KSS bound on $ \eta/s $ is not accidental but rooted in causality, revealed through the analysis of Unruh radiation at finite distance from the horizon. The saturation of holographic bounds and the emergence of a new sum rule from isotropy suggest deep connections between hydrodynamics, quantum field theory in curved spacetime, and thermodynamics of accelerated observers. These results provide a new framework for understanding dissipative processes in strongly accelerated media such as quark-gluon plasma.

$ \eta/s $ 的KSS界限并非偶然，而是根植于因果性，这一结论通过分析视界附近有限距离处的Unruh辐射得以揭示。全息界限的饱和以及由各向同性导出的新求和规则，表明流体力学、弯曲时空中的量子场论与加速观测者的热力学之间存在深刻联系。这些结果为理解强加速介质（如夸克-胶子等离子体）中的耗散过程提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We directly show that the local ratio of the shear viscosity to the entropy density for Unruh radiation at a finite distance from the horizon is universal and satisfies the relation $ η/s = 1/(4πc_s^2) $, which involves the speed of sound $ c_s $. Since $ c_s^2 \leq 1 $ by causality, this establishes the close connection between the famous Kovtun-Son-Starinets bound and causality. Moreover, we show that the ratio of bulk to shear viscosity saturates another well-known bound for the bulk viscosity, predicted within holographic approach. We also show that the condition of isotropy of thermal radiation in the Rindler space leads to a novel sum rule relating the $ c^{(0)}(μ) $ and $ c^{(2)}(μ) $ spectral densities, and we explicitly demonstrate its validity for conformal field theory and free massive Dirac fields in any number of dimensions. The sum rule provides the validity of Pascal law and bears some similarity with Burkhardt-Cottingham sum rule for spin-dependent parton distributions. Our result suggests a new perspective on dissipative transport phenomena in media undergoing extreme acceleration, such as quark-gluon plasma created in relativistic heavy-ion collisions.

### [44] [Superradiant Suppression of Non-minimally Coupled Scalar fields for a Rotating Charged dS Black Hole in Conformal Weyl Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04352)
*Owen Gartlan,Jacob March,Leo Rodriguez,Shanshan Rodriguez,Yihan Shen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This study analytically investigates superradiant scattering of massive and massless charged conformally coupled scalar fields in rotating charged de Sitter black holes within General Relativity (GR) and Conformal Weyl Gravity (CWG). For the massless case, a correspondence between the Heun equation and the semiclassical limit of BPZ equations in 2D CFT is used to compute amplification factors; for the massive case, WKB methods yield approximate amplification factors. Suppression of superradiance in CWG compared to GR is found, with exponential suppression $e^{-2\mu \Lambda^{-1/2}}$ in the massive sector in the cosmological region.

本研究在广义相对论（GR）和共形怀尔重力（CWG）中，对旋转带电de Sitter黑洞时空中的带电共形耦合标量场的超辐射散射进行了分析。对于无质量情况，利用Heun方程与二维共形场论中BPZ方程半经典极限之间的对应关系计算放大因子；对于有质量情况，使用WKB方法得到近似结果。发现CWG中相较于GR存在超辐射抑制，特别是在有质量区域的宇宙学区域内呈现指数级抑制 $e^{-2\mu \Lambda^{-1/2}}$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding how alternative gravitational theories modify superradiant phenomena in black hole spacetimes, especially in the presence of a cosmological constant and charge, provides insights into quantum gravity effects, stability of black holes, and potential observational signatures distinguishing GR from modified gravity. The inclusion of both massive and charged scalar fields in de Sitter backgrounds is motivated by connections to cosmology and holography.

理解替代理论如何修改黑洞时空中存在宇宙学常数和电荷情况下的超辐射现象，有助于揭示量子引力效应、黑洞稳定性以及区分广义相对论与修正引力的可观测信号。在de Sitter背景下引入有质量和带电标量场，动机来自宇宙学与全息原理的联系。

Method: For the massless charged conformally coupled scalar field, the authors exploit a recently discovered correspondence between solutions of the Heun equation and the semiclassical limit of Belavin-Polyakov-Zamolodchikov (BPZ) equations in two-dimensional conformal field theory (CFT), enabling controlled expansion of superradiant amplification factors in a small parameter. For the massive case, they apply WKB approximation techniques to derive order-of-magnitude estimates of amplification factors, particularly comparing behavior in the near-horizon region $r_+ \ll r \ll r_c$ to the cosmological region bounded by the outer ($r_+$) and cosmological ($r_c$) horizons.

对于无质量带电共形耦合标量场，作者利用Heun方程解与二维共形场论（CFT）中Belavin-Polyakov-Zamolodchikov（BPZ）方程半经典极限之间的新近发现的对应关系，实现了超辐射放大因子在小参数下的可控展开。对于有质量情况，采用WKB近似方法推导放大因子的数量级估计，特别比较了靠近视界区域 $r_+ \ll r \ll r_c$ 与由外视界($r_+$)和宇宙学视界($r_c$)限定的宇宙学区域的行为。

Result: Superradiant amplification is consistently suppressed in Conformal Weyl Gravity (CWG) relative to General Relativity (GR) across all studied parameter regimes. In the massless case, precise amplification factors are obtained via the Heun-BPZ correspondence. In the massive case, WKB analysis reveals that amplification in the cosmological region is exponentially suppressed by a factor $e^{-2\mu \Lambda^{-1/2}}$, where $\mu$ is the scalar field mass and $\Lambda$ is the cosmological constant, indicating strong damping of superradiant modes in CWG.

在所有研究的参数范围内，共形怀尔重力（CWG）中的超辐射放大始终低于广义相对论（GR）。在无质量情况下，通过Heun-BPZ对应关系获得了精确的放大因子。在有质量情况下，WKB分析显示宇宙学区域内的放大被因子 $e^{-2\mu \Lambda^{-1/2}}$ 指数抑制，其中 $\mu$ 是标量场质量，$\Lambda$ 是宇宙学常数，表明CWG中超辐射模式受到强烈阻尼。

Conclusion: The results demonstrate that higher-derivative terms in Conformal Weyl Gravity lead to significant modifications in superradiant scattering processes around rotating charged de Sitter black holes, resulting in suppression of amplification—especially exponential suppression in the massive scalar case. This suggests enhanced stability of such black holes in CWG and highlights the role of higher-curvature corrections in altering quantum field theoretic phenomena in curved spacetime.

结果表明，共形怀尔重力中的高阶导数项显著改变了旋转带电de Sitter黑洞周围的超辐射散射过程，导致放大效应被抑制——尤其是在有质量标量场情况下出现指数抑制。这暗示了此类黑洞在CWG中具有增强的稳定性，并突显了高曲率修正项在改变弯曲时空中量子场论现象方面的作用。

Abstract: In this study, we present an analytical investigation of the superradiant scattering of a massive charged conformally coupled scalar field in rotating charged $de~Sitter$ black hole spacetimes within two gravitational theories: General Relativity (GR) and fourth-order Conformal (Weyl-squared) Gravity (CWG). For the massless charged conformally coupled scalar, we exploit a recently discovered correspondence between the Heun equation and the semiclassical limit of Belavin-Polyakov-Zamolodchikov (BPZ) equations in two-dimensional conformal field theory to solve for the superradiant amplification factors as controlled expansions in a small parameter scaling. For the massive charged conformally coupled scalar, we use WKB methods to derive an order of magnitude approximation for the amplification factors in the cosmological region in terms of those in the region $r_+\ll r \ll r_c$ where $r_+$ and $r_c$ are the outer and cosmological event horizons, respectively. For both the massless and massive sectors, suppression of superradiant amplification in CWG relative to that in GR is observed across the parameter regimes studied. Particularly, in the massive sector, we find strong exponential suppression of superradiant amplification on the order of $e^{-2μΛ^{-1/2}}$ in the cosmological region.

### [45] [Anomalies in family unification models from bordism classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04393)
*Tsubasa Sugeno,Hiroki Wada*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper investigates sigma model anomalies in four-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=1$ supersymmetric family unification models with target spaces based on $E_7$ and its subgroups, using the bordism classification of invertible field theories. By computing relevant bordism groups via the Atiyah-Hirzebruch spectral sequence, the authors establish the absence of global anomalies, including when symmetries of coset spaces are gauged.

本文研究了基于$E_7$及其子群的四维$\mathcal{N}=1$超对称族统一模型中的σ模型反常，采用可逆场论的配边分类框架。通过使用Atiyah-Hirzebruch谱序列计算相关配边群，作者证明了全局反常（包括在对陪集空间对称性进行规范时产生的反常）的缺失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Family unification models aim to explain the origin of three generations of quarks and leptons, often realized through nonlinear sigma models where fermion generations emerge as superpartners of sigma fields. However, such constructions may suffer from global anomalies that threaten their consistency. The motivation is to rigorously classify and cancel these anomalies—particularly non-perturbative (global) ones—using modern tools like bordism theory, ensuring quantum consistency of these models.

族统一模型试图解释夸克与轻子三代的起源，通常通过非线性σ模型实现，其中费米子代作为σ场的超对称伴子出现。然而，这类构造可能遭受威胁其一致性的全局反常。本研究的动机是利用配边理论等现代工具严格分类并消除这些反常（特别是非微扰的全局反常），以确保模型的量子一致性。

Method: The authors employ the bordism classification of invertible field theories to detect potential global anomalies in $\mathcal{N}=1$ SUSY nonlinear sigma models with target spaces derived from $E_7$ and its subgroups. They compute the relevant bordism groups $\Omega^5_{\text{Spin}}(BG)$ (capturing 5d invertible phases) using the Atiyah-Hirzebruch spectral sequence (AHSS), analyzing both ungauged and gauged settings. In the gauged case, they consider coset spaces $G/H$ and examine anomalies when the isotropy subgroup $H$ is gauged.

作者采用可逆场论的配边分类方法来探测基于$E_7$及其子群的$\mathcal{N}=1$ SUSY非线性σ模型中的潜在全局反常。他们使用Atiyah-Hirzebruch谱序列（AHSS）计算相关的配边群$\Omega^5_{\text{Spin}}(BG)$（捕捉5维可逆相），分析了未规范和已规范两种情形。在规范情形下，考虑了陪集空间$G/H$，并研究当各向同性子群$H$被规范时的反常。

Result: The computation shows that the torsion part of the relevant bordism groups—which classifies global anomalies—vanishes for the considered $E_7$-based models. Specifically, $\Omega^5_{\text{Spin}}(B(G/H))$ contains no torsion, implying the absence of global sigma model anomalies. This result holds even when the isotropy subgroup $H$ is gauged, confirming the quantum consistency of such family unification constructions.

计算表明，对于所考虑的基于$E_7$的模型，相关配边群的挠部分（用于分类全局反常）为零。具体而言，$\Omega^5_{\text{Spin}}(B(G/H))$不含挠元，意味着全局σ模型反常不存在。即使在各向同性子群$H$被规范的情况下，该结果依然成立，证实了此类族统一构造的量子一致性。

Conclusion: Four-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=1$ supersymmetric family unification models with $E_7$-derived target spaces are free of global anomalies, as confirmed by bordism theory. Gauging isotropy subgroups in coset constructions does not introduce global anomalies, ensuring the quantum consistency of these models. This supports their viability as UV-complete frameworks for explaining fermion generations.

基于$E_7$导出目标空间的四维$\mathcal{N}=1$超对称族统一模型在配边理论下被证实无全局反常。在陪集构造中规范各向同性子群不会引入全局反常，确保了这些模型的量子一致性。这支持其作为解释费米子代数的UV完备框架的可行性。

Abstract: We study anomalies in family unification models within the framework of the bordism classification of invertible field theories. These models are based on four-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=1$ supersymmetric nonlinear sigma models, in which the three generations of quarks and leptons arise as superpartners of the sigma model fields. We focus on models whose target spaces are constructed from the exceptional group $E_{7}$ and its subgroups. For the consistency of the theory, sigma model anomalies must be cancelled. We show the absence of global sigma model anomalies, which are encoded in the torsion part of the relevant bordism groups, by explicitly computing these groups using the Atiyah-Hirzebruch spectral sequence. In constructing family unification models, symmetries acting on the coset spaces are gauged, which may introduce additional anomalies. We identify the relevant bordism groups in this setting and demonstrate that no global anomalies arise when the isotropy subgroup of the coset space is gauged.

### [46] [D-instanton Effects on the Holographic Weyl Semimetals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04424)
*Hwajin Eom,Yunseok Seo*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We study D-instanton effects on a holographic Weyl semimetal using a top-down string theory approach, analyzing the phase structure via D7-brane embeddings and uncovering an instanton-induced gapped phase corresponding to a topological insulator, along with anomalous Hall conductivity.

我们采用自上而下的弦论方法研究D瞬子对全息外尔半金属的影响，通过D7膜嵌入分析相结构，发现瞬子诱导的能隙相对应于拓扑绝缘体，并揭示了反常霍尔电导率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding non-perturbative effects such as instantons in strongly coupled Weyl semimetals remains challenging. Holography provides a powerful tool to explore such systems via dual gravitational descriptions, particularly in regimes where traditional field theory methods fail. The motivation is to clarify how D-instantons influence the phase structure and transport properties of a holographic Weyl semimetal.

理解瞬子等非微扰效应在外尔半金属中的作用仍然具有挑战性。全息原理通过对偶引力描述为此类强耦合系统提供了有力工具，尤其是在传统场论方法失效的区域。本研究旨在阐明D瞬子如何影响全息外尔半金属的相结构和输运性质。

Method: We employ a top-down holographic construction based on D3-D7 brane systems with D-instanton corrections. The phase diagram is derived from the free energy of probe D7-brane embeddings in the presence of instanton number, temperature $T$, electron mass $m$, and Weyl parameter $\mu_W$. Non-linear conductivities are computed using regularity conditions on the worldvolume gauge fields of the D7 brane in the bulk.

我们采用基于D3-D7膜系统的自上而下全息构造，并包含D瞬子修正。相图由探针D7膜嵌入的自由能得出，依赖于瞬子数、温度$T$、电子质量$m$和外尔参数$\mu_W$。非线性电导率通过对体中D7膜上的规范场施加正则性条件计算得到。

Result: The free energy analysis reveals a rich phase structure as a function of $m/\mu_W$, instanton number, and $T/\mu_W$. We identify a novel gapped phase at finite instanton density, which exhibits properties consistent with a topological insulator. Anomalous Hall conductivity is observed due to symmetry-breaking patterns induced by instantons, and non-linear responses are derived from the regularity of the bulk gauge field solutions.

自由能分析揭示了作为$m/\mu_W$、瞬子数和$T/\mu_W$函数的丰富相结构。我们在有限瞬子密度下发现了一种新的能隙相，其性质与拓扑绝缘体一致。由于瞬子引起的对称性破缺模式，观察到反常霍尔电导率，并从体规范场解的正则性推导出非线性响应。

Conclusion: D-instantons play a crucial role in modifying the phase structure of holographic Weyl semimetals, inducing a topologically non-trivial gapped phase analogous to a topological insulator. This work demonstrates the importance of non-perturbative stringy effects in strongly correlated quantum materials via gauge/gravity duality.

D瞬子在改变全息外尔半金属的相结构中起着关键作用，诱导出类似于拓扑绝缘体的非平庸能隙相。这项工作展示了通过规范/引力对偶，非微扰弦效应在强关联量子材料中的重要性。

Abstract: We investigate D-insatnton effects on the holographic Weyl semimetal in top-down approach. From the free energy of the D7 brane embedding solutions, we get phase diagram in terms of the electron mass, instanton number, and temperature in the unit of the weyl parameter. We calculate non-linear conductivities from the regularity condition of the probe D7 brane and investgate anomalous Hall phenomena in the boundary system. From the study of the phase diagram, we suggest the gaped phase induced by the instanton to a topological insulator.

### [47] [The Gauge-Invariant Mass Function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04569)
*Kang-Sin Choi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We demonstrate that renormalization in gauge theories provides a gauge-invariant definition of mass at every virtuality, extending the concept of mass beyond on-shell particles and rendering virtual particles as well-defined as real ones through kinematic distinctions.

我们证明，在规范理论中，重整化为每个虚动量提供了规范不变的质量定义，将质量概念从壳粒子扩展到离壳情况，使得虚粒子与实粒子一样明确，其区别仅为运动学上的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: In gauge theories, while the pole mass (on-shell mass) is known to be gauge-invariant, the notion of mass for off-shell (virtual) particles has traditionally lacked a gauge-invariant formulation. This ambiguity complicates physical interpretations of propagators and effective descriptions of quantum fields away from the mass shell. The motivation is to establish a consistent, gauge-invariant meaning for the mass of a virtual particle throughout its momentum evolution.

在规范理论中，虽然极点质量（壳上质量）是规范不变的，但对离壳（虚）粒子的质量长期以来缺乏规范不变的定义。这种模糊性给传播子的物理解释以及远离质量壳的量子场有效描述带来了困难。本文的动机是建立一个在整个动量演化过程中对虚粒子质量具有规范不变性的统一描述。

Method: We employ the framework of operator renormalization in gauge theories, identifying a gauge-invariant renormalized mass function $m(p^2)$ defined at each virtuality $p^2$. This is achieved by constructing a gauge-invariant effective action or by analyzing the structure of the exact propagator in conjunction with a gauge-invariant vertex function. Renormalization group methods are used to ensure consistency across scales.

我们采用规范理论中的算符重整化框架，识别出在每个虚动量$p^2$处定义的规范不变重整化质量函数$m(p^2)$。这通过构造规范不变的有效作用量，或结合规范不变顶点函数分析精确传播子的结构来实现。同时使用重整化群方法确保跨能标的一致性。

Result: A gauge-invariant mass function $m(p^2)$ is explicitly constructed, valid for all virtualities, which reduces to the pole mass at $p^2 = m^2_{\text{pole}}$. A corresponding gauge-invariant vertex is also defined. The full propagator and vertex structure are thus rendered physically meaningful off-shell, showing that virtual particles carry a well-defined, scale-dependent mass.

明确构造了一个规范不变的质量函数$m(p^2)$，适用于所有虚动量，并在$p^2 = m^{2}_{\text{pole}}$时还原为极点质量。同时定义了相应的规范不变顶点。完整的传播子和顶点结构因此在离壳情况下也具有物理意义，表明虚粒子携带一个明确定义的、依赖于能标的质量。

Conclusion: The distinction between on-shell and off-shell particles in gauge theories is not due to a lack of definability of mass, but rather a kinematic one. Renormalization provides a gauge-invariant trajectory of mass $m(p^2)$, making virtual particles as physically meaningful as real ones. This redefines our understanding of particle propagation in quantum field theory.

规范理论中壳上与离壳粒子的区别并非源于质量不可定义，而仅仅是运动学上的。重整化提供了一条规范不变的质量轨迹$m(p^2)$，使虚粒子与实粒子同样具有物理意义。这重新定义了我们对量子场论中粒子传播的理解。

Abstract: In gauge theories, the mass of a field has been regarded as a purely on-shell concept: the pole mass is gauge-invariant, but the off-shell propagator has had no gauge-invariant definition of mass. We show that renormalization defines a gauge-invariant mass function at every virtuality, together with a gauge-invariant vertex. The virtual particle becomes as well defined as the on-shell one: the distinction is not dynamical but purely kinematic.

</details>


### [48] [New Solutions for RG Equations in QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04766)
*R. M. Iakhibbaev,D. I. Kazakov,D. M. Tolkachev*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We present analytical solutions of renormalization group equations in QCD that explicitly sum leading, subleading, and higher-order logarithms to all orders in perturbation theory, reproducing the inverse logarithm expansion and enabling improved asymptotic behavior.

我们提出了QCD中重整化群方程的解析解，显式地在微扰论的所有阶上对领头、次领头及更高阶对数项进行求和，重现了逆对数展开，并实现了渐近行为的改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The precise understanding of running couplings and Green functions in QCD requires resummation of large logarithmic corrections beyond fixed-order perturbation theory, especially in the asymptotic regime where $\alpha_s$ becomes small but logarithms $\ln \mu$ grow.

精确理解QCD中的跑动耦合和格林函数需要在固定阶微扰论之外对大对数修正进行重求和，特别是在$\alpha_s$变小但对数$\ln \mu$增大的渐近区域。

Method: We solve the renormalization group equations analytically in the asymptotic regime by constructing explicit solutions that systematically sum leading logarithms (LL), next-to-leading logarithms (NLL), and so on, using iterative integration and recursive structures of the beta function and anomalous dimensions in QCD.

我们在渐近区域通过构造显式解来解析求解重整化群方程，利用QCD中beta函数和反常量纲的迭代积分与递归结构，系统地对领头对数（LL）、次领头对数（NLL）等进行求和。

Result: We obtain closed-form analytical expressions for the running coupling $\alpha_s(\mu)$ and Green functions that incorporate all-order logarithmic resummation. These solutions naturally reproduce the standard $1/\ln \mu$ expansion and allow for further improvement via Borel summation or optimal truncation.

我们得到了包含全阶对数重求和的跑动耦合$\alpha_s(\mu)$和格林函数的闭式解析表达式。这些解自然重现了标准的$1/\ln \mu$展开，并可通过Borel求和或最优截断进一步改进。

Conclusion: Analytical resummation of logarithmic corrections in QCD via exact RG solutions enhances predictive power in the asymptotic regime and provides a systematic framework beyond conventional perturbation theory.

通过精确的RG解对QCD中的对数修正进行解析重求和，增强了在渐近区域的预测能力，并提供了超越传统微扰论的系统性框架。

Abstract: We construct simple analytical solutions of renormalization group equations for the running coupling and for the Green functions in QCD in the asymptotic regime. These solutions have an explicit form and subsequently sum up the leading, subleading, and so on logarithms in all orders of PT. They easily reproduce the inverse logarithm expansion and allow for further summation and improvement of the asymptotic behaviour.

</details>


### [49] [Exponentially Long Evaporation of Noncommutative Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04774)
*Pei-Ming Ho,Wei-Hsiang Shao,Takuya Yoda*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We study Hawking radiation in noncommutative spacetime for a dynamical black hole formed via matter shell collapse, showing that spacetime noncommutativity introduces momentum-dependent shifts in the collapsing shell and modifies the field-geometry interaction. As a result, Hawking radiation decays after the scrambling time, leading to exponentially long evaporation.

我们研究了非对易时空中由物质壳坍缩形成的动态黑洞的霍金辐射，发现时空非对易性引入了依赖于辐射模式动量的壳层有效位移，并改变了辐射场与背景几何的相互作用。结果表明，霍金辐射在散射时间后显著衰减，导致蒸发时间呈指数增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Hawking's original derivation assumes a commutative spacetime and local quantum field theory; however, in quantum gravity scenarios such as noncommutative geometry, spacetime may exhibit intrinsic nonlocality. This raises questions about the robustness of Hawking radiation—whether it survives when locality is violated. We aim to investigate how noncommutative spacetime alters the emission process, especially for dynamical black holes where backreaction and time dependence are crucial.

霍金的原始推导基于对易时空和局域量子场论，但在非对易几何等量子引力框架中，时空可能具有内在非局域性。这引发了关于霍金辐射鲁棒性的疑问——当局域性被破坏时它是否依然存在。我们旨在研究非对易时空如何改变辐射过程，尤其是在需考虑反作用和时间依赖性的动态黑洞情形下。

Method: We model the black hole formation through the collapse of a spherically symmetric matter shell in a noncommutative spacetime background, employing a star-product ($\star$-product) deformation of the algebra of functions on spacetime. The dynamics of a scalar field representing Hawking radiation is studied using a modified Klein-Gordon equation that incorporates noncommutative corrections. The interaction between the radiation mode and the collapsing shell is analyzed via a momentum-dependent shift in the effective trajectory of the shell, derived from the nonlocal nature of $\star$-multiplication. We compute the Bogoliubov coefficients to determine the particle production spectrum and track its evolution beyond the scrambling time.

我们通过在非对易时空背景下建模球对称物质壳的坍缩来描述黑洞形成，采用时空函数代数的星积（$\star$-product）变形。通过引入非对易修正项的修正克莱因-戈登方程，研究代表霍金辐射的标量场的动力学。利用由$\star$-乘法非局域性导出的动量依赖性位移，分析辐射模式与坍缩壳之间的相互作用。通过计算Bogoliubov系数确定粒子产生谱，并追踪其在散射时间之后的演化。

Result: Spacetime noncommutativity induces an effective shift in the trajectory of the collapsing shell proportional to the momentum $p$ of the outgoing Hawking mode: $\Delta r \sim \theta p$, where $\theta$ encodes the noncommutativity scale. This modifies the near-horizon field dynamics and breaks strict locality. Consequently, the Bogoliubov coefficients decay exponentially after the scrambling time $t_\text{scr} \sim \beta \log S$, where $\beta$ is the inverse temperature and $S$ the entropy. The total evaporation time becomes $t_\text{evap} \sim \exp(S)$, in contrast to the standard $t_\text{evap} \sim S^2$ scaling.

时空非对易性诱导坍缩壳轨迹产生一个正比于出射霍金模式动量$p$的有效位移：$\Delta r \sim \theta p$，其中$\theta$表征非对易尺度。这改变了近视界区域的场动力学并破坏严格局域性。因此，在散射时间$t_\text{scr} \sim \beta \log S$之后，Bogoliubov系数呈指数衰减。总蒸发时间为$t_\text{evap} \sim \exp(S)$，与标准的$t_\text{evap} \sim S^2$标度形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: In noncommutative spacetime, Hawking radiation is sensitive to Planck-scale nonlocality, invalidating the assumption of UV-insensitivity in conventional derivations. The momentum-dependent interaction between radiation modes and the collapsing geometry leads to strong suppression of late-time emission, resulting in an exponentially long evaporation process. This suggests that information may be preserved over much longer timescales, potentially offering a new perspective on the black hole information paradox within noncommutative quantum gravity.

在非对易时空中，霍金辐射对普朗克尺度的非局域性敏感，破坏了传统推导中紫外不敏感性的假设。辐射模式与坍缩几何之间的动量依赖性相互作用导致晚期辐射被强烈抑制，从而产生指数级长的蒸发过程。这表明信息可能在更长时间尺度上得以保存，为非对易量子引力框架下的黑洞信息悖论提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We investigate Hawking radiation in noncommutative spacetime. For a dynamical black hole formed by the collapse of a matter shell, we demonstrate that spacetime noncommutativity modifies the interaction between the radiation field and the background geometry. In particular, the collapsing shell is effectively shifted by an amount proportional to the momentum of an outgoing Hawking mode. While the nonlocality inherent in noncommutative spacetime invalidates the conventional arguments for the robustness of Hawking radiation, the radiation decays substantially after the scrambling time, resulting in an exponentially long evaporation time.

</details>


### [50] [Planar AdS multi-NUT spacetimes and Kaluza-Klein multi-monopoles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04817)
*Cristóbal Corral,Cristián Erices,Daniel Flores-Alfonso,Benjamín Hernández*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper explores the construction of planar anti-de Sitter (AdS) spacetimes with multiple NUT charges, which are obstructed in standard Einstein gravity. Two approaches are proposed: one using axion fields in a momentum relaxation setup, and another involving quadratic-curvature corrections in Einstein gravity. As a byproduct, multi-magnetic-charge Kaluza-Klein monopoles in AdS are also presented.

本文探讨了在标准爱因斯坦引力中受阻的、具有多个NUT荷的平面反德西特（AdS）时空的构造。提出了两种方法：一种是在动量弛豫模型中引入具有轴子构型的标量场，另一种是在包含二次曲率修正的爱因斯坦引力中实现类似构型。此外，还顺带构造了具有多个磁荷的AdS版本Kaluza-Klein磁单极。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: In higher-dimensional Einstein-AdS gravity, while rotating planar black holes can be constructed via large-gauge transformations, including multiple NUT parameters is problematic due to strong constraints from vacuum field equations. This limits the study of holographic systems with more than one NUT charge, which may encode interesting topological and thermodynamic properties. The authors aim to circumvent these obstructions and enable the exploration of such configurations in holography.

在高维Einstein-AdS引力中，虽然可通过大规范变换构造带旋转参数的平面黑洞，但引入多个NUT参数会因真空场方程的强约束而受阻，限制了对具有多个NUT荷的全息系统的探索，而这类系统可能蕴含有趣的拓扑与热力学性质。作者旨在克服这些障碍，推动此类构型在全息中的研究。

Method: First, they introduce massless scalar fields with linearly dependent axionic profiles on spatial coordinates—commonly used in momentum relaxation models—which break translational symmetry and allow solutions with multiple NUT charges in pure AdS. Second, they consider Einstein gravity extended with quadratic-curvature terms (e.g., Gauss-Bonnet or $R^2$ corrections), where higher-derivative contributions relax the usual integrability conditions, enabling multi-NUT solutions. Both methods are applied to construct planar AdS geometries with flat horizons and multiple NUT parameters.

首先，引入在空间坐标上线性依赖的无质量轴子型标量场——常见于动量弛豫模型——破坏平移对称性，从而在纯AdS中允许含多个NUT荷的解。其次，考虑包含二次曲率项（如Gauss-Bonnet或$R^2$修正）的爱因斯坦引力，其中高阶导数项放松了通常的可积性条件，使多NUT解成为可能。两种方法均用于构造具平坦视界和多个NUT参数的平面AdS几何。

Result: Explicit planar AdS spacetime solutions with multiple NUT charges are constructed in both the axion model and the quadratic-curvature gravity framework. These solutions evade the no-go results of vacuum Einstein-AdS gravity. Additionally, the authors present planar Kaluza-Klein monopole solutions in AdS with independent magnetic charges, generalizing known single-charge configurations.

在轴子模型与二次曲率引力框架中，均成功构造出显式的含多个NUT荷的平面AdS时空解，规避了纯Einstein-AdS引力中的否决结果。此外，作者还给出了AdS中具有独立磁荷的平面Kaluza-Klein磁单极解，推广了已知的单荷情形。

Conclusion: The inclusion of either axion fields or higher-curvature corrections enables the existence of planar AdS spacetimes with multiple NUT parameters, opening new avenues for studying holography with nontrivial topology and mixed gravitational charges. These results suggest that generalized gravitational theories or symmetry-breaking matter content can significantly enrich the landscape of exact solutions in AdS/CFT.

引入轴子场或高曲率修正可使具多个NUT参数的平面AdS时空得以存在，为研究具有非平凡拓扑与混合引力荷的全息对偶开辟了新路径。结果表明，广义引力理论或破缺对称性的物质内容能显著丰富AdS/CFT中精确解的景观。

Abstract: In higher-dimensional Einstein-AdS gravity, it is well known that planar and static anti-de Sitter black holes can be endowed with multiple rotation parameters via a large-gauge transformation. However, a similar prescription fails when multiple NUT parameters are added, thereby obstructing the study of holographic properties with more than one NUT charge. To pave the way towards this direction, we construct explicit planar AdS spacetimes having multiple NUT parameters in two simple ways that allow one to circumvent the strong restrictions imposed by the vacuum field equations. First, motivated by momentum relaxation holographic models, we construct multi-NUT spaces in AdS with flat horizons by adding free scalar fields possessing an axionic profile. In our second approach, we build similar configurations in Einstein gravity with quadratic-curvature corrections. As a byproduct, we end by presenting planar versions of the Kaluza-Klein monopole in AdS with different magnetic charges.

</details>

### [51] [Sign-Locked Gravitational Baryogenesis from Bulk Viscosity and Cosmological Particle Creation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03348)
*Yakov Mandel*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper presents a concrete model of gravitational baryogenesis in which bulk viscosity in the early radiation-dominated universe induces a monotonic Ricci scalar time derivative ($\dot R > 0$), enabling efficient baryon asymmetry generation via the interaction $\mathcal{L}_{\rm int}=(c/M^2)\,\partial_μR\,J^μ_{B-L}$. The irreversible entropy production from viscosity avoids cancellation issues, and successful baryogenesis with $η \sim 10^{-11}$ is achieved for $ξ \sim 10^{-4}$--$10^{-3}$, consistent with EFT and cosmological constraints.

本文提出了一种具体的引力重子生成模型，其中早期辐射主导宇宙的体粘滞性导致单调递增的里奇标量时间导数（$\dot R > 0$），从而通过相互作用项 $\mathcal{L}_{\rm int}=(c/M^2)\,\partial_μR\,J^μ_{B-L}$ 高效产生重子不对称性。粘滞引起的不可逆熵产生避免了符号振荡源的抵消问题，在 $ξ \sim 10^{-4}$--$10^{-3}$ 的参数范围内成功复现观测到的重子不对称度 $η \sim 10^{-11}$，且满足EFT和宇宙学约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Gravitational baryogenesis typically suffers from suppression due to oscillatory or sign-changing $\partial_0 R$, which leads to cancellations in the source term for baryon number violation. The authors aim to construct a robust, thermodynamically motivated mechanism that generates a monotonic, sign-definite $\dot R$ to avoid such cancellations. They explore bulk viscosity — a well-known source of entropy production — as a means to break time-reversal symmetry and drive irreversible dynamics in the early universe.

引力重子生成通常因 $\partial_0 R$ 振荡或变号而导致源项抵消，抑制重子数产生。作者旨在构建一个具有热力学基础的机制，以产生单调且符号确定的 $\dot R$ 来避免此类抵消。他们探索体粘滞性——一种已知的熵产生机制——作为打破时间反演对称性、驱动早期宇宙不可逆动力学的手段。

Method: The authors consider a near-radiation-dominated universe with effective pressure $p_{\rm eff} = p - 3\zeta H$, where $\zeta = \xi \rho / H$ is the bulk viscosity coefficient. They compute the evolution of the Ricci scalar $R$ and its time derivative $\dot R$ in this background. Using the interaction Lagrangian $\mathcal{L}_{\rm int} = (c/M^2)\,\partial_\mu R\, J^\mu_{B-L}$, they derive the baryon asymmetry $η$ by solving the Boltzmann equation during the epoch around decoupling temperature $T_D$. Entropy dilution from the extended viscous phase is included, and consistency with EFT validity ($M \ll \bar M_{\rm Pl}$) and cosmological bounds (e.g., $N_{\rm eff}$, BBN) is imposed to determine viable parameter regions.

作者考虑一个有效压强为 $p_{\rm eff} = p - 3\zeta H$ 的近辐射主导宇宙，其中体粘滞系数为 $\zeta = \xi \rho / H$。他们在该背景下计算里奇标量 $R$ 及其时间导数 $\dot R$ 的演化。利用相互作用拉格朗日量 $\mathcal{L}_{\rm int} = (c/M^2)\,\partial_\mu R\, J^\mu_{B-L}$，通过求解散射温度 $T_D$ 附近的玻尔兹曼方程推导重子不对称度 $η$。研究包含了来自延长粘滞相的熵稀释效应，并施加EFT有效性（$M \ll \bar M_{\rm Pl}$）和宇宙学约束（如 $N_{\rm eff}$、BBN）来确定可行参数区域。

Result: For $ξ > 0$, one obtains $R \neq 0$, $\dot R > 0$, and a baryon asymmetry scaling as $η \propto ξ T_D^5 / (M^2 \bar M_{\rm Pl}^3)$. Successful baryogenesis yielding $η_{\rm obs} \simeq 8.6\times10^{-11}$ is achieved for $ξ \sim 10^{-4}$--$10^{-3}$, $T_D \sim 10^{12}$--$10^{14}\,{\rm GeV}$, and $M \sim 10^{15}$--$10^{16}\,{\rm GeV}$, while respecting EFT control and cosmological limits. A GUT-scale particle creation sector naturally motivates the required $ξ$ range. However, higher-derivative instabilities in standard gravitational baryogenesis are acknowledged, suggesting the need for UV completions or stabilization mechanisms.

当 $ξ > 0$ 时，得到 $R \neq 0$、$\dot R > 0$，且重子不对称度按 $η \propto ξ T_D^5 / (M^2 \bar M_{\rm Pl}^3)$ 缩放。在 $ξ \sim 10^{-4}$--$10^{-3}$、$T_D \sim 10^{12}$--$10^{14}\,{\rm GeV}$、$M \sim 10^{15}$--$10^{16}\,{\rm GeV}$ 的参数范围内，可成功实现 $η_{\rm obs} \simeq 8.6\times10^{-11}$ 的重子生成，同时满足EFT控制和宇宙学限制。GUT尺度的粒子产生机制自然地支持所需的 $ξ$ 范围。然而，标准引力重子生成中的高阶导数不稳定性仍被指出，提示需要UV完备化或稳定化机制。

Conclusion: Bulk viscous cosmology provides a thermodynamically consistent framework for gravitational baryogenesis, where irreversible entropy production ensures a monotonic $\dot R$ and avoids freeze-out suppression. The model successfully reproduces the observed baryon asymmetry within theoretically and observationally allowed parameter ranges. It links baryogenesis to dissipative processes in the early universe and suggests testable correlations between $T_D$, $M$, and $ξ$. However, stability issues in the UV require further study through completed theories or stabilized embeddings.

体粘滞性宇宙学为引力重子生成提供了一个热力学自洽的框架，其中不可逆熵产生确保了单调的 $\dot R$，避免了冻结抑制。该模型在理论与观测允许的参数范围内成功复现了观测到的重子不对称性，将重子生成与早期宇宙的耗散过程联系起来，并提出了 $T_D$、$M$ 和 $ξ$ 之间的可检验关联。然而，紫外区的稳定性问题仍需通过完备理论或稳定嵌入进一步研究。

Abstract: We study a concrete realization of gravitational baryogenesis in which a small bulk-viscous deformation of an otherwise radiation-dominated early universe generates a sign-definite curvature source. The key point is thermodynamic irreversibility: positive entropy production makes the driving term monotonic and therefore avoids the freeze-out cancellation that suppresses rapidly oscillating or sign-changing sources. Motivated by a simple first-order transfer-function diagnostic, we analyze the standard curvature-current operator $\mathcal{L}_{\rm int}=(c/M^2)\,\partial_μR\,J^μ_{B-L}$ in a near-radiation background with effective pressure $p_{\rm eff}=p-3ζH$ and $ζ=ξρ/H$. For $ξ>0$ one finds $R\neq 0$, $\dot R>0$, and a baryon asymmetry $η\propto ξT_D^5/(M^2 \bar M_{\rm Pl}^3)$. We derive the viable $(T_D,M,ξ)$ region, include entropy dilution from a finite viscous epoch, and show that the observed $η_{\rm obs}\simeq 8.6\times10^{-11}$ can be reproduced in a parameter region consistent with current cosmological bounds while maintaining EFT control. The highest-scale benchmarks should be read conditionally on a very high reheating scale in view of current tensor limits. A particle-creation sector of heavy GUT-scale fields then provides a phenomenological motivation for the required range $ξ\sim10^{-4}$--$10^{-3}$. We also discuss the known higher-derivative instability of gravitational baryogenesis and the role of stabilized or completed embeddings.

</details>


### [52] [Global Electroweak Fit Constraints on the Two-Higgs-Doublet Model in Light of the CDF W -Boson Mass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03382)
*Hindi Zouhair*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The CDF II collaboration's recent measurement of the $W$ boson mass shows a significant deviation from the Standard Model prediction. This paper studies the implications of this anomaly within the Two-Higgs-Doublet Model (2HDM), using oblique parameters $\Delta S$, $\Delta T$, and $\Delta U$ to assess radiative corrections. The analysis shows that the 2HDM can accommodate the observed $m_W$ shift via enhanced $\Delta T$ contributions from scalar sector mass splittings, leading to updated constraints on the 2HDM parameter space through global electroweak fits.

CDF II合作组最近对$W$玻色子质量的测量显示出与标准模型预测的显著偏差。本文在双希格斯二重态模型（2HDM）框架下研究了这一反常现象的影响，利用观测量参数$\Delta S$、$\Delta T$和$\Delta U$评估辐射修正。分析表明，通过标量部门质量分裂增强$\Delta T$贡献，2HDM可以容纳观测到的$m_W$偏移，并通过全局电弱拟合得到对2HDM参数空间的更新约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The CDF II collaboration reported a high-precision measurement of the $W$ boson mass that is in $7\sigma$ tension with the Standard Model expectation, while also being in mild tension with other experimental results. This discrepancy motivates exploration beyond the SM, particularly in models with extended Higgs sectors like the 2HDM, which can modify electroweak precision observables through loop corrections. The goal is to determine whether the 2HDM can resolve the $m_W$ anomaly and what constraints arise on its scalar spectrum.

CDF II合作组报告了$W$玻色子质量的高精度测量，其与标准模型预期存在$7\sigma$的张力，同时也与其他实验结果有轻微矛盾。这一差异促使人们探索标准模型之外的新物理，特别是在像2HDM这样具有扩展希格斯部门的模型中，这些模型可以通过圈图修正改变电弱精确观测量。本研究旨在确定2HDM是否能解决$m_W$反常以及对其标量谱会产生何种约束。

Method: We employ the oblique parameters $\Delta S$, $\Delta T$, and $\Delta U$ to parameterize new physics contributions from the 2HDM scalar sector to electroweak precision observables. We compute these parameters as functions of the 2HDM scalar masses and couplings, focusing on type-II and flipped scenarios. A global $\chi^2$ fit is performed including the CDF $m_W$ measurement, other electroweak data (e.g., $Z$-pole observables, weak mixing angle), and theoretical constraints (e.g., perturbativity, unitarity, stability). We compare fits with and without the CDF result to assess its impact on the allowed parameter space.

我们采用观测量参数$\Delta S$、$\Delta T$和$\Delta U$来参数化2HDM标量部门对电弱精确观测量的新物理贡献。我们将这些参数计算为2HDM标量质量和耦合的函数，重点关注type-II和flipped情形。通过执行全局$\chi^2$拟合，包含CDF的$m_W$测量结果、其他电弱数据（如$Z$极点观测量、弱混合角）以及理论约束（如微扰性、幺正性和稳定性），我们比较包含与不包含CDF结果的拟合，以评估其对允许参数空间的影响。

Result: The inclusion of the CDF $m_W$ measurement shifts the preferred region in the $\Delta T$–$\Delta S$ plane, favoring positive values of $\Delta T \sim 0.15$. In the 2HDM, this requires a significant mass splitting between the neutral and charged Higgs states, typically with $m_{H^\pm} < m_h$ or $m_A \ll m_H$, depending on the type. Such configurations are compatible with other electroweak constraints only for specific alignment limits and moderate $\tan\beta$. We present updated exclusion bounds on the 2HDM scalar masses and show that the CDF result strengthens constraints on the mass degeneracy within the Higgs multiplets.

引入CDF的$m_W$测量结果改变了$\Delta T$–$\Delta S$平面上的优选区域，倾向于正的$\Delta T \sim 0.15$值。在2HDM中，这要求中性与带电希格斯态之间存在显著的质量分裂，通常表现为$m_{H^\pm} < m_h$或$m_A \ll m_H$，具体取决于模型类型。此类构型仅在特定对齐极限和中等$\tan\beta$下才与其他电弱约束相容。我们给出了对2HDM标量质量的更新排除界限，并表明CDF结果加强了对希格斯多重态内部质量简并性的约束。

Conclusion: The CDF II $W$ mass anomaly can be accommodated in the 2HDM via enhanced $\Delta T$ contributions from non-degenerate scalar spectra. This requires specific mass hierarchies in the Higgs sector that are testable at current and future colliders. Our global fit provides updated constraints on the 2HDM parameter space, highlighting the importance of precision electroweak data in probing extended Higgs sectors. Future measurements from ATLAS, CMS, and HL-LHC will play a crucial role in confirming or ruling out such scenarios.

CDF II的$W$质量反常可以通过2HDM中标量谱非简并带来的增强$\Delta T$贡献得以解释。这需要希格斯部门中的特定质量层级结构，可在当前和未来的对撞机上进行检验。我们的全局拟合提供了对2HDM参数空间的更新约束，突显了精确电弱数据在探测扩展希格斯部门中的重要性。ATLAS、CMS和HL-LHC的未来测量将在确认或排除此类情景中发挥关键作用。

Abstract: The recent measurement of the $W$ boson mass by the CDF II collaboration exhibits a significant tension with the Standard Model (SM) prediction and other experimental determinations. In this work, we investigate the implications of this result within the framework of the Two-Higgs-Doublet Model (2HDM), focusing on radiative corrections to electroweak precision observables parameterized in terms of the oblique parameters $ΔS$, $ΔT$, and $ΔU$. Using global electroweak fits, we analyze how the inclusion of the CDF measurement modifies the preferred parameter space. We show that the observed shift in $m_W$ can be accommodated in the 2HDM through enhanced contributions to $ΔT$, arising from mass splittings in the scalar sector. The resulting constraints on the scalar spectrum are presented and compared with those obtained using previous electroweak data. These results highlight the role of precision observables in probing extended Higgs sectors and provide updated bounds on viable 2HDM parameter space.
