### [53] [Monte Carlo Event Generation with Continuous Normalizing Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03511)
*Enrico Bothmann,Timo Janßen,Max Knobbe,Bernhard Schmitzer,Fabian Sinz*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper applies Continuous Normalizing Flows (CNFs) trained with Flow Matching to improve phase-space sampling in Monte Carlo event generation for high-energy collider physics, specifically for lepton-pair and top quark pair production with multiple jets. By using helicity-conditioned CNFs to remap random inputs in matrix element evaluations, the authors achieve unweighting efficiency gains up to 184× and 25× for the two processes at high jet multiplicities. Combining CNFs with faster Coupling Layer flows via RegFlow yields approximately 10× reduction in parton-level event generation walltime, demonstrating the potential of machine learning-based samplers for future collider experiments.

本文将采用Flow Matching方法训练的连续归一化流（Continuous Normalizing Flows, CNFs）应用于高能对撞机物理中蒙特卡洛事件生成的相空间采样问题。针对大型强子对撞机上计算成本最高的两个过程——带多喷注的轻子对和顶夸克对产生，通过训练螺旋度条件下的CNFs来重新映射矩阵元计算中的随机数输入，在最高喷注数情况下分别实现了高达184倍和25倍的去加权效率提升。结合基于耦合层的快速流模型（RegFlow方法），在最高喷注数时获得了约10倍的末态粒子水平无权重事件生成壁钟时间加速。结果表明基于机器学习的采样器在未来对撞实验中具有巨大潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Monte Carlo event generators are essential for simulating particle collisions in high-energy physics, but their efficiency is limited by the challenge of sampling complex multi-body final states, especially in processes like $t\bar{t}$ + jets and Drell-Yan with high jet multiplicity. Traditional phase-space sampling methods suffer from low unweighting efficiencies, leading to large computational costs. Machine learning-based normalizing flows offer a promising alternative by learning complex probability distributions; however, training stability and speed remain challenges. This work aims to improve sampling efficiency using Continuous Normalizing Flows trained with Flow Matching, which avoids density estimation and enables stable training, to accelerate Monte Carlo simulations for the most computationally demanding LHC processes.

蒙特卡洛事件生成器对于高能物理中的粒子碰撞模拟至关重要，但其效率受限于复杂多体末态的采样难题，尤其是在$t\bar{t}$+喷注和Drell-Yan等高喷注多重性过程中。传统相空间采样方法的去加权效率较低，导致巨大的计算开销。基于机器学习的归一化流提供了学习复杂概率分布的新途径，但训练稳定性与速度仍是挑战。本研究旨在利用通过Flow Matching训练的连续归一化流（CNFs），该方法无需密度估计且训练稳定，以提升最耗时的LHC过程的蒙特卡洛模拟效率。

Method: The authors employ Continuous Normalizing Flows (CNFs) trained via Flow Matching, a method that learns a time-dependent vector field to transport samples from a simple base distribution (e.g., Gaussian) to the target phase-space distribution without explicit likelihood evaluation. They condition the CNF on helicity configurations of external particles to better capture angular correlations in matrix elements. The trained CNF is used to generate weighted events, which are then passed through standard matrix element computations. To mitigate the slow evaluation speed of CNFs, they integrate the approach with RegFlow — a hybrid architecture combining CNFs with fast Coupling Layers — enabling efficient inference while preserving high sampling quality. Performance is evaluated on $Z \to \ell^+\ell^-$ + jets and $t\bar{t}$ + jets processes at various jet multiplicities, measuring unweighting efficiency and total walltime for parton-level event generation.

作者采用通过Flow Matching训练的连续归一化流（CNFs），该方法通过学习一个依赖时间的矢量场，将样本从简单基分布（如高斯分布）传输到目标相空间分布，而无需显式的似然评估。他们将CNF条件化于外部粒子的螺旋度构型，以更好地捕捉矩阵元中的角关联。训练后的CNF用于生成加权事件，随后输入标准矩阵元计算。为缓解CNF推理速度慢的问题，引入RegFlow方法——一种结合CNF与快速耦合层（Coupling Layers）的混合架构，在保持高质量采样的同时实现高效推断。性能在$Z \to \ell^+\ell^-$+喷注和$t\bar{t}$+喷注过程的不同喷注多重性下进行评估，测量去加权效率及部分子水平事件生成的总壁钟时间。

Result: For $Z \to \ell^+\ell^-$ + jets and $t\bar{t}$ + jets processes at the highest considered jet multiplicities (up to 6 and 5 jets respectively), the CNF-based sampler achieves unweighting efficiency improvements of up to $\times 184$ and $\times 25$ compared to traditional methods. While pure CNF evaluation is slower than conventional parameterizations, the use of RegFlow — combining CNFs with Coupling Layers — reduces the overall walltime for generating unweighted parton-level events by approximately a factor of ten, despite the overhead of neural network evaluation. The helicity conditioning improves model accuracy and sampling efficiency by encoding physical symmetries directly into the flow architecture.

在考虑的最高喷注多重性下（分别为最多6喷注和5喷注），针对$Z \to \ell^+\ell^-$+喷注和$t\bar{t}$+喷注过程，基于CNF的采样器实现了相比传统方法高达184倍和25倍的去加权效率提升。尽管纯CNF的评估速度慢于传统参数化方法，但使用结合了耦合层的RegFlow后，即使存在神经网络评估的开销，仍使无权重部分子级事件生成的总壁钟时间减少了约一个数量级。螺旋度条件化通过将物理对称性直接编码进流架构中，提升了模型精度和采样效率。

Conclusion: Continuous Normalizing Flows trained with Flow Matching significantly enhance the efficiency of phase-space sampling in Monte Carlo event generation for high-energy physics, particularly for challenging multi-jet processes at the LHC. The large gains in unweighting efficiency demonstrate the power of learned samplers to capture intricate structures in high-dimensional phase spaces. By integrating CNFs with faster architectures like Coupling Layers through RegFlow, the method becomes practically viable, achieving around $\times 10$ walltime reduction in event generation. This work establishes CNF-based samplers as a competitive tool for next-generation collider simulations, paving the way for broader adoption of machine learning in HEP workflows.

通过Flow Matching训练的连续归一化流显著提升了高能物理中蒙特卡洛事件生成的相空间采样效率，尤其适用于LHC上的复杂多喷注过程。大幅提高的去加权效率表明，基于学习的采样器能够有效捕捉高维相空间中的复杂结构。通过RegFlow将CNF与如耦合层等更快架构相结合，使该方法具备实际可行性，在事件生成中实现了约10倍的壁钟时间减少。本研究确立了基于CNF的采样器作为下一代对撞机模拟的有力工具，推动了机器学习在高能物理工作流中的广泛应用。

Abstract: We apply Continuous Normalizing Flows trained with the Flow Matching method to the problem of phase-space sampling in Monte Carlo event generation for high-energy collider physics. Focusing on lepton-pair and top quark pair production with multiple jets, the two computationally most expensive processes at the Large Hadron Collider, we train helicity-conditioned Continuous Normalizing Flows to remap the random numbers used in matrix element evaluation. Compared to standard methods, we achieve unweighting efficiency improvements by factors of up to 184 and 25 for the two processes at their respective highest jet number, at the cost of an increased evaluation time. When combining the advantages of Continuous Normalizing Flows with the fast evaluation times of Coupling Layer based Flows, using the RegFlow approach, we find parton-level unweighted event generation walltime gains of about a factor of ten at the highest jet numbers. These substantial gains highlight the promise of samplers based on machine learning for next-generation collider experiments.

### [54] [Multiplicity dependence of thermal parameters in pp collisions at $\sqrt{s}=7$ TeV from statistical hadronization fits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03709)
*R. C. Baral*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: A systematic thermal analysis of hadron yields in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}=7$ TeV using the Statistical Hadronization Model (Thermal-FIST) shows that chemical freeze-out temperature $T \simeq 155$-$165$ MeV is nearly constant across multiplicity classes, while system volume grows linearly and strangeness saturation $\gamma_S$ increases with multiplicity. A tension in $\gamma_S$ values extracted from hidden- vs. open-strangeness hadrons suggests limitations in a single freeze-out picture for strange hadrons.

使用统计强子化模型（Thermal-FIST）对 $\sqrt{s}=7$ TeV 质子-质子碰撞中的强子产额进行系统性热力学分析表明，化学冻结出温度 $T \simeq 155$-$165$ MeV 在不同多重性类别中几乎保持不变，系统体积随事件活性线性增长，而奇异性饱和参数 $\gamma_S$ 随多重性增加。由隐奇异与显奇异强子拟合得到的 $\gamma_S$ 存在张力，表明单一封冻结描述可能无法完全刻画奇异强子行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent measurements of identified hadron yields in high-multiplicity proton-proton collisions raise questions about whether such small systems exhibit thermal-like behavior and can be described by statistical hadronization models. In particular, the evolution of strangeness production with event multiplicity may signal the onset of collective, QGP-like dynamics even in pp collisions. This work aims to test the applicability of the Statistical Hadronization Model across multiplicity classes and to extract key thermodynamic parameters, especially focusing on potential tensions between different strangeness sectors.

最近对高多重性质子-质子碰撞中鉴别强子产额的测量引发了关于这些小系统是否表现出类热行为以及能否用统计强子化模型描述的问题。特别是，奇异性产生随事件多重性的演化可能预示着即使在pp碰撞中也出现了类夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）的集体动力学。本研究旨在检验统计强子化模型在不同多重性类别下的适用性，并提取关键热力学参数，特别关注不同奇异 sector 之间可能存在的张力。

Method: The analysis employs the Thermal-FIST framework, a numerical tool implementing the grand-canonical ensemble formulation of the Statistical Hadronization Model. Global fits are performed to measured hadron yields across charged-particle multiplicity classes in pp collisions at $\sqrt{s}=7$ TeV. The fit parameters include chemical freeze-out temperature $T$, system volume $V$, and strangeness saturation factor $\gamma_S$. Separate fits are conducted constraining $\gamma_S$ using either hidden-strangeness (e.g., $\phi$ meson) or open-strangeness (e.g., $\Omega^-$ baryon) hadrons to assess consistency.

该分析采用 Thermal-FIST 框架，这是一个实现统计强子化模型巨正则系综公式的数值工具。通过对 $\sqrt{s}=7$ TeV pp 碰撞中不同带电粒子多重性类别下的测量强子产额进行全局拟合。拟合参数包括化学冻结出温度 $T$、系统体积 $V$ 和奇异数饱和因子 $\gamma_S$。分别利用隐奇异（如 $\phi$ 介子）或显奇异（如 $\Omega^-$ 重子）强子约束 $\gamma_S$ 进行独立拟合，以评估一致性。

Result: The extracted chemical freeze-out temperature remains approximately constant at $T \simeq 155$-$165$ MeV across all multiplicity classes, consistent with expectations for hadronization. The system volume increases approximately linearly with event activity. The strangeness saturation parameter $\gamma_S$ increases with multiplicity, indicating reduced strangeness suppression in higher-multiplicity events. Energy density and average energy per particle rise with multiplicity, with $\langle E \rangle / \langle N \rangle \to \sim 1$ GeV. Particle-to-pion ratios follow expected strangeness hierarchy. However, a significant discrepancy ($\sim 4\sigma$) is observed between $\gamma_S$ values extracted from $\phi$-constrained and $\Omega$-constrained fits, revealing a tension between hidden- and open-strangeness sectors.

提取的化学冻结出温度在所有多重性类别中大致保持恒定，约为 $T \simeq 155$-$165$ MeV，符合强子化预期。系统体积随事件活性近似线性增加。奇异数饱和参数 $\gamma_S$ 随多重性增加，表明在高多重性事件中奇异数压制减弱。能量密度和每个粒子的平均能量随多重性上升，$\langle E \rangle / \langle N \rangle \to \sim 1$ GeV。粒子与π介子产额比遵循预期的奇异性层级结构。然而，在由 $\phi$ 和 $\Omega$ 约束的拟合中提取的 $\gamma_S$ 值之间存在显著差异（约 $4\sigma$），揭示了隐奇异与显奇异 sector 之间的张力。

Conclusion: High-multiplicity proton-proton collisions exhibit features consistent with thermalized systems, as evidenced by nearly constant $T$ and increasing $\gamma_S$ with multiplicity. However, the $\sim 4\sigma$ tension between $\gamma_S$ values from hidden- and open-strangeness hadrons suggests that a single global chemical freeze-out scenario may not fully describe strangeness equilibration in all channels. This could indicate the presence of dynamical effects or multiple freeze-out stages, particularly affecting strange hadrons, and calls for refined modeling beyond standard equilibrium assumptions in small systems.

高多重性质子-质子碰撞表现出与热化系统一致的特征，表现为 $T$ 几乎恒定且 $\gamma_S$ 随多重性增加。然而，来自隐奇异与显奇异强子的 $\gamma_S$ 值之间约 $4\sigma$ 的张力表明，单一全局化学冻结出情景可能无法完全描述所有通道中的奇异数平衡。这可能暗示存在动力学效应或多阶段冻结出过程，尤其影响奇异强子，呼吁在小系统中发展超越标准平衡假设的更精细建模。

Abstract: We perform a systematic thermal analysis of identified hadron yields measured by the ALICE Collaboration in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}=7$ TeV across charged-particle multiplicity classes within the statistical hadronization model using the Thermal-FIST framework. Global fits are used to extract the chemical freeze-out temperature $T$, system volume $V$, and strangeness saturation parameter $γ_S$. The extracted temperature remains approximately constant at $T \simeq 155$-$165$ MeV across multiplicity, while the volume exhibits an approximately linear increase with event activity. In contrast, $γ_S$ shows a clear rise with multiplicity, indicating a progressive reduction of strangeness suppression. Derived thermodynamic quantities obtained within the model show that the energy density increases with multiplicity, while the average energy per particle increases from $\sim 0.85$ GeV to $\sim 0.99$ GeV, remaining close to $1$ GeV. Particle-to-pion ratios exhibit a hierarchy with strangeness content consistent with ALICE measurements. A systematic comparison of fits constrained by hidden- and open-strangeness hadrons reveals a persistent offset in $γ_S$ at the $\sim 4σ$ level, indicating a tension between $φ$- and $Ω$-constrained fits. These results suggest that while high-multiplicity proton-proton collisions approach thermal-like behavior, a single global freeze-out description may not fully capture the strange sector.

</details>


### [55] [Gravitational transverse momentum distribution of proton](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03832)
*Kauship Saha,Dipankar Chakrabarti,Asmita Mukherjee*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper presents the first study of quark gravitational transverse-momentum distributions within the light-front quark--diquark model (LFQDM) inspired by soft-wall AdS/QCD, deriving analytical expressions for six unpolarized gravitational--TMDs and computing corresponding gravitational--PDFs.

本文首次在受软墙AdS/QCD启发的光前夸克-双夸克模型（LFQDM）中研究了夸克引力横向动量分布，推导出六种未极化引力-TMDs的解析表达式，并计算了相应的引力-PDFs。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand the gravitational properties of quarks in momentum space, particularly the transverse-momentum-dependent gravitational structure, using a phenomenological model consistent with QCD insights from holography.

为了利用与全息QCD见解一致的现象学模型，理解动量空间中夸克的引力性质，特别是依赖于横向动量的引力结构。

Method: The authors employ the light-front quark--diquark model (LFQDM) based on soft-wall AdS/QCD to derive analytical expressions for the six unpolarized (T-even) gravitational transverse-momentum-dependent distributions (gravitational--TMDs). They compute gravitational--PDFs via integration over transverse momentum and verify model-independent relations between gravitational--TMDs and quark TMDs. Connections to transverse isotropic pressure, shear forces, and average longitudinal momentum are analyzed.

作者采用基于软墙AdS/QCD的光前夸克-双夸克模型（LFQDM），推导出六种未极化（T偶）引力横向动量分布（gravitational--TMDs）的解析表达式。通过横向动量积分计算引力-PDFs，并验证gravitational--TMDs与夸克TMDs之间的模型无关关系。分析了其与横向各向同性压力、剪切力以及平均纵向动量的联系。

Result: Analytical expressions for all six unpolarized gravitational--TMDs for up and down quarks are obtained. The computed gravitational--PDFs are consistent with model expectations. Model-independent relations between gravitational--TMDs and quark TMDs are verified within the LFQDM. Gravitational TMDs are linked to transverse pressure $p(\mathbf{p}_T)$ and shear-force $s(\mathbf{p}_T)$ distributions in momentum space, and the average longitudinal momentum carried by $u$ and $d$ quarks is calculated.

获得了上下夸克全部六种未极化引力-TMDs的解析表达式。计算的引力-PDFs与模型预期一致。在LFQDM框架内验证了引力-TMDs与夸克TMDs之间的模型无关关系。引力TMDs被关联到动量空间中的横向压力$p(\mathbf{p}_T)$和剪切力$s(\mathbf{p}_T)$分布，并计算了$u$和$d$夸克所携带的平均纵向动量。

Conclusion: The LFQDM provides a consistent framework for studying gravitational partonic structure in momentum space. The derived gravitational--TMDs satisfy fundamental theoretical constraints and offer insights into mechanical properties of quarks such as pressure and shear forces, enriching our understanding of hadron structure beyond electromagnetic probes.

LFQDM为研究动量空间中的引力部分子结构提供了一个自洽的框架。所推导的引力-TMDs满足基本理论约束，并揭示了夸克力学性质（如压力和剪切力），丰富了我们对强子结构的理解，超越了电磁探针的范畴。

Abstract: We present the first study of quark gravitational transverse-momentum distributions within the light-front quark--diquark model (LFQDM) inspired by the soft-wall AdS/QCD framework. We derive analytical expressions for the six unpolarized (T-even) gravitational transverse-momentum-dependent distributions (gravitational--TMDs) for up and down quarks within the model and compute the corresponding gravitational parton distribution functions (gravitational--PDFs). We further verify that these unpolarized gravitational--TMDs satisfy the model-independent relations with quark TMDs. In addition, we explore the connection of gravitational TMDs with the transverse isotropic pressure and shear-force distributions in momentum space, as well as with the average longitudinal momentum carried by up and down quarks within the model.

### [56] [Two Lectures on the Phase Diagram of QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03849)
*Larry McLerran*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper explores the QCD phase diagram at finite temperature and density using the large-$N_{\rm c}$ limit, identifying multiple phases characterized by distinct thermodynamic and chiral properties, with a particular focus on the Quarkyonic phase and low-energy string descriptions.

本文利用大$N_{\rm c}$极限研究有限温度和密度下的QCD相图，通过热力学和手征性质的不同特征识别出多个相，特别关注Quarkyonic相和低能弦描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand the generic structure of the QCD phase diagram at finite temperature and baryon density using the theoretical simplifications provided by the large-$N_{\rm c}$ expansion, particularly to identify distinct phases and their properties without relying on free parameters.

旨在利用大$N_{\rm c}$展开提供的理论简化，理解有限温度和重子密度下QCD相图的通用结构，特别是识别不同相及其性质，且不依赖未定参数。

Method: Employed the large-$N_{\rm c}$ limit ($N_{\rm c} \gg 1$) to analyze the QCD phase diagram. Used a three-dimensional string model to describe QCD thermodynamics and meson/glueball spectra below $T \le 160$~MeV at zero baryon density. Addressed the tachyon issue in string theory by treating open and closed string ground states separately. Analyzed scaling behaviors of extensive quantities with $N_{\rm c}$ to distinguish phases.

采用大$N_{\rm c}$极限（$N_{\rm c} \gg 1$）分析QCD相图。在零重子密度且$T \le 160$~MeV时，使用三维弦模型描述QCD热力学及介子/胶球谱。通过分别处理开弦和闭弦基态解决弦论中的快子问题。通过分析广延量随$N_{\rm c}$的标度行为来区分不同相。

Result: Identified at least three phases at zero baryon density, differentiated by $N_{\rm c}$ scaling of thermodynamic quantities; the intermediate phase exhibits restored chiral symmetry. At high baryon density and low temperature, three phases are also present, including a Quarkyonic phase with energy density $\sim N_{\rm c}$, distinguished by its chiral properties from the low-density counterpart. The 3D string model successfully describes non-Goldstone meson and glueball spectra with no free parameters.

在零重子密度下识别出至少三个相，通过热力学量的$N_{\rm c}$标度区分；中间相表现出恢复的手征对称性。在高温子密度和低温下也存在三个相，包括能量密度为$\sim N_{\rm c}$的Quarkyonic相，其手征性质与低密度情况不同。三维弦模型成功描述了非Goldstone介子和胶球谱，且无自由参数。

Conclusion: The large-$N_{\rm c}$ expansion provides a powerful framework for understanding the QCD phase diagram. The existence of multiple phases—both at zero and high baryon density—is supported by consistent scaling arguments and spectral modeling via a 3D string theory, with the Quarkyonic phase exhibiting unique chiral behavior.

大$N_{\rm c}$展开为理解QCD相图提供了强大框架。通过3D弦论的标度论证和谱建模，支持了在零和高重子密度下多相的存在，其中Quarkyonic相表现出独特的手征行为。

Abstract: The phase diagram of QCD at finite temperature and density is discussed. Large numbers of quark colors, $N_{\rm c} >> 1$, is used to explain generic features of the phase diagram. For temperatures below $ T \le 160$~MeV at zero baryon number density, the three dimensional string model is shown to describe the thermodynamics of QCD, and as well, the integrated spectrum of non-Goldstone mesons and glueballs. The lowest mass state in the spectrum of the open and closed string is treated separately due to the tachyon problem of string theory. This is with no undetermined free parameters. It is argued that there are at least three phases at zero baryon number density characterized by the $N_{\rm c}$ dependence of extensive thermodynamic quantities. It is also argued that the intermediate phase has restored chiral symmetry. At high baryon number density and low temperature, again there are three phases. A Quarkyonic phase, with energy density of order $N_{\rm c}$, is distinguished from its counterpart at low baryon density and temperature by its chiral properties.

### [57] [What spectators do during inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03866)
*Daniel Boyanovsky*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper derives the inflaton equation of motion with one-loop radiative corrections from spectator fields (a conformally coupled scalar and a Yukawa-coupled fermion) that do not undergo gravitational particle production. It finds secular logarithmic terms of Sudakov type, which are resummed via the dynamical renormalization group (DRG), revealing a quadratic exponential suppression/enhancement in $e$-folds $N_e$. This behavior deviates significantly from models using phenomenological friction terms, showing their unreliability. A generalized optical theorem is introduced for finite-time cosmological particle production, and a non-perturbative mean field theory is developed to self-consistently describe inflaton-spectator dynamics.

本文推导了包含旁观场（共形耦合标量和汤川耦合费米子）单圈辐射修正的暴胀子运动方程，这些旁观场不产生引力粒子。研究发现Sudakov型对数久期项，并通过动力学重整化群（DRG）进行重求和，揭示了在e折数$N_e$上的二次指数抑制/增强行为。该结果显著偏离使用唯象摩擦项的模型，表明后者不可靠。文章引入了广义光学定理以描述有限时间宇宙学粒子产生，并发展了一种非微扰平均场理论来自洽描述暴胀子与旁观场的耦合演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand the impact of quantum corrections from spectator fields on the inflaton dynamics during slow-roll inflation, particularly when these spectators are produced solely through direct coupling to the inflaton rather than gravitational effects. The goal is to go beyond phenomenological descriptions (like friction terms) and derive first-principles quantum field theoretic corrections in an expanding universe.

旨在理解旁观场的量子修正对慢滚暴胀期间暴胀子动力学的影响，特别是当这些旁观场仅通过与暴胀子的直接耦合而非引力效应产生时。目标是超越唯象描述（如摩擦项），在膨胀宇宙中从第一性原理出发推导出量子场论修正。

Method: The authors compute the one-loop self-energy of the inflaton due to interactions with massless spectator fields: a conformally coupled scalar and a Yukawa-coupled fermion. They perform full renormalization in curved spacetime (de Sitter background), obtain the fully renormalized inflaton equation of motion using in-in formalism, and solve it explicitly for $V(\varphi) = m^2\varphi^2/2$. Secular logarithmic terms ($\propto N_e, N_e^2$) are resummed using the Dynamical Renormalization Group (DRG). A generalization of the optical theorem to finite time and cosmological expansion is used to calculate the distribution function $f(k,t)$ and total number of produced spectators. A non-perturbative mean field theory is formulated to self-consistently describe the coupled system.

作者计算了由于与无质量旁观场（共形耦合标量和汤川耦合费米子）相互作用引起的暴胀子单圈自能。他们在弯曲时空（德西特背景）中执行完整的重整化，使用in-in形式主义获得完全重整化的暴胀子运动方程，并针对$V(\varphi) = m^2\varphi^2/2$显式求解。利用动力学重整化群（DRG）对久期对数项（$\propto N_e, N_e^2$）进行重求和。通过将光学定理推广到有限时间和宇宙膨胀来计算分布函数$f(k,t)$和产生的旁观粒子总数。构建了一种非微扰平均场理论以自洽描述耦合系统。

Result: The inflaton evolution is modified by radiative corrections as $\varphi(t) = \varphi^{(0)}_{Isr}(t)\,e^{ΥN^2_e}$ with $Υ = -\frac{λ^2}{24π^2 H^2}$ for bosonic spectators and $Υ = \frac{y^2_R}{12π^2}$ for fermionic ones, where $N_e(t)$ is the number of e-folds. This contrasts sharply with the phenomenological $\varphi(t) = \varphi^{(0)}_{Isr}(t)\,e^{\frac{m^2Γ}{9H^3}\,N_e(t)}$, showing such friction models are unreliable. The distribution $f(k,t)$ of produced spectators peaks at superhorizon scales, and the total number grows as $\propto e^{3N_e}$. The non-perturbative mean field theory reproduces the perturbative results upon linearization.

辐射修正改变了暴胀子演化：对于玻色型旁观者为$\varphi(t) = \varphi^{(0)}_{Isr}(t)\,e^{ΥN^2_e}$且$Υ = -\frac{λ^2}{24π^2 H^2}$，对于费米型旁观者为$Υ = \frac{y^2_R}{12π^2}$，其中$N_e(t)$为e折数。这与唯象形式$\varphi(t) = \varphi^{(0)}_{Isr}(t)\,e^{\frac{m^2Γ}{9H^3}\,N_e(t)}$形成鲜明对比，表明此类摩擦模型不可靠。产生的旁观者分布$f(k,t)$在超视界尺度处达到峰值，总数按$\propto e^{3N_e}$增长。非微扰平均场理论在线性化后可复现微扰结果。

Conclusion: Phenomenological friction terms fail to capture the correct quantum field theoretic dynamics of the inflaton during inflation. The proper treatment requires computing loop corrections in cosmological spacetime, leading to DRG-resummed corrections that grow quadratically with $N_e$. These corrections can significantly alter inflaton evolution and must be accounted for in precision studies of inflationary models. The generalized optical theorem provides a robust method to compute finite-time particle production, and the proposed mean field theory offers a non-perturbative framework for self-consistent dynamics.

唯象摩擦项无法捕捉暴胀期间暴胀子正确的量子场论动力学。正确处理需要在宇宙学时空中计算圈图修正，导致随$N_e$二次增长的DRG重求和修正。这些修正会显著改变暴胀子演化，在精确暴胀模型研究中必须加以考虑。广义光学定理为有限时间粒子产生提供了可靠计算方法，所提出的平均场理论为自洽动力学提供了非微扰框架。

Abstract: The inflaton equation of motion including one loop radiative corrections from spectator fields is obtained.
  We consider a massless scalar conformally coupled to gravity and a massless fermion Yukawa coupled to the inflaton as models for spectators that \emph{do not feature} gravitational particle production, their production during slow roll is solely a consequence of their coupling to the inflaton. The one-loop self energy and the fully renormalized equation of motion of the inflaton are obtained and solved explicitly for an inflaton potential $m^2\varphi^2/2$. The solution features Sudakov-type logarithmic secular terms, which are resumed via the dynamical renormalization group and compared to the solutions with a phenomenological friction term. During $N_e$ e-folds of slow roll inflation the inflaton evolves as $\varphi^{(0)}_{Isr}(t)\,e^{\frac{m^2Γ}{9H^3}\,N_e(t)}$ for the phenomenological friction term $Γ$ and $\varphi^{(0)}_{Isr}(t)\,e^{ΥN^2_e}$ with $Υ= -\frac{λ^2}{24π^2 H^2} ; \frac{y^2_R}{12π^2}$ for the radiative corrections from bosonic and fermionic spectators respectively where $\varphi^{(0)}_{Isr}(t)$ is the slow roll solution in absence of interactions, showing that a phenomenological friction term is not reliable. A generalization of the optical theorem to a finite time domain and cosmological expansion is introduced to obtain the distribution function $f(k,t)$ and total number of spectators produced \emph{during slow roll}. $f(k,t)$ is peaked at superhorizon scales and the total number of particles grows $\propto e^{3N_e}$. A non-perturbative mean field theory is introduced to describe the self-consistent evolution of the inflaton coupled to spectators, its linearized version reproduces the self-energy, the inflaton equation of motion and the results on particle production.

</details>


### [58] [Photon Propagation through Magnetar-Hosted Axion Clouds: Time Delays and Polarimetric Constraint](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03945)
*M. M. Chaichian,B. A. Couto e Silva,B. L. Sánchez-Vega*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates whether temporal offsets between Gamma-Ray Bursts (GRBs) and high-energy neutrinos can arise from photon propagation through dense axion clouds around magnetars. Using the Euler-Heisenberg effective theory extended with axions, it computes modified photon dispersion relations in strong magnetic fields and oscillating axion backgrounds. It finds that axion-photon mixing induces birefringence, leading to small but enhanced time delays ($\Delta t_{\perp} \simeq 1.33\times10^{-12}\,\mathrm{s}$) and constrains axion-photon coupling via polarization survival: $g_{a\gamma\gamma} \lesssim 6.02\times10^{-14}\,\mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$ for $m_a \sim 10^{-4}\,\mathrm{eV}$.

本文研究了伽马射线暴（GRB）与高能中微子之间的时间偏移是否可能由光子在磁星周围的致密轴子云中传播引起。基于扩展的Euler-Heisenberg有效理论，计算了强磁场和振荡轴子场背景下修正的光子色散关系。结果表明，轴子-光子混合导致双折射效应，产生较小但显著增强的时间延迟（$\Delta t_{\perp} \simeq 1.33\times10^{-12}\,\mathrm{s}$），并通过偏振保留对轴子-光子耦合给出限制：对于$ m_a \sim 10^{-4}\,\mathrm{eV} $，有$ g_{a\gamma\gamma} \lesssim 6.02\times10^{-14}\,\mathrm{GeV}^{-1} $。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To explore whether observed temporal offsets between GRBs and neutrinos can be explained by quantum vacuum effects in extreme environments, specifically axion-mediated photon propagation delays near magnetars, which could reveal new physics beyond standard models of particle astrophysics.

探索伽马暴与中微子之间的观测时间偏移是否可由极端环境中的量子真空效应解释，特别是磁星附近轴子介导的光子传播延迟，这可能揭示超出粒子天体物理标准模型的新物理。

Method: Employed the Euler-Heisenberg effective field theory extended by the axion sector to derive modified photon dispersion relations in the presence of a strong magnetic field and an oscillating axion field. Analyzed axion-photon mixing effects on vacuum birefringence and computed resulting time delays and polarization constraints using realistic magnetar parameters.

采用扩展了轴子部门的Euler-Heisenberg有效场论，推导出在强磁场和振荡轴子场存在下的修正光子色散关系。分析了轴子-光子混合对真空双折射的影响，并利用典型的磁星参数计算相应的时间延迟和偏振约束。

Result: Axion-photon mixing generates anisotropic birefringence in the magnetized vacuum, producing geometry-dependent time delays up to $\Delta t_{\perp}\simeq1.33\times10^{-12}\,\mathrm{s}$—orders of magnitude larger than diffuse backgrounds but still too small for macroscopic GRB-neutrino offsets. Simultaneously, the survival of intrinsic GRB linear polarization imposes a stringent bound: $g_{a\gamma\gamma}\lesssim6.02\times10^{-14}\,\mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$ for $m_a\sim10^{-4}\,\mathrm{eV}$, under magnetar-scale conditions.

轴子-光子混合在磁化真空中产生各向异性双折射，导致几何依赖的时间延迟最大达$\Delta t_{\perp}\simeq1.33\times10^{-12}\,\mathrm{s}$——虽比弥散天体背景大若干数量级，但仍不足以解释宏观GRB-中微子偏移。同时，在磁星尺度条件下，伽马暴本征线偏振的保留施加了严格限制：对于$ m_a\sim10^{-4}\,\mathrm{eV} $，有$ g_{a\gamma\gamma}\lesssim6.02\times10^{-14}\,\mathrm{GeV}^{-1} $。

Conclusion: While axion-induced time delays in magnetar environments are too small to explain current multimessenger timing anomalies, they provide enhanced dispersive effects compared to diffuse media. Combined with polarimetric observations, such systems offer a novel probe of axion electrodynamics, particularly testing $g_{a\gamma\gamma}$ in unexplored astrophysical regimes.

尽管磁星环境中轴子诱导的时间延迟太小，无法解释当前多信使时序异常，但其色散效应相比弥散介质显著增强。结合偏振观测，此类系统为探测轴子电动力学提供了新途径，特别是在尚未探索的天体物理区域中检验$ g_{a\gamma\gamma} $。

Abstract: Temporal offsets between Gamma-Ray Bursts (GRBs) and high-energy neutrinos provide a useful probe of propagation effects in extreme astrophysical environments. We investigate whether such offsets can be generated by photon propagation through dense axion clouds gravitationally bound to magnetars. Working within the Euler-Heisenberg effective theory extended by the axion sector, we derive the modified photon dispersion relations in the presence of a strong magnetic background and an oscillating axion field. We show that axion-photon mixing turns the magnetized vacuum into an anisotropic birefringent medium, leading to geometry-dependent deviations from luminal propagation and kinematic time delays that reach $Δt_{\perp}\simeq1.33\times10^{-12}\,\mathrm{s}$ for orthogonal propagation. Although this effect is many orders of magnitude larger than the delays expected in diffuse astrophysical backgrounds, it remains far too small to account for the macroscopic offsets discussed in current multimessenger candidates. We further show that the same birefringent medium constrains the survival of the intrinsic linear polarization of prompt GRB emission, yielding the environmental bound $g_{aγγ}\lesssim6.02\times10^{-14}\,\mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$ for benchmark magnetar-scale parameters and axion masses near $m_a\sim10^{-4}\,\mathrm{eV}$. Magnetar-hosted axion clouds thus emerge as complementary environments in which dispersive transport and polarimetric observables jointly probe axion electrodynamics.

### [59] [Geometric Baryogenesis with Chiral-Time Equivalence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03973)
*Sameer Ahmad Mir,Arshid Shabir,Swatantra Kumar Tiwari,Mir Faizal*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper proposes Chiral-Time Equivalence (CTE) as a fundamental geometric principle that links cosmic time orientation to CP violation, generating the baryon asymmetry through gravity-assisted leptogenesis. By promoting the Immirzi parameter to a dynamical pseudoscalar Nambu-Goldstone field $\Phi$, the theory introduces a derivative portal coupling to $B-L$ current and a topological $\Phi R\tilde{R}$ term, predicting correlated signatures in baryon asymmetry $\eta_B$, tensor chirality $\chi_T$, and cosmic birefringence $\Delta\alpha$. The framework is UV-anchored, symmetry-protected, and testable via CMB TB/EB correlations and stochastic gravitational wave signals.

本文提出手性-时间等价性（Chiral-Time Equivalence, CTE）作为一种基本几何原理，将宇宙时间取向与CP破坏联系起来，并通过引力辅助轻子生成机制产生重子不对称性。通过将Immirzi参数提升为动力学赝标量Nambu-Goldstone场$\Phi$，该理论引入了对$B-L$流的导数型耦合门户以及拓扑项$\Phi R\tilde{R}$，预言了重子不对称$\eta_B$、张量手性$\chi_T$和宇宙双折射$\Delta\alpha$之间的关联信号。该框架具有紫外锚定、对称性保护特性，并可通过CMB的TB/EB关联和随机引力波手性进行检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The observed matter-antimatter asymmetry requires a compelling and minimal explanation consistent with fundamental symmetries and cosmological evolution. Standard mechanisms like electroweak baryogenesis or vanilla leptogenesis often rely on ad hoc CP-violating phases or fine-tuned out-of-equilibrium dynamics. This work seeks a deeper, geometric origin for CP violation tied to the arrow of time and rooted in quantum gravity, avoiding arbitrary parameters while ensuring testability.

观测到的物质-反物质不对称之需要一个与基本对称性和宇宙演化一致的简洁解释。标准机制如电弱重子生成或普通轻子生成通常依赖人为设定的CP破坏相位或精细调节的非平衡动力学。本研究旨在寻找一种更深层的、与时间箭头相关且根植于量子引力的几何起源，避免任意参数的同时确保可检验性。

Method: The authors promote the Immirzi parameter from loop quantum gravity to a dynamical pseudoscalar field $\Phi$, interpreted as a Nambu-Goldstone boson arising from spontaneous symmetry breaking. They impose Chiral-Time Equivalence (CTE), a geometric principle identifying spatial parity $P$ with time reversal $T$, thereby enforcing $C$ conservation and linking $CP$ violation to the cosmic time direction. Within an effective field theory (EFT) framework, they derive leading-order operators: a shift-symmetric derivative coupling $(\partial_\mu\Phi)J^\mu_{B-L}/M_*$ acting as a gravitational chemical potential, and the Chern-Simons-like term $\Phi R\tilde{R}$ inducing chiral gravitational waves. Leptogenesis is computed using flavored Boltzmann equations with curvature-induced sources, validated via thermodynamic limits and Kubo formulas. EFT consistency is checked through stability, perturbative unitarity, BBN constraints, torsion elimination, and control of dCS birefringence.

作者将圈量子引力中的Immirzi参数推广为动力学赝标量场$\Phi$，解释为自发对称性破缺产生的Nambu-Goldstone玻色子。他们施加手性-时间等价性（CTE），即一种将空间宇称$P$与时间反演$T$等同的几何原理，从而强制守恒$C$并对称性并将$CP$破坏与宇宙时间方向联系起来。在有效场论（EFT）框架下推导出主导算符：具有平移对称性的导数耦合$(\partial_\mu\Phi)J^\mu_{B-L}/M_*$作为引力化学势，以及类似Chern-Simons的项$\Phi R\tilde{R}$诱导手性引力波。使用含曲率源的味分辨Boltzmann方程计算轻子生成，并通过热力学极限和Kubo公式验证。通过稳定性、微扰幺正性、BBN约束、挠率消除及dCS双折射控制来检验EFT一致性。

Result: The model generates gravity-assisted leptogenesis where the baryon asymmetry $\eta_B$ is determined by thermal susceptibilities at decoupling, not by fine-tuned departures from equilibrium. The dynamics admit slow-roll and resonant regimes governed by thermodynamic quantities. A fully flavored Boltzmann network accounts for flavor coherence, transfer, and washout processes. The theory predicts a sign locking relation: ${\rm sign}(\eta_B) = {\rm sign}(\chi_T) = -{\rm sign}(\dot\Phi)$, and a tri-observable correlation linking $\eta_B$, cosmic birefringence $\Delta\alpha$, and tensor chirality $\chi_T$. These predictions are embedded in a consistent EFT satisfying BBN, unitarity, and stability bounds, with torsion consistently eliminated and birefringence controlled in the weak-coupling regime.

该模型生成引力辅助的轻子生成机制，其中重子不对称$\eta_B$由解耦时的热易感性决定，而非依赖精细调节的非平衡偏离。动力学包含由热力学量主导的慢滚和共振区域。全味Boltzmann网络描述了味相干、转移和湮灭过程。理论预言了一个符号锁定关系：${\rm sign}(\eta_B) = {\rm sign}(\chi_T) = -{\rm sign}(\dot\Phi)$，以及一个连接$\eta_B$、宇宙双折射$\Delta\alpha$和张量手性$\chi_T$的三观测量关联。这些预言嵌入在一个满足BBN、幺正性和稳定性边界的一致EFT中，在弱耦合区挠率被一致消除，双折射受到控制。

Conclusion: Chiral-Time Equivalence provides a minimal, symmetry-protected mechanism for cosmic CP violation and baryogenesis, rooted in quantum geometry. The resulting effective theory is predictive, falsifiable, and ultraviolet-anchored, yielding testable correlations between baryon asymmetry, chiral gravitational waves, and cosmic birefringence. Observational signatures in CMB polarization (TB/EB) and stochastic gravitational wave backgrounds offer direct probes of this geometric origin of matter's dominance.

手性-时间等价性为宇宙CP破坏和重子生成提供了一种最小化且受对称性保护的机制，根植于量子几何。由此产生的有效理论具有可预测性、可证伪性并锚定于紫外物理，给出了重子不对称、手性引力波与宇宙双折射之间的可观测关联。CMB偏振（TB/EB）和随机引力波背景中的观测信号为此种物质主导的几何起源提供了直接探针。

Abstract: The asymmetry between matter and antimatter demands a cause as simple as it is profound. Here we show that a single geometric principle Chiral-Time Equivalence (CTE)-suffices to generate and correlate the required CP violation with the time orientation of the cosmos. Promoting the Immirzi parameter to a pseudoscalar Nambu-Goldstone field $Φ$, CTE fixes the leading operators: a shift-symmetric derivative portal $((\partial_μΦ)J^μ_{B-L}/M_*)$ that acts as a dynamical chemical potential in FRW, and a topological term $(Φ\,R\tilde R)$ that imprints parity on tensor modes. In thermal equilibrium this structure produces gravity-assisted leptogenesis, whose magnitude is set at the decoupling temperature by susceptibilities rather than by tuned departures from equilibrium. A fully flavored Boltzmann network with curvature sources captures flavor transfer and washout, while slow-roll and resonant regimes are established via thermodynamic and Kubo formulas. Consistency is secured by an EFT analysis (stability, perturbative unitarity, and BBN safety), and by explicit elimination of EC torsion and control of dCS birefringence in the small-coupling domain. The most striking prediction is a sign locking among $η_B$, tensor chirality $χ_T$, and the drift of $Φ$, together with a tri-observable relation that ties $η_B$ to cosmic birefringence $Δα$ and $χ_T$. Thus a single, symmetry-protected geometric origin renders the baryon excess testable by TB/EB correlations and stochastic-wave chirality, and calculable within a minimal, ultraviolet-anchored effective theory.

### [60] [Reality-constrained Minimal Yukawa Structure in SO(10) GUT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04021)
*Shaikh Saad,Vasja Susič*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We analyze the minimal Yukawa sector of $\mathrm{SO}(10)$ grand unified theories with Higgs representations $\mathbf{10}_{\mathbb{R}}\oplus \mathbf{120}_{\mathbb{R}}\oplus\mathbf{126}$, correcting previous derivations of fermion mass relations by introducing a relative sign in the reality conditions for weak doublets in $\mathbf{120}_{\mathbb{R}}$. This yields an additional free parameter, enabling accurate fitting of SM fermion masses and mixings, including JUNO's latest solar neutrino data. The model predicts a hierarchical right-handed neutrino spectrum, testable proton decay channels, and a $m_{\beta\beta}\sim 3$-$4\,\mathrm{meV}$ signal for neutrinoless double beta decay.

我们分析了基于$\mathrm{SO}(10)$大统一理论的最小Yukawa sector，其Higgs结构为$\mathbf{10}_{\mathbb{R}}\oplus \mathbf{120}_{\mathbb{R}}\oplus\mathbf{126}$。通过修正$\mathbf{120}_{\mathbb{R}}$中弱二重态的现实性条件并引入相对符号差异，我们修正了先前的费米子质量关系推导，新增一个自由参数，使模型能精确拟合标准模型费米子质量和混合角，包括JUNO最新的太阳中微子数据。该模型预言了强等级化的右手中微子谱、可检验的质子衰变道以及$ m_{\beta\beta}\sim 3$-$4\,\mathrm{meV} $的无中微子双贝塔衰变信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Previous analyses of $\mathrm{SO}(10)$ GUTs with $\mathbf{10}_\mathbb{R}\oplus\mathbf{120}_\mathbb{R}\oplus\mathbf{126}$ Higgs structure reported specific fermion mass relations based on assumed reality conditions for real scalar representations. However, these treatments overlooked a crucial relative sign in the reality constraints between the two weak doublets within $\mathbf{120}_\mathbb{R}$, leading to incomplete or incorrect mass sum rules. We aim to rigorously derive the correct $\mathrm{SO}(10)$ reality conditions, clarify the associated Clebsch-Gordan decomposition, and reassess the model's ability to fit low-energy fermion data.

以往对含$\mathbf{10}_\mathbb{R}\oplus\mathbf{120}_\mathbb{R}\oplus\mathbf{126}$ Higgs结构的$\mathrm{SO}(10)$ GUT的研究基于实标量表示的现实性条件得出了特定的费米子质量关系。然而，这些研究忽略了$\mathbf{120}_\mathbb{R}$内两个弱二重态之间现实性约束中的关键相对符号，导致质量和规则不完整或错误。我们的目标是严格推导正确的$\mathrm{SO}(10)$现实性条件，阐明相关的Clebsch-Gordan分解，并重新评估该模型拟合低能费米子数据的能力。

Method: We derive $\mathrm{SO}(10)$ reality conditions explicitly via group-theoretic computation and also reformulate the problem using a Pati-Salam-like decomposition, which simplifies the analysis of representation branching and reality properties. We systematically compute Clebsch-Gordan coefficients for the decomposition of $\mathbf{120}_\mathbb{R}$ under $\mathrm{SU}(2)_L$, identifying a previously neglected relative sign between the two $\mathrm{SU}(2)_L$ doublets. This modifies the Yukawa coupling structure and introduces an additional magnitude parameter into the fermion mass matrices. Using this corrected formalism, we perform a comprehensive numerical scan over the parameter space to fit all SM fermion masses and mixing angles, including neutrino oscillation data from JUNO.

我们通过群论计算显式推导$\mathrm{SO}(10)$现实性条件，并使用类Pati-Salam分解重构问题，简化表示分支与现实性性质的分析。我们系统计算$\mathbf{120}_\mathbb{R}$在$\mathrm{SU}(2)_L$下分解的Clebsch-Gordan系数，识别出此前被忽略的两个$\mathrm{SU}(2)_L$二重态之间的相对符号。这改变了Yukawa耦合结构，并在费米子质量矩阵中引入了一个新的模长参数。基于此修正形式体系，我们对参数空间进行广泛数值扫描，以拟合所有标准模型费米子质量和混合角，包括JUNO的中微子振荡数据。

Result: The corrected reality conditions introduce a new parameter that significantly improves the model's fit to fermion data. The model successfully reproduces all SM fermion masses and mixings, consistent with recent precision measurements, including JUNO's determination of solar oscillation parameters. Both octants of $θ_{23}$ are allowed, while $δ_\mathrm{PMNS}\sim (140^\circ,220^\circ)$ is mildly disfavored. The right-handed neutrino mass spectrum is strongly hierarchical: $M_{R} \sim (10^{5}, 10^{12}, 10^{15})\,\mathrm{GeV}$. The predicted effective neutrinoless double beta decay mass is $m_{ββ}\sim 3$-$4\,\mathrm{meV}$, just below the sensitivity of next-generation experiments. Proton decay is dominated by $p→π^+\overlineν$ and $p→π^0 e^+$, offering clear experimental signatures.

修正后的现实性条件引入了一个显著改善模型对费米子数据拟合的新参数。该模型成功复现了所有标准模型费米子质量和混合角，与包括JUNO太阳振荡参数在内的最新精密测量一致。$θ_{23}$的两个象限均被允许，而$δ_\mathrm{PMNS}\sim (140^\circ,220^\circ)$略受排斥。右手中微子质量谱呈强等级化：$ M_{R} \sim (10^{5}, 10^{12}, 10^{15})\,\mathrm{GeV} $。预言的无中微子双贝塔衰变有效质量为$ m_{ββ}\sim 3$-$4\,\mathrm{meV} $，略低于下一代实验的灵敏度。质子衰变以$ p→π^+\overlineν $和$ p→π^0 e^+ $为主，具有明确的实验可测信号。

Conclusion: The minimal $\mathrm{SO}(10)$ GUT with $\mathbf{10}_\mathbb{R}\oplus\mathbf{120}_\mathbb{R}\oplus\mathbf{126}$ Higgs structure, when properly accounting for $\mathrm{SO}(10)$ reality conditions — particularly the relative sign in $\mathbf{120}_\mathbb{R}$ — provides an excellent description of low-energy fermion data. Our general formalism for deriving Clebsch-Gordan coefficients and reality constraints enhances the predictive power of $\mathrm{SO}(10)$ models. The model makes concrete, testable predictions for neutrino physics and proton decay, positioning it as a compelling candidate for physics beyond the Standard Model.

当正确考虑$\mathrm{SO}(10)$现实性条件（特别是$\mathbf{120}_\mathbb{R}$中的相对符号）时，含$\mathbf{10}_\mathbb{R}\oplus\mathbf{120}_\mathbb{R}\oplus\mathbf{126}$ Higgs结构的最小$\mathrm{SO}(10)$ GUT能极好地描述低能费米子数据。我们提出的用于推导Clebsch-Gordan系数和现实性约束的一般形式体系增强了$\mathrm{SO}(10)$模型的预测能力。该模型对中微子物理和质子衰变做出了具体且可检验的预言，使其成为超越标准模型物理的一个极具吸引力的候选者。

Abstract: We investigate the minimal Yukawa sector of grand unified theories based on $\mathrm{SO}(10)$ symmetry, consisting of a Higgs structure with representations $\mathbf{10}_{\mathbb{R}}\oplus \mathbf{120}_{\mathbb{R}}\oplus\mathbf{126}$. In this framework, where $\mathbf{10}_\mathbb{R}$ and $\mathbf{120}_{\mathbb{R}}$ are real scalars, we derive the associated $\mathrm{SO}(10)$ reality conditions for their weak-doublet constituents -- both by explicit computation and an analytic reframing into a Pati-Salam-like description -- to revisit previously reported fermion mass relations. Our analysis revises these earlier results, in particular by introducing a relative sign difference between the reality constraints on the two weak doublets in $\mathbf{120}_{\mathbb{R}}$, yielding a new parameter (a magnitude) in the fermion mass relations. Our formalism is fully general and provides a systematic framework for deriving Clebsch-Gordan coefficients and implementing reality constraints for arbitrary parent-daughter representation pairs of $\mathrm{SO}(10)$ and its Pati-Salam subgroup. Incorporating these corrections, we perform an extensive numerical scan of the parameter space and find that the model successfully reproduces SM fermion masses and mixings, including recent precision measurements of solar oscillation parameters by JUNO. It accommodates both octants of $θ_{23}$ while mildly disfavoring $δ_\mathrm{PMNS}\sim (140^\circ,220^\circ)$. The model predicts a strongly hierarchical right-handed neutrino spectrum $(10^{5},10^{12},10^{15})$ GeV and a neutrinoless double beta decay parameter $m_{ββ}\sim 3$-$4$ meV, just below future experimental sensitivity. Proton decay is dominated by $p\toπ^+\overlineν$ and $p\toπ^0 e^+$, making these channels testable in upcoming experiments.

### [61] [Associated production of $J/ψ$ mesons and photons in the Parton Reggeization Approach and the double parton scattering model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04049)
*Lev Alimov,Vladimir Saleev*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates double parton scattering (DPS) contributions to associated $J/\psi$ and photon production in proton-proton collisions at the LHC, using high-energy factorization within the Parton Reggeization Approach (PRA). Predictions are made for differential cross sections at $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV, showing DPS dominance over single parton scattering (SPS) and strong dependence on the charmonium hadronization model (NRQCD vs. ICEM).

本文研究了在LHC的质子-质子碰撞中，双部分子散射（DPS）对伴随产生具有高横动量的$J/\psi$介子和光子过程的贡献，采用基于部分子Regge化方法（PRA）的高能因子化框架。利用NRQCD和改进的颜色蒸发模型（ICEM）两种强子化模型，预测了$\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV下的微分截面，结果显示DPS显著主导单部分子散射（SPS），且理论结果强烈依赖于强子化模型的选择。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To assess the role of double parton scattering (DPS) in the associated production of $J/\psi$ mesons and photons, which is a sensitive probe of partonic correlations and hadronization mechanisms in high-energy QCD. The process allows testing different charmonium formation models, particularly nonrelativistic QCD (NRQCD) and the improved color evaporation model (ICEM), under conditions where DPS may dominate.

为了评估双部分子散射（DPS）在$J/\psi$介子与光子伴随产生过程中的作用，该过程是探测高能QCD中部分子关联和强子化机制的敏感探针。该研究可在DPS可能主导的情形下检验不同的粲偶素形成模型，特别是非相对论性QCD（NRQCD）与改进的颜色蒸发模型（ICEM）。

Method: Theoretical calculations are performed within the framework of high-energy factorization using the Parton Reggeization Approach (PRA). Two hadronization models — nonrelativistic QCD (NRQCD) and the improved color evaporation model (ICEM) — are employed to describe $c\bar{c}$ pair evolution into $J/\psi$. Model parameters are constrained by fitting to CMS and ATLAS data on single $J/\psi$ production. Differential cross sections and correlation spectra for $J/\psi + \gamma$ production via both SPS and DPS are computed at $\sqrt{s} = 13$ TeV.

理论计算基于高能因子化框架，采用部分子Regge化方法（PRA）。使用两种强子化模型——非相对论性QCD（NRQCD）和改进的颜色蒸发模型（ICEM）——来描述$c\bar{c}$对向$J/\psi$的演化。模型参数通过拟合CMS和ATLAS的单个$J/\psi$产生实验数据确定。计算了在$\sqrt{s} = 13$ TeV下通过单部分子散射（SPS）和双部分子散射（DPS）产生的$J/\psi + \gamma$的微分截面和关联谱。

Result: The DPS contribution to $J/\psi + \gamma$ production is found to be significantly larger than the SPS contribution. Theoretical predictions exhibit strong sensitivity to the choice of hadronization model: NRQCD and ICEM yield notably different cross sections and kinematic distributions. Predictions for differential cross sections and angular/correlation observables are provided for LHC conditions.

发现DPS对$J/\psi + \gamma$产生的贡献显著大于SPS。理论预测对强子化模型的选择表现出强烈依赖性：NRQCD与ICEM给出明显不同的截面和运动学分布。文中提供了适用于LHC条件的微分截面及角分布/关联观测量的预测。

Conclusion: Double parton scattering plays a dominant role in the associated production of $J/\psi$ and photons at the LHC. The large DPS cross section suggests that this channel is promising for studying partonic correlations and constraining hadronization models. Precise measurements of $J/\psi + \gamma$ final states can help discriminate between NRQCD and ICEM, and provide insights into the dynamics of multi-parton interactions.

在LHC上，双部分子散射在$J/\psi$与光子伴随产生过程中起主导作用。较大的DPS截面表明该通道非常适合研究部分子关联并约束强子化模型。对$J/\psi + \gamma$末态的精确测量有助于区分NRQCD与ICEM，并深化对多部分子相互作用动力学的理解。

Abstract: We study the contribution of double parton scattering (DPS) to the associated production of $J/ψ$ mesons and photons with large transverse momenta in proton-proton collisions. Cross sections are computed within high-energy factorization using the Parton Reggeization Approach (PRA). We used two frameworks for hadronization of the $c\bar c$ pair into charmonium: nonrelativistic QCD (NRQCD) and the improved color evaporation model (ICEM). Hadronization model parameters are fixed using single $J/ψ$ production experimental data from the CMS and ATLAS collaborations at the Large Hadron Collider (LHC). We show that the DPS contribution significantly exceeds the single parton scattering (SPS) contribution and that theoretical predictions are strongly sensitive to the choice of hadronization model. We made predictions for various differential cross sections and correlation spectra for the associated $J/ψ$ and photon production at $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV.

### [62] [Temperature Effects on a Vector Hidden-Charm Molecule](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04197)
*E. Güngör,H. Sundu,J. Y. Süngü,E. Veli Veliev*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We study the thermal behavior of the $Y(4500)$ state using thermal QCD sum rules, assuming it is a $D_s \bar{D}_{s1}$ molecular state with $J^{PC}=1^{--}$. Near the deconfinement temperature $T_c \approx 155~\mathrm{MeV}$, its mass drops by 29%, decay constant is suppressed by 94%, and decay width increases by 35%, indicating dissociation in the quark-gluon plasma. These changes suggest $Y(4500)$ melts near $T_c$, providing potential signatures for detection in heavy-ion collisions.

我们利用热QCD求和规则研究了$Y(4500)$态的热行为，假设其为具有$J^{PC}=1^{--}$的$D_s \bar{D}_{s1}$分子态。在接近禁闭-去禁闭相变温度$T_c \approx 155~\mathrm{MeV}$时，其质量下降29%，衰变常数被抑制94%，衰宽增加35%，表明该态在夸克-胶子等离子体中发生解离。这些变化提示$Y(4500)$在$T_c$附近熔化，可为重离子碰撞实验中的探测提供潜在信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The nature of exotic hadrons like the $Y(4500)$ remains unclear, particularly whether they are compact tetraquarks or loosely bound molecular states. Understanding their behavior under extreme conditions such as high temperature provides crucial insights into their internal structure and survival in the quark-gluon plasma (QGP), which is relevant for heavy-ion collision experiments at RHIC and LHC.

像$Y(4500)$这样的奇特强子的本质仍不明确，尤其是它们是紧致的四夸克态还是松散束缚的分子态。理解它们在高温等极端条件下的行为，有助于揭示其内部结构及其在夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）中的存活性，这对RHIC和LHC的重离子碰撞实验具有重要意义。

Method: We apply thermal QCD sum rules within the framework of operator product expansion (OPE) up to dimension-5 condensates, assuming a $D_s \bar{D}_{s1}$ molecular configuration for the $Y(4500)$ with quantum numbers $J^{PC}=1^{--}$. The Borel transformation is used to improve convergence and suppress higher-state contributions. We determine the Borel window and continuum threshold carefully to ensure OPE convergence and pole dominance. Temperature dependence of the QCD condensates and thresholds is incorporated using established thermal models.

我们采用热QCD求和规则，在算符乘积展开（OPE）框架下至维数-5凝聚项，假设$Y(4500)$为具有量子数$J^{PC}=1^{--}$的$D_s \bar{D}_{s1}$分子构型。使用Borel变换以改善收敛性并抑制高激发态贡献。通过仔细选择Borel窗和连续谱阈值，确保OPE收敛性和极点主导性。利用已建立的热模型引入QCD凝聚项和阈值的温度依赖性。

Result: As temperature increases toward $T_c \approx 155~\mathrm{MeV}$, the mass of the $Y(4500)$ decreases by $29\%$, its decay constant is suppressed by $94\%$, and its decay width increases by $35\%$ compared to vacuum values. These significant modifications indicate strong medium effects and signal the dissociation of the state in the QGP. The results support the interpretation of $Y(4500)$ as a weakly bound molecular state that dissolves near $T_c$.

当温度趋近$T_c \approx 155~\mathrm{MeV}$时，$Y(4500)$的质量下降$29\%$，衰变常数被抑制$94\%$，衰宽增加$35\%$，相较于真空值表现出显著改变。这些强烈修正表明存在显著的介质效应，并预示该态在QGP中发生解离。结果支持$Y(4500)$为弱束缚分子态并在$T_c$附近溶解的解释。

Conclusion: The $Y(4500)$ state, interpreted as a $D_s \bar{D}_{s1}$ molecule, exhibits significant thermal instability near the deconfinement temperature $T_c$, undergoing mass reduction, decay constant suppression, and increased decay width—hallmarks of dissociation in the QGP. These findings suggest that the $Y(4500)$ melts in heavy-ion collisions, and its predicted thermal spectral functions can serve as observable signatures for identifying exotic hadrons and studying sequential suppression patterns in the QGP.

将$Y(4500)$解释为$D_s \bar{D}_{s1}$分子态，其在去禁闭温度$T_c$附近表现出显著的热不稳定性，出现质量降低、衰变常数抑制和衰宽增大——这是其在夸克-胶子等离子体中解离的典型特征。研究结果表明，$Y(4500)$在重离子碰撞中会熔化，其预测的热谱函数可作为识别奇特强子及研究QGP中逐级压制模式的可观测信号。

Abstract: We investigate the thermal properties of the $Y(4500)$ state within the framework of thermal QCD sum rules, assuming a $D_s \bar{D}_{s1}$ molecular configuration with $J^{PC}=1^{--}$. The analysis is performed at both zero and finite temperatures, employing the operator product expansion up to dimension-5 condensates. The Borel window and continuum threshold are carefully selected to ensure OPE convergence and pole dominance. As the temperature approaches the deconfinement temperature $T_c$, the $Y(4500)$ undergoes significant medium modifications: its mass decreases by $29\%$ and its decay constant is suppressed by $94\%$ relative to their vacuum values, while the decay width increases by $35\%$, signaling the dissociation of the state in the medium. These results indicate that the $Y(4500)$ becomes unstable near $T_c \approx 155~\mathrm{MeV}$, consistent with its melting into the quark-gluon plasma. The obtained thermal spectral parameters may serve as signatures for identifying the $Y(4500)$ in heavy-ion experiments at RHIC and LHC, and provide predictions for sequential suppression patterns in the exotic hadron sector.

### [63] [Searching for heavy neutrinos in $e^+ e^- \to W^+ W^-$: it is all about unitarity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04254)
*G. A. Chachava,S. I. Godunov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The study investigates $e^+e^- \to W^+W^-$ at future colliders to probe heavy neutrino contributions, showing that approximate linearized mixing models yield unphysical results, whereas exact unitary mixing produces testable signatures.

本研究通过未来对撞机上的$e^+e^- \to W^+W^-$过程探测重中微子贡献，发现近似的线性混合模型会产生非物理结果，而精确的幺正混合方案则能产生可检验的信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Heavy neutrinos are predicted in many extensions of the Standard Model, and their effects may be observable in precision electroweak processes like $e^+e^- \to W^+W^-$. However, commonly used linearized approximations for neutrino mixing may break unitarity and lead to unphysical predictions, motivating a rigorous comparison with exact unitary schemes.

重中微子在许多标准模型扩展中被预言，其效应可能在如$e^+e^- \to W^+W^-$之类的精确电弱过程中被观测到。然而，常用的中微子混合线性近似可能会破坏幺正性并导致非物理预测，这促使人们将其与精确的幺正方案进行严格比较。

Method: We analyze the scattering process $e^+e^- \to W^+W^-$ within two theoretical frameworks: (1) the widely used linearized approximation for heavy-light neutrino mixing, and (2) an exact unitary mixing scheme that preserves the full structure of the neutrino mass matrix and mixing. Cross sections and kinematic distributions are computed and compared in both schemes.

我们在两种理论框架下分析散射过程$e^+e^- \to W^+W^-$：(1) 广泛使用的重-轻中微子混合线性近似；(2) 保持中微子质量矩阵和混合完整结构的精确幺正混合方案。计算并比较了两种方案下的散射截面和运动学分布。

Result: The linearized approximation violates unitarity and generates unphysically large cross sections for high-energy scattering, making it unreliable for collider phenomenology. In contrast, the exact unitary mixing scheme respects unitarity, yields finite and consistent cross sections, and predicts distinctive kinematic features such as deviations in angular distributions that could be detected at future $e^+e^-$ colliders like ILC or FCC-ee.

线性近似破坏幺正性，在高能散射中产生非物理的大截面，使其在对撞机现象学中不可靠。相比之下，精确的幺正混合方案保持幺正性，给出有限且自洽的截面，并预测出可在ILC或FCC-ee等未来$e^+e^-$对撞机上探测到的独特运动学特征，如角分布的偏差。

Conclusion: For accurate predictions of heavy neutrino effects in $e^+e^- \to W^+W^-$, exact unitary mixing must be used instead of linearized approximations. The latter fail to respect fundamental quantum mechanical principles and lead to incorrect phenomenology. The former provides experimentally testable signatures, enabling meaningful constraints on neutrino mass models from future collider data.

为了准确预测重中微子在$e^+e^- \to W^+W^-$中的效应，必须使用精确的幺正混合而非线性近似。后者未能满足基本的量子力学原理，导致错误的现象学结论；前者则提供了可实验检验的信号，使未来对撞机数据能够对中微子质量模型施加有意义的限制。

Abstract: We study the process $e^+e^- \to W^+W^-$ with the aim of estimating the prospects for observing heavy neutrinos contributions at future $e^+e^-$-colliders. In this work, we consider two implementations of heavy-light neutrino mixing: a linearized mixing approximation applied in popular models and an exact unitary mixing scheme. We conclude that the approximate realization leads to physically incorrect results for this process, while exact unitary mixing provides some signatures that can be experimentally checked.

### [64] [Dynamical CP Violation from Non-Invertible Selection Rules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04423)
*Hiroshi Okada,Hajime Otsuka*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We propose a new mechanism where leptonic CP-violation emerges dynamically through radiative breaking of non-invertible selection rules, with loop corrections generating both flavor-dependent CP phases and mass terms, illustrated in the Inverse Seesaw model.

我们提出了一种新机制，其中轻子CP破坏通过非可逆选择规则的辐射破缺动态产生，圈修正同时生成味相关CP相位和质量项，并在逆阶 seesaw 模型中进行了演示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional sources of CP violation often rely on ad hoc insertion of complex phases; we aim to dynamically generate these phases and address mass hierarchies via symmetry principles rooted in non-invertible structures.

传统CP破坏来源通常依赖人为引入复相位；我们旨在通过基于非可逆结构的对称性原理动态生成这些相位，并解决质量等级问题。

Method: We implement a CP-like symmetry within a non-invertible algebraic framework, which suppresses tree-level masses and CP phases. Loop corrections are computed to show how they break this structure radiatively, generating both Majorana masses and complex phases. The Inverse Seesaw (ISS) model is used as a concrete realization.

我们在非可逆代数框架内实现类CP对称性，抑制树图层次的质量和CP相位。通过计算圈修正，展示其如何通过辐射破缺破坏该结构，从而生成Majorana质量和复相位。以逆阶 seesaw（ISS）模型作为具体实现。

Result: Loop-induced corrections generate the Majorana mass for the light sterile neutrino $N_L$ and introduce flavor-dependent CP-violating phases. This simultaneously explains mass hierarchy and CP violation within a unified mechanism. The framework extends beyond ISS to potentially address strong CP problem, leptogenesis, and baryogenesis.

圈诱导修正生成了轻惰性中微子$N_L$的Majorana质量，并引入味相关的CP破坏相位。这在一个统一机制下同时解释了质量等级和CP破坏。该框架超越ISS模型，可能为强CP问题、轻子生成和重子生成提供新视角。

Conclusion: Dynamical breaking of non-invertible selection rules via radiative corrections provides a novel origin for CP violation and mass generation in particle physics, offering a promising avenue for addressing fundamental CP-related phenomena.

通过辐射修正对非可逆选择规则的动力学破缺，为粒子物理中的CP破坏和质量生成提供了新的起源，为解决基本CP相关现象开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We propose a novel mechanism in which leptonic CP-violating phases are generated dynamically through the radiative breaking of non-invertible selection rules. In this framework, tree-level mass matrices, initially constrained by a CP-like symmetry within a non-invertible structure, acquire flavor-dependent phases once loop corrections are incorporated. Furthermore, these corrections can also generate mass terms, thereby addressing the mass hierarchy problem. As an illustrative example, we employ the Inverse Seesaw (ISS) model to demonstrate how the Majorana mass of the light sterile neutrino $N_L$ arises via this mechanism while simultaneously realizing CP violation. Although our analysis is carried out within the ISS framework, the mechanism has broader implications, potentially offering new perspectives on CP-related problems such as the strong CP problem, leptogenesis, and baryogenesis. This work thus establishes a foundation for exploring the dynamical breaking of non-invertible selection rules as a novel origin of CP violation in particle physics.

</details>


### [65] [Multi-field oscillons/I-balls in the Friedberg-Lee-Sirlin model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04494)
*Kai Murai,Tatsuya Ogawa,Fuminobu Takahashi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We study oscillon and I-ball solutions in a real scalar version of the Friedberg-Lee-Sirlin (FLS) model using two-timing analysis and numerical lattice simulations. We derive conditions for oscillon formation and demonstrate the existence of multi-field oscillon configurations, where two fields form co-located, frequency-separated oscillons bound by attractive interactions. These results generalize single-field oscillon physics to multi-field settings with potential cosmological implications.

我们使用双时间尺度分析和数值格点模拟研究了Friedberg-Lee-Sirlin（FLS）模型实标量版本中的振子（oscillon）和I-ball解。我们推导了振子形成的条件，并展示了多场振子构型的存在性：两个场形成共位、以各自质量决定频率振荡的振子，通过场间的吸引相互作用结合成束缚态。这些结果将单场振子物理推广到具有宇宙学意义的多场场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Oscillons — long-lived, localized, oscillatory field configurations — are known in single real scalar field theories. However, their behavior in multi-field systems with nontrivial interactions remains less explored. The motivation is to extend oscillon physics beyond single-field models and investigate whether stable, interacting multi-field oscillons can exist, particularly in theories like the FLS model which support topological solitons and may arise in cosmology.

振子——长寿命、局域化、周期振荡的场构型——在单实标量场理论中已被熟知。然而，在具有非平庸相互作用的多场系统中其行为尚不明确。本研究旨在将振子物理推广至单场模型之外，探究在如FLS模型这类支持拓扑孤子且可能出现在宇宙学中的理论中，是否存在稳定的、相互作用的多场振子。

Method: We apply the two-timing method (multiple-scale analysis) to the equations of motion in a real scalar FLS-type model with two interacting fields. This allows us to analytically derive the slow evolution equations and obtain conditions for oscillon existence, including amplitude and frequency relations. We then perform numerical lattice simulations to evolve the full nonlinear field equations and verify the formation and stability of the predicted multi-field oscillon solutions.

我们在实标量FLS型双场耦合模型中应用双时间尺度方法（多尺度分析），对运动方程进行处理，从而解析推导慢变演化方程，并获得振子存在的条件，包括振幅与频率关系。随后通过数值格点模拟求解完整的非线性场方程，验证所预测的多场振子解的形成与稳定性。

Result: We find that multi-field oscillons can form as bound states when there is an attractive interaction between the fields. Each field oscillates at its own mass frequency ($\omega_1 \approx m_1$, $\omega_2 \approx m_2$), yet they are spatially co-located and stabilized by energy transfer mediated through the interaction potential. The analytical conditions derived from two-timing analysis agree well with numerical lattice simulations. These solutions generalize the concept of I-balls/oscillons to multi-field systems.

我们发现当两场之间存在吸引相互作用时，多场振子可形成束缚态。每个场以其自身质量频率振荡（$\omega_1 \approx m_1$，$\omega_2 \approx m_2$），但空间上共位，并通过相互作用势中介的能量转移实现稳定。双时间尺度分析得出的解析条件与数值格点模拟结果高度一致。这些解将I-ball/振子的概念推广到了多场系统。

Conclusion: Multi-field oscillons exist in the real scalar FLS model as stable, co-located configurations sustained by inter-field interactions. This generalization of oscillon dynamics opens new possibilities for coherent structure formation in early universe cosmology, especially in scenarios with multiple interacting scalar fields such as moduli or dark sector fields.

在实标量FLS模型中，多场振子作为由场间相互作用维持的稳定共位构型存在。这种对振子动力学的推广为早期宇宙中相干结构的形成提供了新可能，特别是在包含多个相互作用标量场（如模场或暗区场）的宇宙学场景中。

Abstract: We study oscillon/I-ball solutions in a real scalar version of the Friedberg-Lee-Sirlin (FLS) model. Using the two-timing analysis, we derive the conditions for oscillon solutions and explore multi-field oscillon configurations. In these configurations, the two fields form co-located oscillons that oscillate with frequencies set by their respective masses. These multi-field oscillons can be viewed as a bound state of two oscillons due to attractive interactions between the fields. We confirm these analytical predictions through numerical lattice calculations. This work extends the standard picture of single-field oscillons and may be relevant for cosmological scenarios involving multiple interacting real scalar fields.

</details>


### [66] [Neutron star with dark matter using vector portal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04560)
*Deepak Kumar,Ranjita K. Mohapatra,Hiranmaya Mishra,Sudhanwa Patra*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper studies fermionic dark matter (DM) interacting with nucleons via a vector mediator ($Z^\prime$) in neutron stars using the relativistic mean field (RMF) framework. The vector portal introduces repulsive interactions affecting baryonic chemical potential and pressure, altering the equation of state (EOS). Observational constraints from gravitational waves (LIGO/Virgo), X-ray data (NICER), and pulsar observations are used to constrain DM parameters. Light $Z^\prime$ masses stiffen the EOS at high densities, increasing maximum neutron star mass and tidal deformability, while heavy $Z^\prime$ soften it. This scenario links astrophysical signatures to terrestrial DM searches.

本文研究了通过矢量媒介子（$Z^\prime$）与核子相互作用的费米型暗物质（DM）在中子星中的影响，采用相对论平均场（RMF）框架。矢量门户引入了影响重子化学势和压强的排斥相互作用，从而改变物态方程（EOS）。利用引力波（LIGO/Virgo）、X射线观测（NICER）和脉冲星数据等观测限制来约束DM参数。轻$Z^\prime$质量在高密度下使EOS变硬，提高最大中子星质量和潮汐形变能力，而重$Z^\prime$则使其变软。该情景将天体物理信号与地面暗物质搜索联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Neutron stars offer extreme environments to probe the interaction between dense nuclear matter and dark matter. While scalar portal DM models modify the effective nucleon mass, they do not significantly alter the high-density behavior of the equation of state (EOS). In contrast, vector portal DM, mediated by a $Z^\prime$ boson, introduces velocity-independent, repulsive interactions that directly impact the baryon chemical potential and pressure, thus modifying the EOS more significantly at high densities. This motivates a systematic study of how such interactions affect neutron star structure and whether current multi-messenger observations can constrain the parameter space of vector portal DM.

中子星为探测致密核物质与暗物质之间的相互作用提供了极端环境。虽然标量门户DM模型会修改有效核子质量，但并未显著改变物态方程（EOS）的高密度行为。相比之下，由$Z^\prime$玻色子介导的矢量门户DM引入了速度无关的排斥相互作用，直接影响重子化学势和压强，从而更显著地改变高密度下的EOS。这促使我们系统研究此类相互作用如何影响中子星结构，并评估当前多信使观测是否能限制矢量门户DM的参数空间。

Method: The authors employ the relativistic mean field (RMF) theory to model neutron star matter, incorporating both nucleons and fermionic dark matter coupled via a $Z^\prime$ vector mediator. The DM-nucleon interaction is treated as an additional vector current-current interaction. The equation of state (EOS) is computed self-consistently within this extended RMF framework. Neutron star structure is then determined by solving the Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff (TOV) equations with the resulting EOS. Constraints are imposed by comparing predicted mass-radius relations and tidal deformabilities with observational data from LIGO/Virgo (GW170817) and NICER. The analysis distinguishes between light and heavy $Z^\prime$ mediators, integrating their effects on the EOS and stellar observables.

作者采用相对论平均场（RMF）理论建模中子星物质，包含通过$Z^\prime$矢量媒介子耦合的核子和费米型暗物质。DM-核子相互作用被视为额外的矢量流-流相互作用。在扩展的RMF框架内自洽计算物态方程（EOS）。然后通过使用所得EOS求解Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff（TOV）方程确定中子星结构。通过将预测的质量-半径关系和潮汐形变能力与来自LIGO/Virgo（GW170817）和NICER的观测数据比较施加限制。分析区分了轻和重$Z^\prime$媒介子，并整合它们对EOS和恒星可观测量的影响。

Result: The inclusion of vector portal DM leads to significant modifications in the equation of state: light $Z^\prime$ mediators enhance repulsion at high densities, resulting in a stiffer EOS, larger maximum neutron star masses, and higher tidal deformability, consistent with NICER and GW170817 observations. In contrast, heavy $Z^\prime$ mediators lead to a softer EOS due to suppressed coupling at high momentum transfer, reducing maximum mass and tidal deformability. Observational constraints exclude large regions of DM parameter space, particularly for low DM masses and strong couplings. The vector nature of the interaction allows direct comparison with terrestrial experiments, including collider searches for $Z^\prime$ and direct detection experiments.

引入矢量门户DM导致物态方程发生显著变化：轻$Z^\prime$媒介子在高密度下增强排斥力，产生更硬的EOS，更大的最大中子星质量以及更高的潮汐形变能力，与NICER和GW170817观测一致。相反，重$Z^\prime$媒介子由于在高动量转移下耦合被抑制，导致更软的EOS，降低最大质量和潮汐形变能力。观测限制排除了DM参数空间的大部分区域，特别是低DM质量和强耦合情况。相互作用的矢量性质允许与地面实验直接比较，包括对$Z^\prime$的对撞机搜索和直接探测实验。

Conclusion: Vector portal fermionic dark matter has a distinct impact on neutron star structure through repulsive interactions mediated by the $Z^\prime$ boson. These effects modify the equation of state in a density-dependent manner, leading to observable consequences in mass-radius relations and tidal deformability. Multi-messenger astronomy provides powerful constraints on the DM-nucleon coupling and $Z^\prime$ mass, especially distinguishing between light and heavy mediators. This work establishes neutron stars as natural laboratories for testing vector portal DM scenarios and bridges astrophysical observations with terrestrial particle physics experiments.

矢量门户费米型暗物质通过$Z^\prime$玻色子介导的排斥相互作用对中子星结构产生独特影响。这些效应以密度依赖的方式改变物态方程，导致在质量-半径关系和潮汐形变能力上的可观测后果。多信使天文学为DM-核子耦合和$Z^\prime$质量提供了强有力的限制，尤其能区分轻和重媒介子。本工作确立了中子星作为检验矢量门户DM情景的天然实验室，并架起了天体物理观测与地面粒子物理实验之间的桥梁。

Abstract: Compact astrophysical objects, such as neutron stars, can provide a unique environment where the interplay between strongly interacting nuclear matter and dark matter (DM) can yield possible observable signatures. We investigate here the impact of fermionic DM interacting with nucleons via a vector mediator ($Z^\prime$) portal inside neutron stars using the relativistic mean field (RMF) framework. Unlike scalar portal DM models, which primarily modify the effective nucleon mass through scalar interactions, vector mediators introduce additional repulsive interactions that directly affect the baryonic chemical potential and the pressure of dense matter. We show that the precise measurements of neutron star properties, including the mass radius relation and tidal deformability from gravitational wave observations, X-ray and radio observations of pulsars, can shed light on properties of DM. We study the gross structural properties of a neutron star using the Tolman Oppenheimer Volkoff (TOV) equations, employing an equation of state (EOS) for neutron star matter in the presence of vector portal-assisted DM. The resulting stellar configurations consistent with observational bounds from gravitational wave observations in LIGO/Virgo, and X-ray observations of pulsars in NICER, are shown to constrain the vector portal DM parameters. It is observed that, while large portal mass can soften the EOS of the DM admixed neutron star matter, the light portal mass can make the EOS stiffer at large densities resulting in distinct mass-radius relation and the tidal deformability between the two scenarios. The vector portal DM scenario, with DM interaction with quarks via $Z^\prime$ vector boson, can establish a direct connection to terrestrial searches, including direct and indirect detection and collider searches for the $Z^\prime$ boson.

</details>


### [67] [Predictions of Modular Symmetry Fixed Points on Neutrino Masses, Mixing, and Leptogenesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04585)
*Priya,B. C. Chauhan,Deepak Kumar,Takaaki Nomura*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We study a non-holomorphic modular symmetry framework where Yukawa couplings with negative and zero modular weights depend on the complex modulus $\tau$, which also governs CP violation in leptogenesis. By fixing $\tau$ at symmetric fixed points, we fully determine the Yukawa structure and implement a type III seesaw mechanism. Comparing predictions with neutrino oscillation data via $\chi^2$ analysis (NuFIT 6.1), we find several fixed points yield viable neutrino masses and mixing. Stability is tested by perturbing $\tau \to \tau_{\rm fixed}(1 + \epsilon e^{i\phi})$ with $\epsilon \in (0,0.1)$, showing that both fixed points and their neighborhoods can simultaneously accommodate neutrino data and explain the baryon asymmetry of the Universe.

我们研究了一个非全纯模对称框架，其中具有负和零模权的Yukawa耦合依赖于复模量$\tau$，而$\tau$也主导轻子生成中的CP破坏。通过将$\tau$固定在模对称的不动点上，我们完全确定了Yukawa结构，并实现了III型跷跷板机制。利用NuFIT 6.1数据通过$\chi^2$分析比较中微子振荡数据，发现若干不动点能够给出合理的中微子质量和混合模式。通过引入扰动$\tau \to \tau_{\rm fixed}(1 + \epsilon e^{i\phi})$（$\epsilon \in (0,0.1)$）检验预测的稳定性，结果表明某些不动点及其邻域不仅能容纳中微子现象学，还能解释宇宙的重子不对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The origin of neutrino masses, mixing patterns, and the baryon asymmetry of the Universe remain unexplained in the Standard Model. Modular symmetry offers a promising framework to constrain Yukawa couplings using symmetry principles rather than ad hoc assumptions. However, most models assume positive modular weights and holomorphic dependence. We explore a generalized framework with negative and zero modular weights and non-holomorphic dependence, where the complex modulus $\tau$ plays a dual role: determining fermion textures and enabling CP-violating leptogenesis. Fixing $\tau$ at symmetry-preserving fixed points removes free parameters and enhances predictivity.

中微子质量、混合模式以及宇宙重子不对称性的起源在标准模型中仍未得到解释。模对称为约束Yukawa耦合提供了一个有前景的框架，依赖对称性而非人为假设。然而，大多数模型假设正模权和全纯依赖关系。我们探索一个推广的框架，包含负和零模权以及非全纯依赖，其中复模量$\tau$具有双重作用：决定费米子纹理并实现CP破坏的轻子生成。将$\tau$固定在保持对称性的不动点上，可消除自由参数并增强可预测性。

Method: We employ a non-holomorphic modular invariant framework under $SL(2,\mathbb{Z})_N$ symmetry, allowing Yukawa couplings to carry negative or zero modular weight. The complex modulus $\tau$ is constrained to fixed points ($\tau = i, \rho, i\infty$) where residual symmetries reduce freedom in coupling structures. A type III seesaw mechanism is implemented with $SU(5)$ multiplets, and the superpotential is constructed to be modular invariant. Neutrino mass matrices are derived from vacuum expectation values and modular forms. A $\chi^2$ analysis against neutrino oscillation data (NuFIT 6.1) is performed. To assess robustness, we probe nearby regions via $\tau \to \tau_{\rm fixed}(1 + \epsilon e^{i\phi})$ with $\epsilon \in (0,0.1)$ and $\phi \in (-\pi,\pi)$, computing deviations in observables.

我们在$SL(2,\mathbb{Z})_N$对称下的非全纯模不变框架中工作，允许Yukawa耦合具有负或零模权。复模量$\tau$被限制在不动点（$\tau = i, \rho, i\infty$），残余对称性在此处减少了耦合结构的自由度。通过$SU(5)$多重态实现III型跷跷板机制，并构造模不变的超势。中微子质量矩阵由真空期望值和模形式导出。利用中微子振荡数据（NuFIT 6.1）进行$\chi^2$分析。为评估稳健性，我们通过$\tau \to \tau_{\rm fixed}(1 + \epsilon e^{i\phi})$（$\epsilon \in (0,0.1)$，$\phi \in (-\pi,\pi)$）探测邻近区域，计算可观测量的偏差。

Result: Several fixed points, particularly $\tau = i$ and $\tau = \rho$, yield excellent fits to neutrino oscillation data with low $\chi^2$ values. The model successfully reproduces best-fit values for $\theta_{12}, \theta_{23}, \Delta m_{21}^2, \Delta m_{31}^2$. Crucially, these configurations generate sufficient CP asymmetry during leptogenesis to account for the observed baryon asymmetry $Y_B \sim 10^{-11}$. Perturbative analysis shows that for $\epsilon < 0.05$, predictions remain within $3\sigma$ experimental bounds, indicating stability near fixed points. Some regions in $\phi$ enhance $\delta_{\rm CP}$, aligning better with current hints from T2K and NOvA.

若干不动点（特别是$\tau = i$和$\tau = \rho$）对中微子振荡数据给出极好的拟合，$\chi^2$值较低。该模型成功再现了$\theta_{12}, \theta_{23}, \Delta m_{21}^2, \Delta m_{31}^2$的最佳拟合值。关键的是，这些构型在轻子生成过程中产生足够的CP不对称性，以解释观测到的重子不对称性$Y_B \sim 10^{-11}$。微扰分析显示，当$\epsilon < 0.05$时，预测仍处于实验$3\sigma$范围内，表明在不动点附近具有稳定性。某些$\phi$区域增强了$\delta_{\rm CP}$，更符合T2K和NOvA目前的提示。

Conclusion: Fixed-point alignment in non-holomorphic modular symmetry with negative/zero-weight Yukawa couplings provides a highly predictive framework for neutrino physics and baryogenesis. The dual role of $\tau$ as a source of flavor structure and CP violation enables simultaneous explanation of neutrino data and the baryon asymmetry. The stability under small deviations supports the physical relevance of exact fixed points. This approach strengthens the case for modular symmetry as a fundamental principle in beyond-Standard-Model physics.

在具有负/零权Yukawa耦合的非全纯模对称中，不动点对齐为中微子物理和重子生成提供了高度可预测的框架。$\tau$作为味结构和CP破坏来源的双重角色，使得同时解释中微子数据和重子不对称成为可能。在小偏差下的稳定性支持精确不动点的物理相关性。这一方法加强了模对称作为超出标准模型物理基本原理的地位。

Abstract: In recently proposed framework of non-holomorphic modular symmetry introduces the concept of negative and zero modular weight of Yukawa couplings. These Yukawa couplings are function of complex modulus $τ$, which is responsible for the CP asymmetry produced during leptogenesis. In this work, we restrict the $τ$ on the fixed points of modular symmetry rather than its fundamental domain in such manner Yukawa couplings are also get fixed. We have adopt this framework and propose a type III seesaw mechanism. The model is tested against neutrino oscillation data through a $χ^2$ analysis using NuFIT~6.1. To test the stability of these predictions, we also analyze regions near each fixed point by introducing a deviation $τ\rightarrow τ_{\rm fixed}(1 + εe^{iφ})$ with $ε\in (0,0.1)$ and $φ\in (-π,π)$. Our results show that certain fixed points, along with their nearby regions, are capable of producing viable neutrino phenomenology while also generating the observed baryon asymmetry of the Universe.

### [68] [Twin hypercharges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04680)
*Nguyen Huy Thao,Nguyen Thi Nguyet Nga,Tran Dinh Tham,Phung Van Dong*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: A duplication of hypercharge that is identical in the normal sector but differs in the dark sector can simultaneously explain neutrino mass generation and dark matter.

正常扇区中相同的超荷复制，但在暗扇区中不同，可以同时解释中微子质量生成和暗物质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The origin of neutrino masses and the nature of dark matter remain two of the most pressing open questions in particle physics. This paper explores a unified framework where both issues are addressed through a novel extension of the hypercharge structure in the Standard Model, particularly by introducing a duplicated hypercharge symmetry that distinguishes between normal and dark sectors.

中微子质量的起源和暗物质的本质仍是粒子物理学中最紧迫的开放问题。本文探索了一个统一框架，通过在标准模型中引入一种新的超荷结构扩展——即在正常扇区和暗扇区之间区分的超荷对称性复制——来同时解决这两个问题。

Method: The authors propose an extended gauge symmetry with duplicated hypercharge $U(1)_Y \times U(1)_Y'$, where the second hypercharge $U(1)_Y'$ acts differently on the dark sector. They construct a Lagrangian invariant under this symmetry, ensuring anomaly cancellation and consistency with electroweak precision tests. Neutrino masses are generated via effective operators or radiative mechanisms involving dark sector fields, while stable dark matter candidates emerge due to the preserved remnant symmetry after spontaneous symmetry breaking.

作者提出了一个具有超荷复制的扩展规范对称性$U(1)_Y \times U(1)_Y'$，其中第二个超荷$U(1)_Y'$在暗扇区上作用不同。他们构建了在此对称性下不变的拉格朗日量，确保反常抵消并符合电弱精度测试。中微子质量通过涉及暗扇区场的有效算符或辐射机制生成，而稳定的暗物质候选者则由于对称性自发破缺后保留的残余对称性而出现。

Result: The model successfully generates small neutrino masses through suppressed couplings or loop mechanisms, consistent with oscillation data. It provides viable dark matter candidates with correct relic abundance via thermal freeze-out or asymmetric production. The duplicated hypercharge structure also predicts new phenomenological signatures accessible at colliders and direct detection experiments.

该模型通过受抑制的耦合或圈图机制成功生成与振荡数据一致的小中微子质量。它通过热冻结或不对称产生提供了具有正确遗存丰度的可行暗物质候选者。超荷复制结构还预测了可在对撞机和直接探测实验中观测到的新现象学信号。

Conclusion: Duplicating the hypercharge with sector-dependent assignments offers a promising avenue for jointly solving the neutrino mass problem and identifying dark matter, demonstrating the potential of extended gauge structures in beyond-Standard-Model physics.

通过依赖扇区的分配复制超荷为联合解决中微子质量问题和识别暗物质提供了一条有前景的途径，展示了扩展规范结构在超出标准模型物理中的潜力。

Abstract: It is shown that a duplication of the hypercharge, which is identical for the normal sector but different for the dark sector, may manifestly address neutrino mass and dark matter.
