### [69] [Natural SUSY with mixed axion/axino dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04687)
*Howard Baer,Vernon Barger,Kairui Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper explores mixed axion-axino dark matter in the context of natural supersymmetry (SUSY), where the axino is the lightest SUSY particle (LSP). It identifies viable parameter regions in the axion decay constant $f_a$ versus axino mass $m_{\tilde{a}}$ plane for both DFSZ and KSVZ axion models, showing that keV-scale axinos can contribute significantly to warm or cold dark matter depending on $f_a$.

本文研究了自然超对称（natural SUSY）框架下轴子-轴微子混合暗物质，其中轴微子（axino）为最轻的超对称粒子（LSP）。文章在DFSZ和KSVZ轴子模型中绘制了轴子衰变常数$f_a$与轴微子质量$m_{\tilde{a}}$参数空间中的可行区域，发现keV量级的轴微子在不同$f_a$下可主导温暗物质或作为冷暗物质的小成分存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Natural SUSY remains viable despite constraints from WIMP searches, but higgsino-like LSPs are increasingly disfavored by direct detection experiments. Meanwhile, SUSY models with the Peccei-Quinn mechanism predict an axion-axino-saxion supermultiplet, offering alternative dark matter candidates. The axino, being highly model-dependent in mass, motivates exploration as a potential LSP and dark matter component, especially in light of mixed axion-axino scenarios.

尽管WIMP搜寻实验对自然超对称仍留有空间，但希格斯微子型LSP因直接探测实验限制而愈发不被支持。同时，包含Peccei-Quinn机制的超对称模型预言了轴子-轴微子-萨克森三重态（axion-axino-saxion supermultiplet），提供了替代的暗物质候选者。轴微子质量高度依赖模型，这激励其作为LSP及暗物质组分的研究，尤其是在轴子-轴微子混合场景下。

Method: The authors calculate the relic abundance of axions and axinos in natural SUSY models with PQ symmetry, considering thermal and non-thermal production mechanisms. They analyze the mixed dark matter scenario by solving Boltzmann equations for axino production and including axion misalignment contributions. Constraints from cosmology and astrophysics are applied, and the viable parameter space in the $f_a$–$m_{\tilde{a}}$ plane is mapped for both DFSZ and KSVZ models.

作者在具有PQ对称性的自然超对称模型中计算轴子与轴微子的遗存丰度，考虑热产生与非热产生机制。通过求解轴微子产生的Boltzmann方程并包含轴子错位机制（misalignment）贡献，分析混合暗物质情形。结合宇宙学与天体物理限制，在DFSZ与KSVZ模型中绘制$f_a$–$m_{\tilde{a}}$参数空间的可行区域。

Result: For axino masses around 100 keV, two viable solutions emerge: one with $f_a \sim 10^{11}$ GeV yielding predominantly warm axino dark matter, and another with $f_a \sim 3\times 10^{12}$ GeV giving mostly cold axion dark matter with a small axino fraction. These results show that mixed axion-axino dark matter remains viable in natural SUSY, particularly when the axino is the LSP.

对于约100 keV的轴微子质量，出现两种可行解：一种是$f_a \sim 10^{11}$ GeV时以温轴微子暗物质为主；另一种是$f_a \sim 3\times 10^{12}$ GeV时以冷轴子暗物质为主，轴微子占极小比例。结果表明，在自然超对称中，当轴微子为LSP时，轴子-轴微子混合暗物质仍可成立。

Conclusion: Axino LSP scenarios in natural SUSY with PQ symmetry offer viable alternatives to conventional WIMP dark matter, especially in light of tightening direct detection bounds. Mixed axion-axino dark matter provides a rich phenomenology, with keV-scale axinos acting as warm dark matter candidates at lower $f_a$, while higher $f_a$ values allow axion-dominated cold dark matter with subdominant axino contributions.

在自然超对称与PQ对称性框架下，轴微子LSP为传统WIMP暗物质提供了可行替代方案，尤其在直接探测界限日益收紧的背景下。轴子-轴微子混合暗物质展现出丰富现象学：低$f_a$时keV量级轴微子可作为温暗物质候选者，高$f_a$时则允许轴子主导的冷暗物质并伴有次要轴微子成分。

Abstract: While supersymmetric models provide a solution to the big hierarchy problem, natural SUSY is also allowed by the little hierarchy problem. In supersymmetric models which include the Peccei-Quinn (PQ) solution to the strong CP problem, one expects the presence of an axion-axino-saxion supermultiplet with a micro-eV-scale axion and a saxion with mass of order the soft breaking scale. The axino mass is much more model-dependent, and may occur in the range of keV-TeV: over 9 orders of magnitude. This leads to the possibility of the axino as lightest SUSY particle (LSP) and the presence of mixed axion plus axino dark matter. The case of natural SUSY with higgsino-like WIMPs as LSP seems (nearly) excluded by multi-ton noble liquid WIMP detector limits, even in the case where the LSP has a depleted abundance compared to axions. We examine the case where the axino is LSP leading to mixed axion-axino dark matter in a natural SUSY context. We map out regions of PQ scale f_a vs. axino mass m_{\ta} parameter space where such a scenario remains viable in both the SUSY DFSZ and KSVZ axion models. For axino mass ~100 keV, we find solutions in accord with the measured dark matter abundance with mainly warm axino dark matter for f_a~ 10^{11} GeV and also solutions with mainly axion cold DM and a tiny axino contribution for higher f_a~ 3\times 10^{12} GeV.

</details>


### [70] [Probing Unification Scenarios with Big Bang Nucleosynthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04870)
*I. M. Dreyer,C. J. A. P. Martins*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We extend the BBN code PRyMordial to constrain Grand Unified Theories through variations in fundamental couplings, particularly the fine-structure constant $\alpha$, using observational data of Helium-4 and Deuterium. Two scenarios for varying gravitational coupling—via particle masses or Newton's constant—are analyzed, yielding tight constraints on $\Delta\alpha/\alpha$ at the BBN epoch. The results show no resolution to the cosmological Lithium problem.

我们扩展了大爆炸核合成代码PRyMordial，通过基本耦合常数（特别是精细结构常数$\alpha$）的变化来约束对大爆炸核合成敏感的一类大统一理论，并利用氦-4和氘的观测丰度数据。分析了两种引力耦合变化的可行情形：通过粒子质量或牛顿引力常数变化实现。结果给出了在大爆炸核合成时期$\Delta\alpha/\alpha$的严格限制，表明这些模型无法解决宇宙学锂问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Grand Unified Theories (GUTs) often predict variations in fundamental constants such as the fine-structure constant $\alpha$ and the gravitational coupling. These variations can leave imprints on Big Bang Nucleosynthesis (BBN) yields, making BBN a powerful probe of early-universe physics. However, a self-consistent and precise treatment of these effects is required to derive robust constraints. Moreover, the persistent cosmological Lithium problem motivates exploration of whether such varying-constant models could resolve this discrepancy.

大统一理论（GUTs）通常预言基本常数（如精细结构常数$\alpha$和引力耦合）会发生变化。这些变化会影响大爆炸核合成（BBN）的产额，使BBN成为探测早期宇宙物理的有力工具。然而，需要自洽且精确的处理方法以获得可靠限制。此外，长期存在的宇宙学锂问题促使人们探索这类变常数模型是否能解决这一差异。

Method: We extended the publicly available BBN code {\tt PRyMordial} to include a self-consistent perturbative framework that accounts for variations in fundamental couplings, particularly $\alpha$. We considered two distinct physical scenarios for the variation of the gravitational sector: (1) variation of particle masses while keeping Newton's constant $G_N$ fixed, and (2) variation of $G_N$ with fixed particle masses. Using current observational data of primordial Helium-4 ($Y_p$) and Deuterium (D/H) abundances, we performed a likelihood analysis to constrain $\Delta\alpha/\alpha$ at the BBN epoch relative to today's value. The analysis includes nuclear reaction rate dependencies on $\alpha$ and other couplings.

我们扩展了公开可用的BBN代码{\tt PRyMordial}，纳入了一个自洽的微扰框架，以考虑基本耦合常数（特别是$\alpha$）的变化。我们考虑了引力部分变化的两种不同物理情景：(1) 粒子质量变化而牛顿常数$G_N$保持不变；(2) $G_N$变化而粒子质量固定。利用当前原初氦-4（$Y_p$）和氘（D/H）丰度的观测数据，我们进行了似然分析，以限制BBN时期相对于今天值的$\Delta\alpha/\alpha$。分析包括核反应率对$\alpha$和其他耦合的依赖性。

Result: For the scenario with varying particle masses, we obtain a 68\% confidence level constraint of $\Delta\alpha/\alpha = 2 \pm 51$ ppm. In the scenario with varying Newton's constant, the constraint tightens to $\Delta\alpha/\alpha = 2 \pm 22$ ppm. These are among the most precise constraints on $\alpha$ variation from BBN. We further find that neither scenario resolves the cosmological Lithium problem, as the predicted Lithium-7 abundance remains inconsistent with observations.

对于粒子质量变化的情景，我们在68\%置信水平下得到$\Delta\alpha/\alpha = 2 \pm 51$ ppm的限制。在牛顿常数变化的情景中，限制更严格，为$\Delta\alpha/\alpha = 2 \pm 22$ ppm。这是目前来自BBN对$\alpha$变化最精确的限制之一。我们还发现，这两种情景均未能解决宇宙学锂问题，因为预测的锂-7丰度仍与观测不一致。

Conclusion: The extended {\tt PRyMordial} code enables precise and self-consistent constraints on fundamental constant variations during the BBN epoch within GUT-motivated models. The tighter constraint in the varying-$G_N$ scenario suggests greater sensitivity of BBN to gravitational sector modifications. However, these models do not alleviate the cosmological Lithium problem, indicating that alternative solutions must be sought.

扩展后的{\tt PRyMordial}代码能够在受大统一理论启发的模型中，对BBN时期的基​​本常数变化施加精确且自洽的限制。在$G_N$变化情景中更严格的限制表明，BBN对引力部分修改更为敏感。然而，这些模型未能缓解宇宙学锂问题，表明必须寻求其他解决方案。

Abstract: We extend a recently developed Big Bang Nucleosynthesis (BBN) code, {\tt PRyMordial}, to constrain a broad class of Grand Unified Theories to which BBN is sensitive, since these lead to varying fundamental couplings. A previously developed self-consistent perturbative analysis of the effects of these variations has been implemented in {\tt PRyMordial}, leading to robust constraints of the value of the fine-structure constant, $α$, at the BBN epoch using current observations of Helium-4 and Deuterium abundances. We explored two different viable scenarios, relying on alternative assumptions on the gravitational sector: the variation of the gravitational coupling can be implemented by varying either particle masses, or Newton's gravitational constant. For the variation of masses, we obtained at $68\%$ confidence level a constraint on the relative variation of $α$, between the BBN epoch and the present-day laboratory value, of $Δα/α=2\pm51$ ppm (parts per million), while for the variation of Newton's constant the analogous constraint is $Δα/α=2\pm22$ ppm. We also show that, given these constraints, these models do not provide a solution to the cosmological Lithium problem.

### [71] [CP-violation effects in neutral meson oscillations in the left-right weak interaction model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04716)
*A. P. Serebrov,O. M. Zherebtsov,A. K. Fomin,R. M. Samoilov,N. S. Budanov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The latest neutron decay data suggest an extension of the Standard Model with a right-handed vector boson $W_R$, characterized by mixing angle $\zeta = -0.039\pm0.014$ and mass-squared ratio $\delta = 0.070\pm0.010$. This extended left-right model successfully describes CP violation in neutral meson oscillations ($K^0$, $D^0$, $B^0$, $B_s^0$), aligning with experimental results and indicating that CP violation arises from the admixture of $W_R$.

最新的中子衰变数据表明需扩展标准模型，引入右手矢量玻色子$W_R$，其混合角为$\zeta = -0.039\pm0.014$，质量平方比为$\delta = 0.070\pm0.010$。该左右对称模型利用参数$\delta$和$\zeta$成功描述了中性介子振荡（$K^0$、$D^0$、$B^0$、$B_s^0$）中的CP破坏现象，理论计算结果与实验一致，表明CP破坏源于$W_R$的混合成分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Precision measurements of neutron decay show anomalies unexplained by the Standard Model, suggesting new physics. The motivation is to explain these deviations and simultaneously account for observed CP violation in neutral meson systems, which the Standard Model only partially describes. Introducing a right-handed weak interaction via $W_R$ offers a unified explanation.

中子衰变的精确测量显示出标准模型无法解释的异常，暗示新物理的存在。本文旨在解释这些偏差，并同时阐明中性介子系统中观测到的CP破坏现象，而标准模型对此仅能部分解释。通过引入右手弱相互作用$W_R$可提供统一解释。

Method: An extended left-right symmetric model is employed, incorporating both $W_L$ and $W_R$ bosons with mixing parameter $\zeta$ and mass ratio squared $\delta = (m_{W_1}/m_{W_2})^2$. Using this framework, the contributions of $W_R$ to box diagrams governing neutral meson oscillations are computed, and the resulting CP-violating observables (e.g., $\epsilon_K$, $a_{\rm SL}$) are derived and compared to experimental data.

采用扩展的左右对称模型，包含$W_L$和$W_R$玻色子，具有混合参数$\zeta$和质量平方比$\delta = (m_{W_1}/m_{W_2})^2$。在此框架下计算$W_R$对主导中性介子振荡的箱型图的贡献，并推导出相应的CP破坏观测量（如$\epsilon_K$、$a_{\rm SL}$），与实验数据进行比较。

Result: The model with $\zeta = -0.039\pm0.014$ and $\delta = 0.070\pm0.010$ reproduces the experimentally observed levels of CP violation in $K^0$, $D^0$, $B^0$, and $B_s^0$ systems. In particular, it accounts for the indirect CP violation in kaon decays ($|\epsilon_K|$) and provides consistent predictions for semileptonic asymmetries in $B$-meson decays, all within current experimental bounds.

该模型在$\zeta = -0.039\pm0.014$和$\delta = 0.070\pm0.010$下重现了$K^0$、$D^0$、$B^0$和$B_s^0$系统中实验观测到的CP破坏水平。特别是，它能解释Kaon衰变中的间接CP破坏（$|\epsilon_K|$），并对B介子衰变中的半轻子不对称性给出符合当前实验限制的一致预测。

Conclusion: The presence of a right-handed vector boson $W_R$ with small mixing $\zeta$ and mass splitting $\delta$ provides a consistent explanation for both neutron decay anomalies and CP violation in neutral meson oscillations. This supports the left-right symmetric extension of the Standard Model as a viable path beyond standard phenomenology, linking low-energy precision tests with fundamental symmetry breaking.

右手矢量玻色子$W_R$的存在，具有小混合角$\zeta$和质量分裂$\delta$，为中子衰变异常及中性介子振荡中的CP破坏提供了自洽解释。这支持了标准模型的左右对称性扩展作为超越标准现象学的可行路径，将低能精密检验与基本对称性破缺联系起来。

Abstract: An analysis of the latest, most accurate experimental data on neutron decay indicates the need to expand the Standard Model by introducing an admixture of the right vector boson $W_R$ with a mixing angle of $ζ= -0.039\pm0.014$ with the left vector boson $W_L$ and a ratio of the squares of the masses of $W_1$ and $W_2$ equal to $δ= 0.070\pm0.010$. In this regard, the possibility of describing CP-violation effects in neutral meson oscillations within the framework of the left-right weak interaction model with parameters $δ$ and $ζ$ was investigated. It was shown that within this model, CP violation effects in the decays of $K^0$-mesons, $D^0$-mesons, $B^0$-mesons, and $B_s^0$-mesons can be successfully described. The results of calculations within the extended left-right model with parameters $δ$ and $ζ$ are confirmed by experimental results. Thus, the nature of CP violation is related to the presence of a right-handed vector boson admixture.

Abstract: This document summarizes the discussions at the program "Precision QCD with the Electron Ion Collider", held from May to June 2025 at the Institute for Nuclear Theory (INT) at the University of Washington. The program was co-sponsored by the INT and by the Center for Frontiers in Nuclear Science (CFNS, Stony Brook University). Abstract: We present a constituent two-gluon description of the lowest-lying glueball states in pure Yang--Mills theory, calibrated against quenched lattice results. The framework incorporates an instanton-induced dynamical gluon mass, Casimir-scaled adjoint confinement, the short-distance adjoint Coulomb interaction, and instanton-induced central and tensor forces. ### [74] [Study of the molecular Properties of the $P_c$ and $P_{cs}$ States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04821)
*Jing-Zhi Cao,Huan-Yu Wei,Jiao-Xue Yang,Jian Sun,Chu-Wen Xiao*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We investigate hidden charm pentaquark states $P_c$ and $P_{cs}$ using a coupled-channel framework based on heavy quark spin symmetry and local hidden gauge formalism, solving the Bethe-Salpeter equation with a momentum cutoff. The full coupled-channel treatment is crucial for $P_c$ states due to width sensitivity, while less critical for $P_{cs}$. Dominant bound channels differ in coupling strength to decay channels between systems. Pole trajectories, wave functions, and root-mean-square radii (0.5–2 fm) support molecular interpretations.

我们利用基于重夸克自旋对称性和局域隐规范形式的耦合道框架，通过动量截断法求解Bethe-Salpeter方程，系统研究了隐粲五夸克态$P_c$和$P_{cs}$的介子-重子分子特性。全耦合道相互作用对$P_c$态至关重要，因其显著影响极点宽度；而对$P_{cs}$态则非必需。主导束缚道在不同系统中与衰变道的耦合强度表现不同。极点轨迹、波函数及均方根半径（0.5–2 fm）支持其分子态解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The discovery of the $P_c$ and $P_{cs}$ states has motivated investigations into their internal structure, particularly whether they can be explained as meson-baryon molecules. Understanding their nature requires a systematic treatment of coupled channels and symmetries such as heavy quark spin symmetry (HQSS), especially given the proximity of these states to relevant thresholds. Clarifying the role of HQSS and channel coupling is essential to determine the dynamical origin of these states.

$P_c$和$P_{cs}$态的发现激发了对其内部结构的研究，尤其是它们是否可被解释为介子-重子分子态。鉴于这些态接近相关阈值，理解其性质需要系统处理耦合道和重夸克自旋对称性（HQSS）等对称性。阐明HQSS和道耦合的作用对于确定这些态的动力学起源至关重要。

Method: We employ a coupled-channel framework combining heavy quark spin symmetry and the local hidden gauge formalism to construct the interaction kernel. The Bethe-Salpeter equation is solved in the on-shell factorization scheme using a momentum cutoff regularization. Pole trajectories are analyzed by varying the binding energy. Wave functions are extracted from the residue of the scattering amplitude at the pole, and root-mean-square radii are computed via two independent methods: integration in coordinate space and the Feynman-Hellmann theorem.

我们采用结合重夸克自旋对称性和局域隐规范形式的耦合道框架构建相互作用核。在壳层因子化方案下使用动量截断正规化求解Bethe-Salpeter方程。通过改变束缚能分析极点轨迹。波函数由散射振幅在极点处的留数提取，均方根半径通过两种独立方法计算：坐标空间积分和Feynman-Hellmann定理。

Result: For the $P_c$ system, full coupled-channel interactions respecting HQSS are essential—the poles' widths are highly sensitive to channel coupling. Dominant bound states arise from $\bar{D} \Sigma_c$ and $\bar{D}^* \Sigma_c$, which strongly couple to lower decay channels. In contrast, for $P_{cs}$, treating PB and VB sectors separately yields similar results, indicating reduced importance of full HQSS. Main bound channels $\bar{D} \Xi_c$ and $\bar{D}^* \Xi_c$ couple strongly to $\bar{D}_s \Lambda_c$ and $\bar{D}_s^* \Lambda_c$, but weakly to lower open-charm decay channels. Pole trajectories of $\bar{D} \Xi'_c$, $\bar{D}^* \Xi'_c$, and $\bar{D}^* \Xi_c^*$ show distinct behaviors. All primary bound channels exhibit similar binding energies in single-channel calculations due to equally attractive potentials. Wave functions are localized within $0\sim6$ fm and decay rapidly beyond $4$ fm. Root-mean-square radii range from $0.5$ to $2$ fm, consistent with typical hadronic molecular scales.

对于$P_c$系统，满足HQSS的全耦合道相互作用至关重要——极点宽度对道耦合极为敏感。主导束缚态来自$\bar{D} \Sigma_c$和$\bar{D}^* \Sigma_c$，且与低能衰变道强耦合。相比之下，对于$P_{cs}$，分别处理PB和VB道得到相似结果，表明全HQSS的重要性降低。主要束缚道$\bar{D} \Xi_c$和$\bar{D}^* \Xi_c$与$\bar{D}_s \Lambda_c$和$\bar{D}_s^* \Lambda_c$强耦合，但与低能开粲衰变道弱耦合。$\bar{D} \Xi'_c$、$\bar{D}^* \Xi'_c$和$\bar{D}^* \Xi_c^*$的极点轨迹表现出明显差异。所有主要束缚道在单道计算中表现出相似的束缚能，源于同等吸引性的势。波函数局域于$0\sim6$ fm内，在超过$4$ fm后迅速消失。均方根半径介于$0.5$至$2$ fm之间，符合典型的强子分子尺度。

Conclusion: The $P_c$ states require a full coupled-channel treatment with heavy quark spin symmetry to accurately describe their widths, supporting a meson-baryon molecular interpretation. In contrast, the $P_{cs}$ states can be reasonably described without enforcing full HQSS, due to weaker couplings to lower decay channels. The calculated root-mean-square radii ($0.5\sim2$ fm) and localized wave functions confirm the spatial extent expected for hadronic molecules. These findings reinforce the molecular picture for both $P_c$ and $P_{cs}$, while highlighting key differences in their dynamical structures arising from strangeness and channel coupling patterns.

$P_c$态需要结合重夸克自旋对称性的全耦合道处理才能准确描述其宽度，支持介子-重子分子态解释。相比之下，由于与低能衰变道耦合较弱，$P_{cs}$态无需严格实施全HQSS即可合理描述。计算得到的均方根半径（$0.5\sim2$ fm）和局域化波函数证实了其空间延展符合强子分子预期。这些结果强化了$P_c$和$P_{cs}$的分子图像，同时突出了因奇异性和道耦合模式不同而导致的动力学结构差异。

Abstract: In the present work, we systematically investigate the meson-baryon molecular properties of the hidden charm pentaquark states $P_c$ and $P_{cs}$ within a coupled channel framework that combines heavy quark spin symmetry and the local hidden gauge formalism. By solving the Bethe-Salpeter equation with the momentum cutoff method, we obtain the pole trajectories, wave functions, and root-mean-square radii. For the hidden charm system, the full coupled channel interactions respecting the heavy quark spin symmetry are essential to generate the $P_c$ states, as they significantly affect the poles' widths. The dominant bound channels are $\bar{D} Σ_c$ and $\bar{D}^* Σ_c$, which couple strongly to lower decay channels. In contrast, for the hidden charm strange system, the full heavy quark spin symmetry treatment is not necessary, where the splitting PB and VB sectors yield similar results. The main bound channels $\bar{D} Ξ_c$ and $\bar{D}^* Ξ_c$ couple strongly to $\bar{D}_s Λ_c$ and $\bar{D}_s^* Λ_c$, respectively, but only weakly to the lower decay channels, differing from the hidden charm case. The trajectories of the pole widths for the loosely bound channels $\bar{D} Ξ'_c$, $\bar{D}^* Ξ'_c$, and $\bar{D}^* Ξ_c^*$ exhibit distinct behaviors. Notably, all the primary bound channels have similar binding energies in the single channel interactions due to equally attractive potentials. Furthermore, we also calculate the wave functions and root-mean-square radii of the corresponding poles. The wave functions are localized within $0\sim 6$ fm and vanish fast beyond $4$ fm. The root-mean-square radii, evaluated by two consistent methods, typically lie between $0.5$ and $2$ fm, comparable to the characteristic scale of molecular states.

</details>


### [75] [Light neutrinos, Dark matter and leptogenesis near electroweak scale and $Z_4$ symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04886)
*Kunal Pandey,Rathin Adhikari*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: A $Z_4$-symmetric Type I seesaw model with three complex Yukawa parameters and one real mass parameter can explain neutrino oscillation data within 3$\sigma$. Adding three small soft-breaking terms allows the lightest right-handed neutrino to be a freeze-in dark matter candidate, while the heavier ones generate baryon asymmetry via resonant leptogenesis.

在具有$Z_4$对称性的I型seesaw模型中，仅需三个复Yukawa参数和一个实质量参数即可在3$\sigma$范围内解释中微子振荡数据。引入三个小的软对称性破缺项后，最轻的右手中微子可通过freeze-in机制成为暗物质候选者，而较重的两个则通过共振轻子数生成（resonant leptogenesis）自然产生宇宙的重子不对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To simultaneously explain neutrino masses, dark matter, and baryon asymmetry within a minimal extension of the Standard Model using discrete $Z_4$ symmetry in the Type I seesaw framework.

旨在通过在I型seesaw框架中引入离散的$Z_4$对称性，在标准模型的最小扩展下同时解释中微子质量、暗物质和重子不对称性。

Method: Imposed $Z_4$ symmetry on the Type I seesaw Lagrangian, reducing Yukawa couplings to three independent complex parameters. Introduced three real soft $Z_4$-breaking terms to enable dark matter production via freeze-in and resonant leptogenesis for baryogenesis.

在I型seesaw拉格朗日量中施加$Z_4$对称性，将Yukawa耦合减少为三个独立的复参数；引入三个实的软$Z_4$破缺项，以实现通过freeze-in机制产生暗物质以及通过共振轻子数生成实现重子生成。

Result: Neutrino oscillation parameters (mass-squared differences, mixings, $CP$ phase) are reproduced within 3$\sigma$. The lightest right-handed neutrino acquires a keV–MeV scale mass via soft breaking and acts as a freeze-in dark matter candidate. Resonant enhancement in decays of heavier right-handed neutrinos enables successful leptogenesis at electroweak scale.

中微子振荡参数（质量平方差、混合角、$CP$相位）在3$\sigma$范围内被复现。最轻的右手中微子通过软破缺获得keV–MeV量级的质量，并作为freeze-in暗物质候选者。较重右手中微子衰变中的共振增强使得在电弱尺度下成功实现轻子数生成。

Conclusion: A minimal $Z_4$-based seesaw model can simultaneously accommodate neutrino data, dark matter, and baryogenesis through soft symmetry breaking, offering a unified framework for physics beyond the Standard Model at the electroweak scale.

一个基于$Z_4$的极小seesaw模型通过软对称性破缺可同时容纳中微子数据、暗物质和重子生成，为电弱尺度下的超越标准模型物理提供了统一框架。

Abstract: Considering $Z_4$ symmetry in Type I seesaw scenario, one could obtain mass-squared differences of light neutrinos, mixings and $CP$ violating phase within $3 σ$ confidence level based on neutrino oscillation data. This is possible with only three independent complex parameters for allowed Yukawa couplings and one real mass parameter for heavy right handed neutrino fields around electroweak scale. After considering only three more real parameters as coming from small soft-symmetry breaking terms, the lightest right handed neutrino could be considered as dark matter candidate via freeze-in mechanism and the other two heavier right handed neutrinos through their decays, could generate the baryonic asymmetry of the universe naturally via resonant leptogenesis.

</details>


### [76] [$\boldsymbol{B_c}$ Meson Spectroscopy from Bayesian MCMC: Probing Confinement and State Mixing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04846)
*Christas Mony A.,Rohit Dhir*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: A Bayesian analysis of the $B_c$ meson spectrum is performed using Cornell and logarithmically modified Cornell potentials, with MCMC sampling enabling rigorous uncertainty propagation; both potentials describe known states well, while the modified version induces systematic shifts in higher excitations, offering improved modeling of intermediate-distance quark-antiquark interactions.

采用贝叶斯方法结合Cornell势和对数修正Cornell势对$B_c$介子谱进行分析，通过MCMC抽样实现严格的不确定性传播；两种势均能很好地描述已知态，而修正势在高激发态中引入系统性偏移，改进了对中间距离夸克-反夸克相互作用的建模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The $B_c$ meson, composed of two different heavy quarks ($b$ and $c$), provides a unique laboratory for testing quantum chromodynamics (QCD) in the non-perturbative regime. Its spectrum, especially higher radial and orbital excitations, is sensitive to the detailed form of the confining potential between heavy quarks. While the standard Cornell potential (Coulomb plus linear) successfully describes many features, deviations may arise at intermediate distances. The motivation is to systematically explore how minimal modifications—specifically a logarithmic deformation—that preserve both short-distance asymptotics and long-distance confinement affect spectral predictions and their uncertainties.

由不同重夸克（$b$和$c$）组成的$B_c$介子为检验非微扰区量子色动力学（QCD）提供了独特平台。其能谱，特别是高径向和轨道激发态，对重夸克间束缚势的形式高度敏感。尽管标准Cornell势（库仑加线性）成功描述了许多特性，但在中间距离可能出现偏差。本研究旨在系统探索最小修正——特别是保持短程渐近行为和长程禁闭的对数形变——如何影响能谱预测及其不确定性。

Method: We employ a non-relativistic potential model with the Cornell potential $V(r) = -\frac{4}{3}\frac{\alpha_s}{r} + \sigma r$ and its logarithmically modified version $V_{\text{mod}}(r) = -\frac{4}{3}\frac{\alpha_s}{r} + \sigma r + \beta \log(r/r_0)$, where the logarithmic term introduces controlled flexibility at intermediate $r$. Parameters are determined via Bayesian inference using Markov chain Monte Carlo (MCMC), allowing full exploration of posterior distributions and proper treatment of parameter correlations and uncertainties. Spin-dependent corrections (spin-spin, spin-orbit, tensor) are included perturbatively. Unequal quark masses ($m_b \neq m_c$) are consistently incorporated in the reduced mass and wavefunction calculations. Radial and orbital Regge trajectories are analyzed using both linear fits and nonlinear parametrizations to assess trajectory curvature.

采用非相对论势模型，使用Cornell势$V(r) = -\frac{4}{3}\frac{\alpha_s}{r} + \sigma r$及其对数修正形式$V_{\text{mod}}(r) = -\frac{4}{3}\frac{\alpha_s}{r} + \sigma r + \beta \log(r/r_0)$，其中对数项在中间$r$处引入可控灵活性。通过基于马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）的贝叶斯推断确定参数，从而全面探索后验分布，并正确处理参数关联与不确定性。自旋相关修正（自旋-自旋、自旋-轨道、张量）以微扰方式包含。不等夸克质量（$m_b \neq m_c$）在约化质量和波函数计算中被一致地引入。使用线性拟合和非线性参数化分析径向和轨道Regge轨迹，以评估轨迹曲率。

Result: Both potentials reproduce the experimentally known $B_c$ states within uncertainties, with low-lying states predicted with high precision and increasing errors for higher excitations. The logarithmic modification leads to small but systematic shifts in the masses of higher radial and orbital excitations, indicating sensitivity to the intermediate-range potential shape. Regge trajectories exhibit clear nonlinearity for low-lying $S$-waves, becoming approximately linear at higher angular momenta—a signature of transition from non-relativistic to more linear confinement dynamics. MCMC enables robust uncertainty quantification, revealing strong parameter degeneracies and correlated errors in predictions.

两种势均能在不确定范围内重现实验上已知的$B_c$态，低激发态预测精度高，高激发态误差增大。对数修正导致高径向和轨道激发态质量出现小但系统的偏移，表明对中间程势形状的敏感性。Regge轨迹在低$S$波中表现出明显非线性，在高角动量下趋于近似线性，标志着从非相对论到更线性禁闭动力学的过渡。MCMC实现了鲁棒的不确定性量化，揭示了强参数简并性和预测中的相关误差。

Conclusion: The logarithmically modified Cornell potential provides a physically motivated extension of the standard model, improving flexibility in describing the intermediate-distance quark interaction without compromising asymptotic behavior. The observed nonlinearity in Regge trajectories supports the need for such refinements in potential models. The Bayesian framework with MCMC sampling allows for reliable uncertainty propagation and model comparison, making it ideal for guiding future spectroscopic searches for unobserved $B_c$ excitations. Predictions for higher $B_c$ states are provided with quantified uncertainties, serving as benchmarks for experiments at LHCb and Belle II.

对数修正Cornell势为标准模型提供了物理动机明确的扩展，在不损害渐近行为的前提下增强了对中间距离夸克相互作用的描述灵活性。观察到的Regge轨迹非线性支持在势模型中进行此类改进的必要性。结合MCMC抽样的贝叶斯框架允许可靠的不确定性传播和模型比较，非常适合指导未来对未观测$B_c$激发态的光谱搜索。本文提供了具有量化不确定性的高$B_c$态预测，可作为LHCb和Belle II实验的基准参考。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive Bayesian study of the $B_c$ meson spectrum using non-relativistic Cornell and logarithmically modified Cornell potentials, introducing the logarithmic term as the minimal deformation that preserves short-range Coulombic and long-range linear confinement while adding controlled flexibility at intermediate distances to probe the sensitivity of higher excited states to the confining form. Model parameters are sampled via Markov chain Monte Carlo (MCMC), enabling rigorous propagation of correlated uncertainties to all predictions. Spin-dependent interactions are treated perturbatively, with unequal heavy-quark masses accounted for consistently. Both potentials reproduce the known states within uncertainties, with small errors for low-lying states that grow for higher radial and orbital excitations. Analyzing radial and orbital Regge trajectories using linear and nonlinear parametrizations, we observe pronounced nonlinearity for low $S$-waves trending toward linearity at higher excitations. The modified potential yields modest, systematic shifts in higher excited states, reflecting the logarithmic correction's impact. We provide updated theoretical predictions for excited $B_c$ states with uncertainties, serving as benchmarks for ongoing and future experiments.

</details>
